Chapter 652: Encounter

Lu Yang had initially planned to sell the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance exam questions. However, since the other party already knew they were from the Dao-Seeking Sect, selling fake questions would be troublesome if they came knocking on their doorstep later.

After the four left, black-robed figures continuously sought out the two to purchase the yang-boosting blood—probably because they felt embarrassed to buy it openly in the side hall.

Meng Jingzhou experienced the joy of earning money for the first time.

Just as Meng Jingzhou thought no one else was coming and they could pack up, another black-robed figure flew over, his steps steady and measured. He placed one hand before his chest and asked politely, “Benefactors, do you still have yang-boosting blood?”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Monk, at least disguise your identity.

If you break the lust precept, and Buddha comes looking for trouble, will the blame fall on you or me?

The polite monk continued, “Also, this poor monk has no spirit stones. May I perform a ritual in lieu of payment? Monks do not speak of falsehood. I am skilled in rituals, be it celebrating births, prolonging lifespans, exorcising evil, or delivering souls.”

Hearing this, Meng Jingzhou contemplated seriously. Celebrating a birth first requires me to have a son, prolonging my lifespan first requires my lifespan to be depleted, exorcising evil first requires evil entities daring to approach me, and delivering souls first requires me to be dead. None seems applicable.

Lu Yang suddenly asked, “May I ask for your dharma name?”

The polite monk answered readily, “This poor monk is Shi Chan.”

“Fellow Daoist Shi Chan?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exclaimed in unison, not expecting to meet a fellow Daoist from the Hanging Monastery here.

Shi Chan was surprised that the two sounded like they knew him. Among the people I know, no one sells yang-boosting blood.

The three simultaneously removed their black robes, revealing their true faces.

Shi Chan had handsome features and wore his kasaya neatly. His expression was aloof, with the corners of his mouth tugged into a faint smile that transcended the mundane world. He was the very image of an accomplished monk.

Although they hadn’t met formally, they had seen portraits of each other.

“You two are Fellow Daoist Lu Yang and Fellow Daoist Meng Jingzhou?” Shi Chan was delighted to see them, his voice rising two pitches and his cold expression melting slightly.

Half a year ago, when he visited the Dao-Seeking Sect, his main goal had been to find these two and learn the Lu-Style Arhat Fist and the Single’s Curse Fist, but he had been unlucky and missed them.

“I didn’t expect to meet you two senior brothers here. It truly is fate.”

Lu Yang was also surprised. During the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, Shi Chan was the only outstanding disciple from the Five Great Immortal Sects who hadn’t attended. Shi Chan had gone to the slaughterhouse, and Master Jiesha was practicing the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation and couldn’t notify Shi Chan during the Golden Core finals.

“If I remember correctly, Senior Brother Shi Chan, shouldn’t you be at the slaughterhouse?”

Shi Chan shook his head gently. “I was originally there. However, three months ago, a barbeque shop called ‘One More Time’ acquired our slaughterhouse. The people from the barbeque shop heard about this poor monk’s identity and fired me.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, That’s probably because they were afraid Shi Chan would discover that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed is behind the barbeque shop.

After all, we diabolic creeds and you immortal sects have irreconcilable stances.

“But it doesn't matter. This poor monk was planning to leave anyway. Coincidentally, I comprehended the meaning of ‘laying down the butcher’s knife and becoming a Buddha on the spot’ at the time. I successfully shattered my golden core to form a nascent soul, advancing to the Nascent Soul Stage.”

The three walked toward the city center as they talked.

Great Xia had no curfew. Even at night, the city was lively and bustling. The three put away their black robes and revealed their usual attire, which didn’t stand out in the crowd.

Lu Yang casually asked, “Then why did you go to the black market? Didn’t you say you have no spirit stones?” Can one even beg for alms in a black market?

Shi Chan smiled. “I just have to report it, and I’ll get some spirit stones.”

The two were speechless.

Shi Chan’s tone was laced with regret. “Originally, this poor monk thought it was a black market of the diabolic path trading souls. Unfortunately, after looking around, I realized it was just a small black market for tax evasion.

“When my shifu could still speak, he told me these small black markets are tacitly approved by the authorities and shouldn’t be reported. Although I couldn’t report the black market, meeting you two senior brothers there was already an extraordinary gain.

“This poor monk is stupid for failing to connect the yang-boosting blood to Senior Brother Meng. The senior brothers of the Dao-Seeking Sect had long told me that Senior Brother Meng is a rare cultivation genius whose Dao heart is as tough as iron, avoiding women to become stronger. Since Senior Brother Meng has cultivated to the Nascent Soul Stage, his blood having yang-boosting effects is reasonable.”

“And what do you need Old Meng’s blood for? Do you have a sweetheart?”

“You jest, Senior Brother Lu. This poor monk has left secular life. How could one in monastic life have a sweetheart? I wish to refine the pure yang blood to temper my mental state and achieve the realm of ‘remaining unflustered even with a beauty in one’s embrace.’”

Shi Chan stopped in his tracks. He extended his right hand and pointed to a busy brothel nearby, smiling faintly. “This is where I temper my mental state. Even with a beauty in one’s embrace, the heart shall remain as calm as in meditation, viewing her as a rouge-powdered skeleton. Only then can one’s mental state achieve major success.

“Senior Brother Lu, I’ve heard that your shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, is a secular cultivator. I presume you’re familiar with secular cultivation methods and can understand my approach.”

Actually, Lu Yang wanted to say his shifu’s secular cultivation often took place in prison cells, not in such expensive places, but saying that would disgrace the sect, so he figured no further explanation was necessary.

Since they were all fellow immortal sect disciples and a few drops of blood weren’t worth much, Meng Jingzhou generously gave Shi Chan twenty drops.

For an ordinary Nascent Soul cultivator, one drop was already effective. For a genius Nascent Soul cultivator like Shi Chan, one or two drops wouldn’t suffice; he needed twenty drops in one go.

Sensing the yang energy in the blood, Shi Chan pressed his palms together and bowed slightly. “Thank you in advance, senior brothers.”

He didn’t stand on ceremony and swallowed all twenty drops. “Indeed, it’s effective.”

Shi Chan’s eyes lit up. Senior Brother Meng’s blood is far more potent than I expected. My body is already reacting, and this is a sensation I’ve never experienced before.

Seeing that he couldn’t suppress the blood’s effect, he walked directly toward the brothel, his expression apathetic and his demeanor unworldly.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t know how long Shi Chan would be in the brothel, so they waited in a nearby tavern.

It was a good chance to tally the night’s earnings.

“150,000 spirit stones, 500,000 spirit stones, 100,000 spirit stones... A total of 2.3 million spirit stones!” Meng Jingzhou beamed with joy. It’s my first time doing business, and I’m already earning this much—looks like I’m very talented in commerce.

However, this business couldn’t be done continuously. The blood sold tonight wasn’t casually dripped from his body but was compressed and refined to achieve a quality akin to essence blood. He needed to rest for a few days before refining the next batch.

“But proving I can earn money is enough. Why must I keep selling blood?”

2.3 million spirit stones—even a Nascent Soul cultivator can’t produce that much at once.

“Here, I’ll give half to you.” Meng Jingzhou gleefully pushed half of the storage rings to Lu Yang. Although this dog Lu Yang’s choice of words in his sales pitch wasn’t pleasant, it had been very helpful and aided in subsequent sales. Sharing the spirit stones is only fair.

Lu Yang didn’t decline, accepting the spirit stones.

The two chatted while drinking free water, ignoring the tavern boss’s angry glare.

“Shouldn’t Shi Chan be coming out by now?”

As they spoke, Shi Chan emerged from the brothel calmly, his expression the same as when he entered—devoid of joy or sorrow.

Lu Yang waved, signaling Shi Chan to come over. “How did tempering your mental state go?”

Shi Chan smiled faintly. “The tempering failed.”

Chapter 653: Accomplished Monk

Although Shi Chan failed in tempering his mental state, as a highly accomplished monk proficient in Buddhist teachings, he was not discouraged. “Senior brothers, you need not worry about this poor monk breaking the precepts. The path of cultivation is fraught with difficulties. How could it be smooth sailing without any waves? Failure is inevitable.

“It is precisely through failure that one understands the preciousness of success. It is precisely by knowing the pleasure of indulging lustful desires that a successfully tempered mental state appears even more firm.”

“...Then what if Master Jiesha finds out you broke the precepts?”

“Only the three of us know about this matter. Monks do not speak of falsehoods, but you are not monks, senior brothers. If my shifu asks, please lie.”

Lu Yang signaled for Shi Chan to sit down and have some water instead of standing. “And what if Master Jiesha asks you?”

Shi Chan’s expression changed slightly as he thought of the consequences if his shifu found out, but then he suddenly relaxed. “Then this poor monk will have no choice but to cultivate the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation as well.”

Lu Yang, “...”

As expected of an accomplished monk, his considerations are thorough.

Meng Jingzhou looked at Shi Chan with a resentful gaze. The ancient Pure Yang Immortal Physique having a girlfriend is one thing, but now even a monk can visit brothels?

So I’m the only unlucky fellow left?

“A Buddha said, ‘One must climb back up from where one fell.’ Since this poor monk failed today, once I earn some money, I shall fight again another day. I plan to stay in this city for a few days. What are your plans, senior brothers?”

Meng Jingzhou made a “time-out” gesture. “Are you sure a Buddha said that?”

Shi Chan chuckled. He rolled up his wide sleeves, dipped his index finger in water, and drew three circles on the table, explaining, “Buddhism emphasizes that the past, present, and future are one. There are Buddhas of the past, present, and future. As a Buddhist disciple, my goal is naturally to achieve Buddhahood. Although I am not a Buddha now, I will definitely be one in the future. Since the past, present, and future are one, aren’t my words the words of a Buddha?”

Meng Jingzhou felt that Shi Chan joining the Hanging Monastery was the Dao-Seeking Sect’s loss.

Lu Yang wasn’t familiar with the matters of Buddhism and consulted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who had single-handedly founded Buddhism. “Immortal Fairy, is there such a saying in Buddhism?”

“I can’t remember. I was only in charge of fabricating stories; theoretical aspects weren’t my responsibility.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was lazily sprawled on her lotus throne, stretching like a little kitten.

At the moment, Lu Yang’s mental space had transformed into a spacious Mahavira Hall,[1] with liuli-glazed tile roofs, interlocking wooden brackets under the eaves, and exquisitely carved doors and windows.

The Mahavira Hall thrived with incense and offerings. It enshrined the true form of Buddhism’s founder, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and her lotus throne.

Since I’m the founder of Buddhism, all current Buddhist monks are considered my grand-disciples. Since we’ve met one of them, I might as well redecorate the Second-in-Command’s mental space for a change of atmosphere.

“Then who was responsible for the theory?” Lu Yang asked.

“Everyone except me.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He turned to Shi Chan. “Senior Brother Shi Chan, could I ask how you plan to earn money?”

Judging by Shi Chan’s idea of earning money by reporting the black market, Lu Yang was highly skeptical of Shi Chan’s moneymaking skills.

“By performing rituals,” Shi Chan replied.

“Oh right, you’re a monk.” Lu Yang suddenly remembered Shi Chan was from the Hanging Monastery.

Shi Chan looked at Lu Yang in bafflement, then glanced down at his own attire. From my appearance to my actions, everything about me should be the image of a monk.

“Then this poor monk will rest for the night and meet you two here tomorrow morning.”

“Wait a moment, do you have any money left? Where are you planning to stay?” Lu Yang stopped the reckless Shi Chan from departing.

If Shi Chan was previously just too poor to buy Old Meng’s body but could go to the brothel, it’s now hard to say whether he has any money left after going to the brothel.

After being forcefully pulled back by Lu Yang, Shi Chan explained, “This poor monk has no money. However, when traveling the world, anywhere can be home. I have already found a bridge archway. It cannot block the wind but can shelter one from rain. There will be no wind or rain tonight, so the place is suitable for lodging.”

Lu Yang was speechless. We’re all fellow immortal sect disciples. The two of us staying in an inn while you live under a bridge—how would that look if word gets out?

“In any case, we two earned quite a bit tonight. Old Meng will treat you to an inn.”

Meng Jingzhou glowered at Lu Yang. You get to be the good guy while I fork out the money?

Lu Yang placated Meng Jingzhou. “I’m letting you do a good deed. Think about it, who is Senior Brother Shi Chan? He’s an accomplished monk from the Hanging Monastery. Meanwhile, you usually commit many misdeeds. Providing lodging for an accomplished monk is a great meritorious deed. It’s only because you shared the spirit stones with me that I’m giving this amazing opportunity to you.”

“Get lost.” Meng Jingzhou wasn’t buying it. However, staying at an inn didn’t cost many spirit stones, so he didn’t mind paying.

He turned to Shi Chan. “I haven’t seen a Buddhist ritual before. It’s a perfect chance for us to stay a few days and watch how you conduct them.”

“Then thank you, senior brothers.” Shi Chan was genuinely happy that the two were willing to stay in the city.

Perhaps I’ll get the opportunity to learn the two fist techniques and also learn from Senior Brother Meng about how to restrain one’s desires.

The blood of an ordinary Single’s Spirit Root wouldn’t have such an effect. Senior Brother Meng must have pushed himself to the extreme to create this yang-boosting blood.

I can’t even withstand twenty drops; I dare not imagine how Senior Brother Meng endured it while having blood coursing through his whole body.

Speaking of inns, Meng Jingzhou had some bad memories. “We stayed at three inns in a row, and all three had incidents. Surely the fourth one won’t have any incidents again, right?”

Lu Yang had always been confident in his luck. “It won’t. Think about the number of battles we’ve encountered involving Fusion cultivators, Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and half-immortals. Didn’t we survive them all without even a scratch?

“This is clearly a sign of our good luck.”

Meng Jingzhou remarked inwardly, Why don’t you first think about why we’ve encountered so many battles involving mighty experts?

The three successfully found an inn catering to cultivators. Such inns had Spirit-Energy Gathering Arrays inside to aid cultivation. If it were just Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, any inn would do. They could simply open their mouths and perform “Swallowing Heaven,” which was more effective than a Spirit-Energy Gathering Array. But with Shi Chan, that wouldn’t work.

“Boss, three Heaven-Grade Rooms.” Having earned money for once, Meng Jingzhou was in high spirits and paid for all three of their rooms.

The boss is a male, so it seems that a case of a younger brother-in-law on the husband’s side vying for the inheritance won’t occur.

Heaven-Grade Rooms were abundant, ensuring cultivators wouldn’t come to blows over them.

The three headed to their respective rooms.

Lu Yang pushed open the door to see the room in a mess. The wardrobe and table were overturned, while the window was wide open and let in a cold draft. On the bed, a man and a woman were wrestling. The man was dressed in black and held a dagger, his eyes filled with killing intent. The disheveled woman struggled desperately and had a streak of blood on her neck matching the blood on the dagger.

The room had a Soundproofing Array, preventing any sound from escaping.

The woman looked at Lu Yang as if she had seen hope.

Lu Yang backed out of the room and checked the room number.

Wrong room.

1. It refers to the main hall of a temple. ☜

Chapter 654: Killer

“Umm, you, if you let her go now and turn yourself in to the authorities, it might still count as voluntary surrender.” Lu Yang said earnestly as he walked back into the room to admonish the murderer.

This is obviously a case of a woman staying next door, an assassin climbing through the window to assassinate her, and me stumbling upon it.

“You shall die too!” The man in black wielded a dagger. Seeing Lu Yang reenter the room, his eyes glinted coldly, but he was immediately pinned to the ground by Lu Yang.

“I guessed you wouldn’t surrender.” Lu Yang suppressed the man with one hand, his tone calm.

The man in black wore an expression of disbelief. He hadn’t even seen Lu Yang’s movements before being subdued. “F-foundation Establishment Stage?!”

To have instantly subdued an almighty Level Nine Qi Training assassin like me, he must be a Foundation Establishment great cultivator!

Now that things have come to this, suicide is the only option!

Lu Yang grabbed the man’s head and pried out two of his front teeth, which concealed lethal poison. Then, he picked up a rag from the floor and stuffed it in the man’s mouth to prevent him from committing suicide by biting his tongue. Finally, he tapped several acupoints on the man’s body, sealing his meridians and rendering him powerless to move.

The assassin was plunged into despair. Who is this uninvited guest? Is he a bodyguard hired by the target? Why is he so familiar with suicide methods?

But this person hasn’t noticed I’d smeared slow-acting poison on the dagger. No one can detect it until it takes effect, and once it does, even an immortal would struggle to save the target. Since I’ve already scratched the target, she doesn’t have long to live.

Besides, even if he does detect it, it’s useless. My poison is exceptionally rare; even I don’t have an antidote.

Lu Yang took out a pill from his identity jade tablet and handed it to the woman, who was still shaken from the incident. “You’ve been poisoned. His dagger was coated with a poison called ‘Cyan Ghost Soul-Entwining Poison,’ which acts up after three days. A cyan ghost will claim your soul, and you will lose your life. It’s not an extremely rare poison; my detoxifying pill can cure it.”

This is just leftover poison from what the Pill Cauldron Peak plays with.

“Ah? Ah, thank you.” The woman woodenly consumed the antidote. It felt cool and soothing, calming her heart considerably.

After her heart had settled down, she looked at Lu Yang gratefully. “Thank you, savior. My name is...”

“Stop! Don’t tell me what your name is, where you’re from, what identity you have, or why an assassin is after you. I’m just the guest next door. I know nothing. I see you have cultivation; I have crippled the assassin’s cultivation, so you can take him to the authorities yourself.” Lu Yang interrupted the woman’s introduction with familiarity.

I have roamed the jianghu for years by relying on my ability to stir up trouble. I can tell at a glance that this is trouble, likely entangled with many more matters behind it.

“Haha, Old Lu, I heard noise from your side and knew you had something going on here too!” Meng Jingzhou’s hearty laughter came from behind Lu Yang.

Meng Jingzhou entered the room, his smile freezing.

The situation in the room was clear. One could tell what happened at a glance.

Why does this grandson get to play the hero saving the damsel in distress again?

“Miss, what matter did you encounter to have someone trying to kill you?”

Just as Lu Yang was about to stop her, the woman introduced herself. “My name is Fuling.[1] I’m from the neighboring Xuan City. My family runs a cloth business, and I came here to expand our family enterprise.

“Since childhood, I’ve shown extraordinary business acumen. My father repeatedly considered handing the entire family business over to me, but my stepmother always obstructed it. She believes her son should inherit the family business, so she constantly makes things difficult for me. Fortunately, I’ve overcome those difficulties one by one.

“This assassin was probably sent by my stepmother. It’s all thanks to your help that I escaped this disaster, Young Master.”

Lu Yang shook his head gently. “This assassin probably wasn’t sent by your stepmother.”

Fuling was surprised, her eyes flickering with confusion. “Why do you say that, Young Master?”

“Since you came here to expand the family enterprise, your stepmother would at least wait until the trade routes here are established before getting rid of you. Eliminating you this early is tantamount to abandoning the business here.”

Fuling pondered it seriously. Indeed, that’s possible. “Could it be because I went to the black market?”

“Why do you say that?”

“Young Master, you may not know, but there is a black market not far from here. I went there tonight and saw a twenty-year-old lingzhi mushroom that looked decent, so I bought it. Could it be that I got lucky, and it’s not a lingzhi but something else?”

“Could you show it to me?”

Since Fuling owed Lu Yang her life, she trusted he wouldn’t harm her and took out the lingzhi she purchased from the black market.

The lingzhi was the size of a palm, with a dark red hue and concentric circles on its cap.

“Miss, you guessed half right. This thing is a lingzhi, but not an ordinary one—it’s a three-hundred-year-old Lightning Tribulation Lingzhi that was once struck by lightning. Due to the great tribulation it endured, its appearance differs greatly from a normal three-hundred-year-old lingzhi.

“It seems you have pretty good luck, miss.”

As a friend of the Little Herb Kings, Lu Yang had learned much botanical knowledge from them.

Lu Yang continued, “However, this still isn’t the reason for the assassination attempt on you.”

“Why is that?” Fuling’s eyes glimmered with bafflement.

“This assassin hid poison in his teeth, which clearly points to him being a professional, not someone acting on a whim for wealth. He climbed through the window to take your life.”

Fuling contemplated and shared, “I have a childhood sweetheart who cares for me. He is very outstanding. A female disciple from a sect likes him, but he rejected her, saying that while she is a great person, if he hadn’t met me first, he might have liked her.

“It’s possible that this female sect disciple sent the assassin.”

Lu Yang mulled over it and reckoned it was possible. For the time being, he couldn’t find any other suspicious points. “Which sect is this female disciple from?”

The assassin writhed on the floor, unable to speak due to the rag Lu Yang stuffed in his mouth. After listening to Fuling and Lu Yang’s analysis for a long time, he finally spat out the rag. “Umm, can you let me say something?”

The three looked down at the assassin simultaneously.

The assassin felt guilty under their gazes but still said, “Miss Fuling, right? Sorry, it seems I got the wrong person. My target is in the room opposite. She’s called Kongque[2].”

Fuling, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

Hearing the assassin’s words, Meng Jingzhou seemed to have solved the mystery, looking like realization had dawned upon him. “So that’s how it is.”

Lu Yang was stunned. “What did you understand?”

“I ran into a plundering cultivator in my room. He hid well, but I still found him. After subduing him, he confessed he intended to steal a lingzhi.”

Just then, Shi Chan also walked over. “Hmm, this poor monk was planning to head to your rooms to find you, senior brothers. Why are you here?”

“What is it?”

“Here’s the thing. I met a woman in the hallway. She stays here, and her name is Kongque. She said an assassin is after her. Noticing I have cultivation, she asked me to protect her. I wanted to ask you for your opinions, senior brothers.”

1. Fuling is the name of a common TCM ingredient and is a type of fungus. It is used for various symptoms and diseases. Its common properties are reducing water retention, calming the mind, improving digestion, and more. You may also find it in food and drinks for yangsheng purposes. ☜

2. “Kongque” means peacock in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 655: Self-Reliant

It was Shi Chan’s first time encountering a benefactor requesting protection. Compassion was the quintessence of monastic life. As a monk, protecting others was his duty. Thus, he agreed. However, he didn’t know what preparations or precautions were necessary to protect others.

Given his two senior brothers had roamed the jianghu for many years, Shi Chan figured they must be more experienced than himself, who had spent all his time slaughtering pigs. Hence, he decided to come and consult them.

Lu Yang looked down at the assassin. Originally, he had planned to check the opposite room for a lady named Kongque, in case the assassin was lying. Now, there’s no need.

Meng Jingzhou looked at Lu Yang on his left—the hero who saved the beauty—then at Shi Chan on his right—someone capable of protecting a beauty.

Why am I the only one who gets a plundering cultivator?

Plundering cultivator, why did you have to hide in my room for no reason? Go rob someone! If you don’t rob, how can I get my turn to be the hero saving the beauty?

The plundering cultivator hadn’t gone into the wrong room. He simply thought no new guests would arrive so late at night and hid in an empty room, intending to steal the three-hundred-year-old Lightning Tribulation Lingzhi after Fuling fell asleep.

Who would have thought three people would check in so late?

One could only say that he was unlucky like Meng Jingzhou.

Shi Chan finally noticed Fuling and was bewildered. “Benefactor Kongque, why are you here?”

“Master, you’ve mistaken me for someone else. My name is Fuling.”

“Senior Brother Shi Chan, what’s going on?”

“Benefactor Fuling and Benefactor Kongque look exactly alike.”

Lu Yang was astonished. “Miss, do you have a sister?”

“No...” Fuling started to deny it, but a layer of blurry memories suddenly surfaced. “Yes, I have a twin sister, but she went missing when I was very young.”

Lu Yang mentally sorted through the events and felt that he had pieced things together. He turned to Shi Chan. “Go and bring Miss Kongque over. Tell her the assassin has been caught.”

Shi Chan was taken aback. Could the person lying on the floor be the assassin?

Right, this black attire doesn’t look like it belongs to a good person.

Kongque was hiding in Shi Chan’s room, clutching the prayer beads he had left. Upon learning the assassin had been caught, she was overjoyed. She had even considered sharing Shi Chan’s room for the night.

As expected of a master, catching him so quickly.

“Thank you, Master!”

Shi Chan chanted “Amitabha” before saying, “Benefactress, you need not thank me. This was the effort of my two senior brothers. This poor monk didn’t contribute to this matter.”

Kongque assumed he was being modest and handed Shi Chan a storage ring. “Here are some spirit stones. Please accept them, Master.”

Shi Chan shook his head gently. “Compassion is the quintessence of monks; saving people is this poor monk’s duty. How can I accept money?”

“This isn’t for you, Master, but a donation for incense offered to Buddha.”

Shi Chan continued to refuse. “This poor monk is Buddha.”

“Ah?” Kongque was floored.

Without further explanation, Shi Chan followed Lu Yang’s instructions and brought Kongque to Fuling’s room.

As soon as the two young girls saw each other, they were momentarily stunned speechless.

The air seemed to congeal.

Fuling broke the silence first, her lips quivering, tears flowing uncontrollably. “Elder Sister?”

“Y-you’re my younger sister?”

“Elder Sister!”

“Younger Sister!”

The two girls embraced, weeping bitterly. Despite being separated at the age of two, they were reunited eighteen years later; it was a touching scene.

“Elder Sister, where did you go then? Why are you called Kongque now?”

Kongque wiped her tears, still sobbing. “After I got lost, my shifu found me. He searched everywhere nearby but couldn’t find you, so he took me back to his Daoist abbey and raised me. I was young and couldn’t remember my name, so my shifu named me Kongque.”

Lu Yang thought, I knew a professional assassin shouldn’t have mistaken the target. As I thought, there’s a reason behind it.

Fuling’s room was suddenly crowded: Lu Yang’s trio, Fuling, Kongque, the assassin, and the plundering cultivator Meng Jingzhou had dragged over.

Seven people gathered together.

Lu Yang silently scanned the crowd: reunited sisters, a visually challenged assassin, and a plundering cultivator intent on theft.

My initial plan was just to check into an inn. I simply entered the wrong room. How did so many things happen in the blink of an eye?

Now that the whole story was clear, Lu Yang was embarrassed to suggest that Fuling take the assassin to the authorities herself.

Two reunited sisters—one dragging an assassin and the other dragging a plundering cultivator as they cheerfully head to the yamen to report the crime—this scene feels wrong no matter how I imagine it.

“Let’s go, we’ll take them to the yamen.” Lu Yang sighed, deciding to see the good deed through. Besides, he couldn’t escape. Even if they didn’t go to the yamen, the constables would come to take his statement as a witness.

The seven of them noisily walked down, startling the inn owner.

I don’t remember there being so many people upstairs.

Lu Yang explained the situation to the innkeeper, who broke out in a cold sweat.

Thank goodness these three young heroes were here; otherwise, a murder would have occurred at my inn. The consequences are unthinkable—who would dare stay here afterward?

The innkeeper thanked them profusely and waived the lodging fees for Lu Yang’s trio, even promising they could stay as long as they wished.

Since the sisters had nearly been harmed in his inn, the owner also waived their fees and made the same promise as an apology.

The five of them carrying the two captives went out and soon encountered constables patrolling the streets. After hearing the story, the constables quickly brought all seven of them back to the yamen to understand the details.

The follow-up unfolded as Lu Yang expected—the assassin and plundering cultivator were handed over to the yamen, the three of them gave witness statements, and at the end, each received a brocade banner commending their courageous act for justice and spirit stones as a reward.

This time, Shi Chan did not refuse.

After all that hassle, the three were physically and mentally exhausted and could finally return to the inn to rest. Only the two sisters were still full of energy, having just reunited.

After a night’s rest, Lu Yang stretched lazily, feeling comfortable all over and rejuvenated.

“Old Meng, wake up!” Lu Yang was kind enough to knock on the door to wake Meng Jingzhou.

Meng Jingzhou opened the door with an unfriendly expression, staring resentfully at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang ignored his gaze.

Shi Chan emerged from his room in glowing spirits, completely different from his state last night. Clearly, he had also rested well. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, good morning.”

“Where are we going today? To perform a ritual?”

“It is so.”

Lu Yang teased, “I thought you’d use the spirit stones from the yamen rewarded to you last night to go to the brothel and temper your mental state.”

“Senior Brother, you jest. One shouldn’t receive rewards without corresponding merit. This poor monk did nothing yesterday. It was all thanks to you two senior brothers that I gained a reputation for acting courageously for justice. It was hard to refuse the imperial court’s spirit stones, so I’ll treat them as a donation to the sect. How could they be used for my personal purposes?”

“Want me to give you some spirit stones?” Meng Jingzhou suggested with a chuckle.

Shi Chan shook his head. “If this poor monk uses spirit stones given by Senior Brother Meng to go to the brothel, it wouldn’t be me going, but Senior Brother Meng going. It wouldn’t achieve the tempering effect.

“When Shifu could still speak, he often taught me to be self-reliant. The spirit stones for going to the brothel must be earned with my own ability.”

Chapter 656: Performing Good Deeds and Accumulating Virtue

“Then how do you plan to attract business? By going door to door?”

Shi Chan shook his head and pulled out a large banner from his identity jade tablet. The front listed various services, from exorcising ghosts to praying for children to healing illnesses; it had everything one could need.

The back of the banner read “Price Negotiable.”

Shi Chan led the two to the city’s busiest area. He paid a venue fee, secured a small empty spot, set up his stall, unfurled the banner, and sat down steadily behind the table. His movements were practiced, indicating it wasn’t his first time doing this.

He kindly brought out two extra chairs for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to sit on.

To Shi Chan’s left was a noodle vendor, and to his right was a shaobing vendor. Shi Chan’s banner was similar to a fortune-teller’s and especially eye-catching. Passers-by frequently turned their heads, noticing this idiosyncratic monk. However, as he was so unconventional, no one dared to approach for help at the beginning.

Shi Chan felt regretful. Every time I set up my stall, business will be slow at first. Later, when people realize I’m indeed a capable monk and line up to seek help, I will see a huge crowd, find the workload too much for me to handle, and leave early.

“People lack an innovative spirit and dare not accept new things. If I had your esteemed shifu’s gift of the gab, I would certainly also tell stories in teahouses to promote Buddhist teachings to the world.”

It was Lu Yang’s first time encountering someone praising his shifu, and he felt overwhelmed. If Shifu Nine Springs learns about this in the Nine Springs below, he’ll probably be gratified.

“By the way, Senior Brother Meng, have you considered joining a Buddhist sect? This poor monk observes that your Buddhist affinity runs deep; you’re even self-taught, developing the Single’s Curse Fist yourself. You must be a future Buddha like me.”

“...My Single’s Spirit Root doesn’t mean I’ll never have sexual activities in this lifetime.” The Single’s Spirit Root forces one into singlehood, while Buddhism demands voluntary singlehood. They are two different things.

Meng Jingzhou had long inquired with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy through Lu Yang. As long as I become an immortal, I will no longer be restricted by the Single’s Spirit Root and can freely indulge in my lustful desires.

“Brother Meng, that’s a fallacy. Buddhism advocates performing good deeds and accumulating virtue to gain good fortune.

“Once, a bhikkhunī (Buddhist nun) asked Buddha, ‘If someone originally intended to commit an evil deed but accidentally performs a good deed, can it bring good fortune?’

“Buddha replied, ‘Yes, it can. For those who perform good deeds, it is the action and not the intent that counts.’”

“So...?” Meng Jingzhou was perplexed, not understanding what point Shi Chan was trying to make.

“This poor monk is saying ‘it is the action and not the intent that counts.’ Senior Brother Meng, although you are forced to have no affinity with the opposite gender, in reality, you have achieved Buddhism’s requirement to stay away from lust. This is precisely a sign of deep Buddhist affinity.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Just you wait! I’ll see when you save enough money to go to the brothel. I’ll book the entire brothel in advance, then give you another twenty drops of yang-boosting blood. Let’s see how you hold it in!

With no business for the moment, Lu Yang chatted with the uncle selling noodles on the left, while Meng Jingzhou chatted with the uncle selling shaobing on the right.

After waiting about an hour, they finally got a customer.

The visitor was dressed opulently, adorned with gold and silver. He had a jade thumb ring on each thumb and a large, protruding belly.

“Master, my luck hasn’t been good lately. I’ve been having a streak of bad fortune. Several business deals fell through. Can I seek wealth here?”

Shi Chan wore a serene expression as he pressed his palms together. “Benefactor, if I could seek wealth, I wouldn’t be setting up a stall here.”

The wealthy merchant was rendered speechless. He had never met such an honest young monk. I thought he’d spout some nonsense, urge me to donate incense money, and then pretend to seek wealth for me.

Shi Chan introduced a second method. “Benefactor, if you insist on seeking wealth, you can ask my senior brother for help. Senior Brother Meng’s family is immensely wealthy, rivaling a nation. If you seek wealth from him, you can obtain a loan.

“You can also perform more good deeds to offset your bad luck.”

The merchant found this young monk quite unreliable, so he shook his head and left.

Seeing the wealthy merchant depart, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, somewhat regretful. “How foolish.”

In the Mahavira Hall, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was draped in a kasaya and sat on her lotus throne, her bearing solemn and majestic. However, her little feet were restless, her pink, pearl-like toes wiggling continuously.

“Who’s foolish?” Lu Yang was confused.

“That wealthy merchant. He doesn’t recognize others’ kind intentions and won’t listen to advice. This immortal has always advocated for performing good deeds and accumulating virtue. It’ll definitely dispel his bad luck.

“This advocacy of mine stems from personal experience. My life has been smooth-sailing, and it is related to frequently performing good deeds, contributing to charitable causes, and being willing to lend a hand.

“Thinking far back about the time before I ascended to an immortal, the world was in chaos. Killing was rampant, and conflicts between two parties invariably ended with one’s death.

“This immortal once challenged beyond my level, defeating the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal. Not only did I spare their lives, but I also cooked for them, turning conflict into harmony. For a time, I spread it as a beautiful tale.

“Buddhism often says ‘saving a life is better than building a seven-story pagoda.’ The principle originates from this event.

“In the ancient era, communication was limited. If one wished to learn from others, they must undergo harsh trials and swear deadly oaths. Even then, mastering true skills and knowledge wasn’t guaranteed; their shifu would keep some techniques to themselves. Worse, some used cultivation techniques to control disciples, planting gu poison, curses, or whatnot.

“This immortal was different. Seeing that Lianyi and Little Ling had talent, I imparted to them my cooking skills and the Play-Dead Technique without reservation.

“And there was the Barbarian Tribe. Seeing that they were naturally slow-witted, possessing great physical strength but not knowing how to use it, I enlightened their minds, allowing them to grow stronger.”

As Lu Yang listened to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s recount, he finally understood that sheer strength was the only true principle.

Could it be that my numerous misdeeds attracted the scourge that is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, bringing me bad luck?

Despite the first sale flopping, Shi Chan was not discouraged and continued waiting for the next one.

“Eh? Little monk, what are you doing here? Are you out of money?” A rather attractive woman stopped, looking at Shi Chan with interest.

“So it’s Benefactress Miaoshan.”

“Who is this?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

“Let this poor monk introduce you to her. This is Benefactress Miaoshan from the Spring Fragrance House. She was one of the many female benefactors who attended to me last night.”

Last night, after Shi Chan refined the twenty drops of pure yang blood, he wished to achieve the best tempering effect, so he called for multiple benefactresses at the Spring Fragrance House to test him.

“Little monk, if you’re out of money, I can serve you for free once.” Miaoshan licked her lips seductively.

“You jest, Benefactress Miaoshan. This poor monk indeed couldn’t withstand the trial last night and failed in tempering my mental state. But only one night has passed. At the moment, my heart is still like water and will definitely not be tempted by you, Benefactress.”

Seeing Shi Chan refuse, Miaoshan was rather disappointed. Noticing the services listed on Shi Chan’s banner out of the corner of her eye, she asked again, “What if I say I want to pray for a child?”

“Then you’ll have to pay, Benefactress.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes were red from envy. Is this the result of Shi Chan performing good deeds and accumulating virtue?

Chapter 657: Persuasion

Meng Jingzhou felt he had performed quite a number of good deeds.

Although my background isn’t great and I was forced to collude with the Meng Family, I had long run away from home and severed ties with them.

After coming to the Dao-Seeking Sect, I devoted myself to cultivation to avoid my father tracking me down someday and hanging me up for a beating.

Is this the result of fooling around with Lu Yang every day?

That’s not right either. How does Lu Yang have such deep immortal affinity, receiving personal guidance from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Miaoshan blinked, her face flushed with a spring-like charm. “In that case, little monk, how much money do you want?”

“Ten taels of silver.”

“Here.” Miaoshan didn’t hesitate, taking a silver ingot from her sleeve and slapping it onto the table.

Shi Chan verified the silver ingot’s authenticity, then turned to ask, “Senior brothers, the benefactress has a request. Which of you is willing to contribute?”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

This time, it was Miaoshan’s turn to be stunned. “Wait, shouldn’t you be the one, little monk?”

Shi Chan pressed his palms together, his expression solemn. “Benefactor Miaoshan, this poor monk has left secular life. How could I do such a thing?”

Miaoshan’s expression turned strange. Judging by your actions last night, you didn’t seem like someone who has left secular life.

Shi Chan continued, “What happened at Spring Fragrance House yesterday was merely this poor monk failing to withstand the test.”

“Then can I not pray for a child anymore?” Miaoshan asked.

“Yes.” Shi Chan returned the silver ingot to Miaoshan. “In a few days, once I have saved enough silver, this poor monk will head to the Spring Fragrance House again to temper my mental state.”

Only then did Miaoshan’s expression turn brighter.

After sending away two potential customers in a row, another hour passed before the third potential customer arrived.

“Master, you perform exorcisms here, right?” A middle-aged man approached Shi Chan, his expression clearly troubled. Fraudulent fortune-tellers loved deceiving such people; just a few ambiguous words could convince this middle-aged man that they were a true master.

“Yes. Benefactor, may I ask if you’re seeking an exorcism? From this poor monk’s observation, you are not invaded by evil spirits but have matters weighing on your heart, which is causing panic and cold sweats.”

Shi Chan poured some Heart-Calming Tea refined by the Hanging Monastery. “The tea is free of charge. Please drink.”

The middle-aged man drank the tea in one gulp and calmed down. “It’s not me; it’s my daughter.”

“What’s the matter with your daughter?”

“Once, my daughter went out and met a young fellow living two streets away. Since then, things got completely out of hand. She fell in love with him at first sight and claimed it was destiny, loving him wholeheartedly.

“I didn’t approve of this marriage, so she went on a hunger strike. She hasn’t eaten for three days now!

“In the past, when she threw tantrums and went on hunger strikes, she couldn’t last more than a day. This time, she actually lasted three days! Even tempting her with her favorite barbeque skewers from One More Time Barbeque Shop didn’t work!”

“Benefactor, separating lovers is not a good deed. This poor monk will not commit such an act for money; it damages my merit and virtue. Moreover, cases of love at first sight have existed since ancient times and are not rare. However, it’s inappropriate if the hunger strike leads to death. This poor monk can advise your daughter.”

“That would be wonderful.”

Shi Chan packed up the stall, and the three went to the middle-aged man’s residence.

On the way, they learned the man’s name was Zhong Ming. His family ran a medicinal herb business. As his wife died early, he raised his daughter alone. His daughter was named Zhong Qing’er, and the young fellow was named Kang Wei.

This morning, Zhong Ming had purchased a three-hundred-year-old lingzhi. Coincidentally, the seller was a female Qi Training cultivator. He asked her if there was any expert who could help if his daughter was possessed, and she recommended Shi Chan, whom she had met at the inn last night.

“So it was Miss Fuling who referred him,” Lu Yang mused. No wonder Zhong Ming directly asked Shi Chan about exorcism without suspecting a scam.

The residence was sizable with three courtyards,[1] and it also employed several servants.

Zhong Ming led the three to Zhong Qing’er’s boudoir. On the floor were meals and barbeque skewers that had already turned cold.

“This is my daughter’s boudoir. Uh, Master, since you have left secular life, can you enter a boudoir?”

“Naturally, I can.” Shi Chan pushed the door open and entered the boudoir in an aboveboard manner.

This boudoir couldn’t be any more ordinary. It had a round tea table in the center, burnt-out candles, miscellaneous books, a bronze mirror, and rouge and powder by the wall.

Zhong Qing’er lay on the bed, pale from hunger. Seeing her father bring in a monk and two unknown individuals, she said feebly, “If I can’t be with Milord Kang, I’d rather starve to death!”

“Miss, this poor monk is here to persuade you to eat. If you choose to starve to death, this poor monk also offers soul deliverance services, which are more expensive than persuasion.

“This poor monk is more adept at conducting soul deliverance rituals. I worked at a slaughterhouse for over a year. Countless livestock died by my hand, and I gave all of them deliverance rituals to help their souls find peace.” Shi Chan took out the large banner again, pointing to the words “soul deliverance” to prove he wasn’t lying.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou tried their best to look stern, like Shi Chan’s left and right guardians.

Zhong Qing’er, “...”

“This poor monk is not eloquent and lacks the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s gift of the gab, making it hard for persuasion to be effective. However, I have fasting pills and can force-feed you, miss.”

“If you’re unwilling, I can also throw you out of the residence and onto the street. At that time, with no one caring for your safety and no family support, you will naturally be willing to eat.”

The more Zhong Qing’er heard his words, the paler she became.

Zhong Ming also got a huge fright. Master looks gentle, but his methods aren’t gentle at all.

Tears welled up in Zhong Qing’er’s eyes from fright. Did Father find a monk or a butcher?

“I-I’ll eat.”

I just wanted to scare Father; I wasn’t actually planning to starve to death.

“Can I eat the barbeque skewers from One More Time Barbeque Shop?”

“No, you can’t. Benefactress, you haven’t eaten for three days. Overeating could be life-threatening. You should have light and plain food.” Shi Chan turned to Zhong Ming. “Please prepare a bowl of plain congee.”

Zhong Ming was surprised that his daughter acquiesced so quickly before being overwhelmed with joy. He immediately went out to cook personally.

Soon, Zhong Qing’er was sipping plain congee with a spoon.

“Thank you, Master. How much incense money would be appropriate?”

Shi Chan shook his head. “We can’t leave yet. Your daughter is indeed possessed. There is a very faint trace of power fluctuation on her.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded inwardly. They had also noticed that Zhong Qing’er was clearly under a spell. However, they didn’t know which spell it was—or rather, which spell could make someone fall in love.

“She is affected by the Illusion Dream Technique.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy identified the spell Zhong Qing’er was under at a glance.

“Illusion Dream Technique?”

“It’s a spell that makes people dream, with the dream’s content controlled by the caster. Remember this immortal’s Yellow Millet Dream Pillow? It’s similar, but inferior to my pillow.”

1. Larger houses and residences in ancient China were formed by courtyards. One courtyard typically consisted of a main room, side rooms, servant chambers, and hallways/corridors. Each courtyard also came with one front door and one back door. This image shows an example of a courtyard. Bigger houses have more of such “courtyard units.” In this chapter, the size or structure of the residence is described as “three in three out,” which points to the house having three courtyards. Having three courtyards suggests the owner is from the middle class. Five or seven courtyards are for nobles and high-ranking officials. As a rule of thumb, estates were not allowed to have nine courtyards due to “nine” being associated with the emperor. ☜

Chapter 658: Entering Dreams

“A spell related to dreaming?” Lu Yang rarely touched upon such matters. Dream-entering spells were an esoteric branch. From what he knew, only a few in the Dao-Seeking Sect, like First Elder, researched this field, with First Elder being the most proficient.

Suddenly, Lu Yang’s expression turned strange. He vaguely remembered that when he began cultivating, he had encountered a mysterious figure in his dreams who called himself “Tofu Heavenly Sovereign,” claiming one could become stronger just by eating tofu...

Back then, I was ignorant and assumed it was simply a nightmare.

But now that I think about it, could it have been Big Senior Sister’s doing?

“If you’re unfamiliar with dream-entering spells, it’s easy to fall victim to them. However, with this immortal here, I guarantee you won’t be controlled by such spells!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spent her days in the mental space watching spectacles or sleeping soundly, a testament to the depth of her research in dream-entering spells.

“One can control people by entering dreams?”

“Of course. You should have experienced it. You sleep and dream, and after waking up, the dream’s content gradually fades from memory, leaving only a blurry impression, right?”

Lu Yang nodded. The process sounds right.

“Then if someone uses a spell to determine your dream’s content and keeps this up long-term, wouldn’t you be subtly changed over time?”

Realization dawned upon Lu Yang, prompting him to remember something.

Long ago, a merchant guild performed large-scale dream-entering spells to advertise themselves and sell their goods, bringing about impressive sales figures for those products. Later, the scheme was exposed. Great Xia fined the merchant guild to the brink of bankruptcy and enacted advertising laws to prevent similar incidents.

“Immortal Fairy, are you saying this is the case for Young Miss Zhong?”

“Yes.”

Having received an immortal’s guidance, Lu Yang immediately shifted his consciousness back out.

At the moment, Shi Chan and Meng Jingzhou were still discussing what spell Zhong Qing’er was under when Lu Yang confidently stated the answer he had just acquired, earning high praise from Shi Chan.

“As expected of Senior Brother Lu Yang! Benefactress Zhong Qing’er must be under such a spell!”

Meng Jingzhou cast a sidelong glance at Lu Yang. I know exactly how capable this brat is. Such a professional answer clearly came from the immortal.

Shi Chan turned to ask Zhong Qing’er, who was still eating congee with pickles.

“Benefactress, did you truly fall for Kang Wei the first time you saw him? Have you seen him elsewhere before, like in a dream?”

The three hadn’t concealed their conversation; Zhong Qing’er overheard it while eating. Shi Chan’s question made her frown slightly, and she was uncertain. “I don’t remember clearly. I do feel like I’ve seen him somewhere before, but upon careful thought, I really haven’t.

“The moment I saw Milord Kang on the street a week ago, I felt we had known each other for a long time and that we were destined lovers.”

Zhong Qing’er hadn’t fallen in love with Kang Wei blindly. If he was truly behind this, she would certainly demand an explanation.

Shi Chan held up two fingers. “Two possibilities.

“Either the Nine-Netherworlds Creed is right, and reincarnation truly exists, which means you and Benefactor Kang were connected by fate in your past life.

“Or you are under a dream-entering spell.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Reincarnation does exist, but it’s limited to Li Haoran alone.

“The second possibility is most likely.”

Zhong Ming flew into a rage and slapped his thigh. “I knew that there was something off about that Kang brat!” He grabbed a metal shovel, ready to charge out and capture Kang Wei.

Shi Chan stopped Zhong Ming. “Benefactor, don’t be hasty. Kang Wei’s actions have violated the law, but we need evidence for a solid case. How about this? The three of us will also enter the dream tonight. Finding evidence within the dream is the safest method.”

Hearing this, Zhong Ming calmed down. Indeed, this is the best solution.

Lu Yang asked, “You can use dream-entering techniques?”

“I’ve learned a bit. Once, when this poor monk was out subduing demons and vanquishing evil, a female demon coveted my beauty and tried to control me in a dream. Fortunately, I was reciting scriptures in the Mahavira Hall in the dream, and the Buddha statue manifested, suppressing the female demon.

“I was worried similar incidents would happen, so I learned dream-entering techniques. If Benefactor Kang casts the Illusion Dream Technique tonight, I will pull both senior brothers into the dream.”

“Alright.”

“Benefactor Zhong Ming, please bring three sets of bedding, so we three senior and junior brothers can sleep.”

Zhong Ming immediately called servants to clean the boudoir’s floor and bring three sets of quality bedding from the side rooms.

“I am ashamed to speak of this, but it’s rumored that the founder of Buddhism could fall asleep anytime and anywhere, truly achieving the realm of ‘Heaven, Earth, and I coexisting.’ This poor monk has yet to reach such a realm; I need a bed to sleep.”

Lu Yang stole a glance at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who was sound asleep on her lotus throne in an extremely inelegant posture. Back in the Demon Region, she often slept in trees; she can indeed sleep anywhere.

They could only enter the dream at night; otherwise, if only the three of them entered the dream while Kang Wei didn’t, it would be pointless.

The waiting process was rather boring, so the three chatted with Zhong Qing’er.

Zhong Qing’er saw that Shi Chan was handsome with a dignified bearing. Although he was a monk, his looks were outstanding. He was worthy of being called a beautiful young man and far more handsome than Kang Wei.

Shi Chan noticed and admonished her. “Benefactress, this poor monk has left secular life. If you have any other thoughts about me, please sever them to avoid them forming a knot in your heart.”

Meng Jingzhou found Shi Chan an eyesore no matter how he looked at him and wanted to force-feed him twenty drops of yang-boosting blood right now.

Night fell.

Zhong Qing’er started dozing off during the conversation and soon fell asleep.

“Has the other party cast the spell?” Meng Jingzhou was eager. He had never actively entered a dream before.

“Wait a bit longer.”

Another quarter of an hour passed, and Shi Chan suddenly yelled, “Now! Senior brothers, prepare to enter the dream!”

Meng Jingzhou immediately lay down, burrowing under the comfortable quilt and closing his eyes.

Suddenly, his expression changed. “Oh no!”

“What’s wrong?”

“I’m too excited; I can’t fall asleep!”

The others were speechless.

Fortunately, Lu Yang was adaptable and quick on his feet. He darted out of the quilt and stretched. “No problem. I’ll just punch you, and you’ll fall asleep. Relax, or it won’t work as well.”

“What the heck, hold on, are you f*cking serious...”

A large fist gradually filled Meng Jingzhou’s vision. A loud bang followed, and he lost consciousness.

Lu Yang was satisfied with the results and fell asleep peacefully.

Shi Chan also fell asleep. In the dream, he formed hand seals and cast the Dream-Entering Technique, pulling himself and the two sleeping beside him into Zhong Qing’er’s dream.

“So we’re inside a dream? It feels so novel.” It was Meng Jingzhou’s first time consciously entering a dream, and he felt a hazy sensation.

Lu Yang also found it fascinating. They were in a peach blossom grove, with petals falling like pink snow.

“That is the benefactress over there.” Shi Chan pointed to a small pavilion not far away. It was the best viewing spot in the peach grove, allowing one to admire peach blossoms without getting covered in petals. “Don’t make a sound. Let’s sneak over and take a look first.”

The three tiptoed quietly toward the pavilion.

Inside the pavilion, Zhong Qing’er was dressed boldly, far more seductively than the attire she wore in her boudoir.

She was holding the hand of the Shi Chan she had dreamed, gazing at him affectionately. The illusory Shi Chan had hair and was even more handsome.

“Shi Chan, let’s be together, shall we?”

“Alright.”

Not far away, a man stumbled over, watching the scene in disbelief.

“Qing’er, who...who is he?”

Zhong Qing’er looked at the man and said flatly, “Kang Wei, let’s break up.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

He turned to look at the real Shi Chan.

Brat, do you have some kind of Succubus Immortal Physique?

Chapter 659: Pendant

Originally, the trio’s plan was to find concrete evidence, expose Kang Wei’s true colors, and make Zhong Qing’er realize her previous love was just a deception.

All that was now unnecessary; she had fallen in love with someone else—Shi Chan.

“Senior Brother Meng, you jest. This poor monk is merely more handsome than the average person. Alas, people only see my fine outer appearance but remain unmoved by my Buddhist principles.”

Meng Jingzhou’s desire to hit someone grew stronger.

Meanwhile, the drama of two men vying for one woman continued in the pavilion.

“Kang Wei, you’re a good person, but we’re not suitable for each other.” Zhong Qing’er snuggled against the fake Shi Chan’s embrace, watching his expression while speaking to Kang Wei, afraid the fake Shi Chan might be displeased.

The fake Shi Chan booped Zhong Qing’er on the nose. “Silly, why would I be unhappy? You rejected him and chose me. I can’t be any happier.”

“Shi Chan, you’re so great.”

“You too.”

Kang Wei, “...”

What’s going on? Everything was fine yesterday. How come I’m being cuckolded today?

And in a dream too.

“Looking at Kang Wei, he seems like an ordinary person with no signs of cultivation.”

Even if cultivators didn’t reveal their cultivation, their breathing and walking differed from those of ordinary people who had never cultivated, unless they deliberately concealed it or had reached the realm of returning to simplicity.

“How can an ordinary person use dream-entering spells?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou frowned. Wouldn’t that make the two of us seem stupid?

“Let’s just make a move now. I honestly can’t watch this anymore; it’s giving me goosebumps,” Meng Jingzhou proposed.

As Shi Chan watched his fake self and Zhong Qing’er being lovey-dovey, he also found it hard to bear and silently nodded in agreement.

“Go!” Meng Jingzhou roared, his voice so loud it startled even Lu Yang.

“Who’s there?!”

Kang Wei reacted first. He was lucid in the dream. As Zhong Qing’er was the dream’s owner, she was muddle-headed and slow to react.

However, Kang Wei’s quick reaction was useless. When the three top prodigies of the current era acted, even Divine Transfiguration cultivators would avoid confronting them head-on, much less an ordinary person like him.

The three charged forward, pinning Kang Wei to the ground. With a thought, Shi Chan conjured a rope and bound Kang Wei tightly.

“We’ve had our eyes on you for a while now, brat. Behave!” Meng Jingzhou warned fiercely, his visage distorted with menace.

Only then did Zhong Qing’er react. “Two...two Shi Chans?”

Shi Chan looked at Zhong Qing’er quietly, deciding that he must stay as far as possible from the Zhong Estate after this matter was resolved.

Suddenly, Kang Wei’s figure began to fade. Shi Chan was sharp-eyed and adroit, deftly producing a talisman and sticking it on Kang Wei’s forehead to halt the transformation. “This poor monk has prevented his awakening. Senior brothers, please wake up and go to Benefactor Kang’s house. I will remain here to prevent any unforeseen incidents.”

“Alright, but how do we wake up?”

“Follow me.” Shi Chan demonstrated a hand seal and placed it before his chest. He didn’t conceal his meridian circulation when performing the hand seal; with Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s talents, they could learn it just by watching him once.

The two slowly woke up, kicked off their blankets, and sprang up like a carp kip-up.

They had already gotten hold of Kang Wei’s address from Zhong Ming. Carrying Shi Chan, they jogged two streets while ignoring the surprised looks from passers-by and found Kang Wei’s home.

His home was a simple house made of bricks and tile, far inferior to the Zhong Family’s large three-courtyard residence.

The two kicked the door open and found Kang Wei fast asleep inside.

“He really is an ordinary person.”

“What’s that in his hand?”

Kang Wei’s fingers were interlaced over his chest, holding a pendant.

“There are spirit energy fluctuations from the pendant; it should be a magical artifact. His ability to invade Young Miss Zhong’s dream is related to this pendant.”

Lu Yang shook Shi Chan. “Wake up, we’re here.”

Inside the dream, Shi Chan felt himself awakening and preemptively threw Kang Wei out of the dream. Otherwise, if he left the dream and Kang Wei didn’t, the latter might take Zhong Qing’er as hostage.

Kang Wei and Shi Chan woke up in succession.

Kang Wei naturally knew the others were cultivators and that he stood no chance.

Shi Chan demanded, “Benefactor Kang, this poor monk hopes you will confess truthfully.”

“Choose—will you confess obediently, or do we beat you up before you confess?” Meng Jingzhou cracked his knuckles loudly. He pressed Kang Wei against the wall and punched the wall beside his ear.

Without a word, Lu Yang extended two fingers and shot out a green sword qi that was one zhang long. It merely took a casual swipe for a corner of the nearby table to fall off, making Kang Wei’s heart tremble with fear. He was just an ordinary mortal and had never witnessed such a scene.

“I’ll confess, I’ll confess everything. Where should I start?”

“From how you met Young Miss Zhong and where you got this pendant!”

“Y-yes. The first time I saw Young Miss Zhong was a month ago. It was a chance encounter on the street, and I fell in love with her at first sight. From then on, I lost my appetite and couldn’t sleep; all I could think of was her.

“However, I knew my background wasn’t worthy of a wealthy young miss. Yet, I couldn’t let her go.

“At the time, Boss Hong approached me. He said he had a pendant; as long as I aimed it at Qing’er, I could enter her dream every night. Over time, with constant hints and prompts, she would come to like me.

“To buy this pendant, I even took out a huge loan from a merchant guild.”

“Who is Boss Hong?”

“He’s the local gang leader around here and has over thirty subordinates. I met him at a gambling den. He once cultivated at the Bamboo Leaf Sect and is a cultivator with unfathomable power. Later, he did something wrong in the sect and was expelled.

“Although he was expelled, I heard he still has contact with the Bamboo Leaf Sect’s masters in private.” Kang Wei attempted to use the Bamboo Lead Sect’s name to scare the trio.

“Where is Boss Hong?” Lu Yang was unmoved; he hadn’t even heard of this minor sect.

Kang Wei didn’t answer, and Meng Jingzhou assumed a ferocious expression, resembling the legendary Acalanatha (Immovable Vidyaraja). He frightened Kang Wei until the latter trembled like a leaf, forcing him to lead them to Boss Hong.

Boss Hong lived just one street away.

“Hong Estate. Quite imposing.”

Boss Hong’s residence was even bigger than the Zhong Family’s.

“Halt! Who are you?!”

As the local gang leader, Boss Hong had men stationed at the entrance of the Hong Estate to prevent enemies from knocking on his door.

Lu Yang’s trio naturally didn’t bother with answering. With a casual wave, they sent the guards flying.

Inside the Hong Estate, Boss Hong’s subordinates were raucously gambling as they ate and drank. Seeing the three intruders, they rushed forward to stop them.

Meng Jingzhou punched the air, and the resulting sonic boom directly knocked these people unconscious.

~~~

In a room deep within the Hong Estate, Boss Hong was conversing with a young lady. “Junior Sister, your request is a little difficult. The authorities are very strict about this. If they trace it back to me, I’m afraid my life would be over.”

The young maiden smiled and handed Boss Hong a wooden box. “I’ll have to trouble you to put in more effort, Senior Brother Hong.”

Boss Hong opened the box, and his heart skipped two beats.

It’s actually a Foundation Establishment Pill! And it’s not the lowest grade either!

Without batting an eyelid, he stowed the box away calmly and smiled. “The authorities may be strict, but who is your senior brother? How could I not have a way? Who do you want me to kill though?”

“She’s called Fuling, from Xuan City. Her cultivation is at the Level Three Qi Training Stage. She has come here to do business. Just a slightly pretty woman who dares to snatch my lover-gege. She truly doesn’t know how the character for ‘death’ is written!”

Boss Hong smiled ingratiatingly. “In that case, she truly deserves to die.”

Suddenly, sounds of fighting came from outside.

Boss Hong furrowed his brows. “I’ll go out to see what’s going on.”

“Who are you people?!”

Boss Hong walked out of the room, radiating his Great Perfection Qi Training aura to intimidate the trio.

A young woman dressed in bright clothes followed Boss Hong out. She had a well-proportioned figure and a pitiable countenance.

At first, Lu Yang thought Boss Hong had abducted her, but then he noticed she was at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

A Bamboo Leaf Sect disciple?

“Did you sell this pendant to Benefactor Kang?” Shi Chan chanted “Amitabha” as he retrieved Kang Wei and the pendant.

“So what if I did?” Boss Hong knitted his brows, not expecting them to be here for this reason.

Selling a pendant isn’t illegal. Why are a monk and two protectors looking for me in the middle of the night instead of sleeping?

Lu Yang sneered. “Selling a pendant isn’t illegal, but instigating Kang Wei to deceive Young Miss Zhong is wrong.”

There was another reason he didn’t reveal. This pendant is a magical artifact, while Kang Wei is just an ordinary person who could afford it only through a loan. Its origin might not be clean.

“Who are you people? Aren’t your hands reaching a bit too far into others’ business?” Boss Hong had mingled in the jianghu for years and wasn’t easily bullied. With a low shout, two massive hands composed of black mist materialized behind him.

“Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang.”

Clang.

Without another word, Boss Hong knelt on the ground, hands behind his head. “I am guilty. I’ll turn myself in.”

Chapter 660: Fortune Affinity Runs Deep

Had it been constables or yamen bailiffs, Boss Hong would have mustered some courage to resist.

But Lu Yang was different.

Who in Great Xia didn’t know Lu Yang? Cultivators knew he had fought Young Creed Leader Lu of the Heavenly Court Creed to a draw at the Golden Core Stage, and commoners knew he was the protagonist of Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang.

The Five Great Immortal Sects were factions of inconceivable prestige, their ranks overflowing with mighty cultivation experts as numerous as clouds. Rumors even said they didn’t bother subdividing the Qi Training Stage.

On the other hand, the Bamboo Leaf Sect’s old ancestor, who boasted the highest cultivation, was only at the Nascent Soul Stage. That didn’t even qualify for polishing the shoes of someone from one of the immortal sects.

As for Lu Yang of the Dao-Seeking Sect, it went without saying. He was a peerless prodigy who had served as the acting sect leader at a young age and was the undisputed future sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Even the city lord would have to treat Lu Yang with the utmost respect, let alone a mere Qi Training cultivator like myself.

Meng Jingzhou shot a glance at the slightly smug Lu Yang, a wave of regret washing over him. I was a beat too slow in announcing my own name. Even if I do so now, the effect would be inferior to Lu Yang’s.

The young maiden who had emerged with Boss Hong also jumped in fright at Lu Yang’s name. To think this is the legendary Prodigy Lu! Compared to Prodigy Lu, the person I like seems insignificant.

Besides, this Prodigy Lu is also pretty good-looking.

Judging by the positions of the two men standing beside him, they should be his equals. Both are exceptionally handsome, especially the monk; he’s the most handsome.

The young maiden began mulling over which of the three she should choose.

Lu Yang narrowed his eyes and smiled. “Boss Hong, turning yourself in isn’t as simple as just surrendering. You must also truthfully confess all your deeds.”

“I’ll confess, I’ll confess everything!” Boss Hong hastily assured him.

“Where did the pendant you sold come from? And how many have you sold?”

“It...it was over a month ago. Someone approached me, hoping I could help him sell a batch of pendants. I was reluctant at first, but his cultivation was high. My situation would be dangerous if I had refused, so I had no choice but to agree to his demands.

“That person also had one specific condition—I could only sell the pendants to mortals, not cultivators.”

Lu Yang frowned. “Who was this person? What did he look like? What was his cultivation level?”

“I-I don’t know his name. He was tall and thin, like a bamboo pole. A-and I don’t know his cultivation level either.”

The trio furrowed their brows. It seemed the person behind the pendants had ulterior motives, though they weren’t sure what his goal was.

“Immortal Fairy, wake up, stop cultivating.” Lu Yang entered the Mahavira Hall within his mental space and shook the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who was practicing her Dream-Entering Spell.

“Ah? What is it? Is Lass Yun attacking?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mumbled with her eyes half-open, groggily sitting up from her lotus platform.

“We’ve encountered a matter and could draw upon your knowledge.”

“Yawn... What is it?”

“See this pendant in my hand?”

“Pendant?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw the pendant swaying in his hand through his perspective. “Who refined this?”

“Is there a problem with this pendant?”

“There’s no problem. It’s just that the refining technique is crappy, far inferior to my Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.”

Lu Yang was speechless for a moment. “What about its target? Does it work on both mortals and cultivators?”

“It's too crudely crafted; it can only enter the dreams of mortals. There’s no problem with the refining concept. Had it been refined more meticulously, it could have affected cultivators’ dreams as well. If I must pinpoint a problem, it would be that this pendant can record dreams.”

“Record dreams?”

“Meaning it can record the content of the dreams and their effects on the dream’s owner.”

Lu Yang couldn’t figure out the perpetrator’s ultimate goal.

Never mind, I’ll stop thinking about it; let the authorities handle it.

“And who are you?” Lu Yang turned his gaze to the pitiable-looking young maiden.

“I-I’m his junior sister. I was just dropping by to visit him,” the young maiden stammered, frightened by Lu Yang’s scare.

“Oh? You have a twenty-year age gap, and you visit him late at night—a lone man and a single alone together in a room?”

“Y-yes.”

Shi Chan took a step forward, chanting a True Words Mantra. A massive golden Buddhist character was imprinted on the young maiden’s forehead. “Benefactress, please speak the truth.”

Under the influence of the True Words Mantra, the young maiden confessed her motive in full detail. “I came to ask Senior Brother Hong to kill a rival named Fuling...”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why is it Miss Fuling again?

Since the situation was now clear, there was no need to linger. Lu Yang left the Hong Estate and found a constable patrolling the streets.

“Brother constable, we have another case here!” Lu Yang called out to him. Last night, they had handed over the killer and the plundering cultivator to this very constable.

I didn’t expect to run into him again here.

After Lu Yang explained the events at the Hong Estate, the constable stared at him as if he had seen a ghost.

Last night, you delivered a killer who attempted murder, and tonight, you’ve caught a bunch of people who aborted a murder attempt?

The constable nearly assumed that Lu Yang was an out-of-town assassin expanding his business here, making use of the authorities to eliminate local competitors.

The constable quickly contacted his superiors and soon summoned a large contingent of constables who escorted everyone from the Hong Estate to the municipal office for interrogation the same night.

The Zhong father and daughter also came to the yamen as a witness and a victim respectively.

“Master, is the matter over?” Zhong Ming asked.

“Indeed. The matter concerning your daughter was caused by Kang Wei’s use of a magical artifact. The truth is already revealed, and it now depends on how the authorities handle it.”

“Thank you so much!” How could Zhong Ming not be thrilled? The problem that has plagued me for a week was resolved by the master in a single night. “Then about the incense money...”

“Five hundred taels of silver.”

For Zhong Ming, five hundred taels was a paltry sum. He immediately produced a silver note worth one thousand taels from his sleeve. “Master, this is a small token of my gratitude.”

“That is too much.” Shi Chan insisted on accepting only five hundred taels of silver.

Unable to persuade him otherwise, Zhong Ming could only produce a five-hundred-tael silver note and present it deferentially.

With the matter concluded, Shi Chan returned to the inn, not even sparing a glance at Young Miss Zhong.

“Going to the Spring Fragrance House tonight to temper your mental state?” Lu Yang teased. Following Shi Chan to perform rituals is truly an eye-opening experience.

“Not so. Only one night has passed; it is not yet the peak of this poor monk’s lustful desires, so the tempering effect won’t be optimal. In my view, it is better to wait quietly for three days.

“Now that’s attention to detail.”

~~~

Upon returning to the inn, the trio ran into Fuling and her sister, who had also just returned.

“Eh, Master, you’re back very late.”

“The ritual took some time. This poor monk observes that you have also returned rather late, benefactresses.”

Fuling smiled, her eyes narrowing to slits. “We were lucky today. We finally secured a deal with a client who had been unyielding before. It was only after discussing many details that we realized how late it was.”

Shi Chan chanted “Amitabha.” “Benefactress Fuling, your fortune affinity runs deep.”

“Then I’ll borrow your auspicious words and hope that comes to pass. But what happened today was indeed quite strange.

“I don't know why, but that client who was raising excessive demands just yesterday changed his tune today. He said things like ‘consider it performing good deeds and accumulating merit’ and ‘let’s see if what the Master said works.’”

Chapter 661: High Efficiency

“I was too exhausted last night and didn’t get the chance to ask, but Miss Kongque, why did that killer target you?” Meng Jingzhou asked, his voice filled with a valiant and righteous spirit.

Kongque pondered for a moment. These three had saved my last night; they’re trustworthy, so it should be fine to tell them. “This isn’t a convenient place to talk. Shall we return to my room first?”

The group of three men and two women proceeded to Kongque’s room.

She poured tea for the four guests and set down the teapot, unhurriedly beginning her tale. “This all started after my shifu left the Daoist temple. The temple my shifu presided over was called the Mountain River Temple. Only he and I lived there.

“In his youth, my shifu attracted many romantic debts and often had lovers knocking on his door. As time passed, Shifu saw that my cultivation had progressed enough for self-preservation and used traveling the world as a pretext to leave the temple and evade his creditors.

“After learning of my shifu’s departure, the visits from those lovers decreased significantly. The temple became cold and desolate, left with me alone.

“One day, while I was meditating in my room, I heard a loud noise from the courtyard. I rushed out to find a blood-soaked man who had crashed into the courtyard. The man was handsome, but grievously wounded; even his collar was drenched in blood.

“I couldn’t bother to think that much. I carried the man inside, cut away his clothing, and tended to his injuries. The man remained unconscious for roughly a week. I don’t know what cultivation technique he practiced, but his wounds gradually healed.”

“When the man finally woke up, he was reticent, not even uttering a word of thanks, and he outstayed his welcome at the temple. Since I couldn’t just throw him out, I had no choice but to let him remain in the temple.

“Another month passed, and the man’s injuries had fully recovered. Suddenly, he grabbed my wrist and said he had fallen for me, hoping I could leave with him.

“But I didn’t even know his name or background. His attitude was overbearing, and my wrist hurt from his grip. After I broke free, I refused him outright.

“The corners of his mouth twisted into a cold smile. He said no one had ever dared to refuse his orders before and that I was the first. He stated that anyone he desired must either become his or become dead. If I didn’t go with him, he would send an endless stream of assassins after me. Then, he left.
