“I wasn’t sure whether he was bluffing, but I kept feeling like his words carried a wicked aura that terrified me. I packed my belongings that very night, thinking that if I came to a bustling city like this, the assassins he sent wouldn’t dare to look for me.

“That’s how I came to Chunjiang[1] City, where I also encountered my younger sister and you three young heroes.”

“So arrogant?” Meng Jingzhou raised an eyebrow. Even I, an almighty Holy Son of the Heavenly Court Creed, and the hoodlum Young Creed Leader beside me wouldn’t act like that.

“Miss Kongque, rest assured. With us here, no assassin can harm you!”

“Amitabha, so that’s how it is. It seems last night’s assassin was just the first. More assassins will likely come for Benefactress Kongque in the future.”

Shi Chan retrieved a string of sandalwood prayer beads from his sleeve and gifted it to Kongque. “These beads have been imbued with this poor monk’s vow power. It can withstand attacks at the Nascent Soul Stage for a quarter of an hour, and I will also sense when they are activated. Please accept them for your protection, Benefactress Kongque.”

“Na-nascent Soul Stage?” Kongque was flabbergasted. How many spirit stones must this be worth? I can’t afford something this precious even if I sell myself. “I-I can’t afford this.”

Shi Chan smiled, pressing them into her hand. “Buddha said, ‘Saving a life is better than building a seven-story pagoda.’ I will receive my reward in due time. You need not offer anything, Benefactoress. This poor monk simply hopes you will refrain from committing evil deeds and perform more good deeds in the future. That will be considered repayment.”

“Many thanks then, Master.” Kongque treated the prayer beads as a priceless treasure, wrapping them in a handkerchief before carefully tucking them into the front of her robe. “This is the second time I’ve received the grace of Buddhism.” Kongque smiled brightly.

“Second time?”

“The first time was a story our mother told us. It happened before we sisters were born. I was separated from my family when I was very young, so my memories are vague.

“Younger Sister, you probably remember it more clearly than I do, right?”

Fuling gave a soft affirmative. “Initially, Father and Mother struggled to conceive a child. They happened to hear that the Ancient Forest Temple housed a senior monk proficient in praying for children, so Mother went there to seek out that monk, named Master Yuxin.

“After returning, Mother indeed became pregnant.

“Mother told us that our births were a grace from Buddhism and a blessing from Buddha. She said we must perform good deeds and accumulate virtue to repay the grace of Buddha.

“After Elder Sister went missing, Mother also went to the Ancient Forest Temple to find Master Yuxin. Unfortunately, Master Yuxin had already passed away in a seated posture.”

Lu Yang’s expression turned peculiar. Master Yuxin’s method for granting fertility worked so quickly? Was it a proper method?

He turned to Shi Chan. “Have you heard of the Ancient Forest Temple or Master Yuxin?”

Shi Chan shook his head lightly. “There are countless temples in the world; this poor monk can’t know them all. As for Master Yuxin, I have not heard of him either. Perhaps he was an accomplished monk who concealed himself within the mundane realm.”

Knock, knock, knock.

Sounds of knocking came from Kongque’s door.

“Is Miss Kongque in?”

Kongque immediately grew wary, fixing her gaze intently on the door as a strong sense of danger swirled in her heart.

“Who is it?”

“From the yamen.”

Kongque was bewildered and grew even more vigilant. Why are people from the yamen looking for me? I’d told them everything I could when I reported the case last night.

Lu Yang knitted his brows. He used his spiritual consciousness and observed that the people outside were indeed constables—or at least, dressed in constable uniforms. Furthermore, their cultivation levels weren’t low, at the Golden Core Stage. They also carried a faint scent of blood, likely having just killed someone.

Lu Yang gave Kongque a meaningful look, signaling that it was safe for her to open the door with the three of them present.

Mustering her courage, Kongque opened the door to reveal three unfamiliar constables.

The constables were also taken aback to see three men and two women in Kongque’s room. Why are there so many people?

“Which one of you two ladies is Miss Kongque?” the lead constable asked, unable to distinguish between Fuling and Kongque. It would be embarrassing to mistake one for the other.

“I am. May I ask the reason for your visit?” Kongque replied calmly.

“This involves your privacy, Miss Kongque. Please step outside for a moment.”

Kongque grew even warier and shook her head firmly. “Everyone here is trustworthy. You may speak here.”

The lead constable hesitated for a bit, but chose to respect Kongque’s decision.

“It’s like this. Miss Kongque, based on the reason you provided for being targeted by the assassin last night and the employer named by the assassin himself, we reported the situation to our superiors immediately. We’ve already used these clues to identify the man who wants you dead. The provincial governor deemed him a major scourge and instructed us to take action immediately.

“Just moments ago, in a coordinated operation across multiple cities, we raided this man’s stronghold and arrested him. A total of three Divine Transfiguration cultivators, fifteen Nascent Soul cultivators, and several Golden Core cultivators participated in this operation, and I’m one of them.

“We wanted to confirm with you, Miss Kongque. Is this the man?” The constable pulled a sheet of paper from his robe. The man depicted on it was handsome, with a trace of wickedness in his features.

Kongque, “...”

You authorities are quite efficient, huh?

1. “Chunjiang” translates to “spring river.” ☜

Chapter 662: Ambush

“It’s him.” Kongque nodded, her expression peculiar. The sheer efficiency of the authorities had taken her a moment to process.

“Then we have the right person.” The lead constable let out a sigh of relief.

If we’d gone through so much trouble the whole day only to nab the wrong person in the end, that would really be a farce. But even if we had caught the wrong guy, this man we captured is no good person either. Based on the evidence on hand, this person is a serious repeat offender. Everyone involved in this operation will be credited with a major contribution.

“According to procedure, Miss Kongque, we still need you to provide a formal statement of identification. Could you follow us to the yamen?”

Kongque nodded. It was her legal obligation. “Can they come with me?” She pointed to Lu Yang’s trio and Fuling. She felt uneasy going to the yamen alone.

“Of course, they can. However, they cannot be present during the recording of the statement.” The lead constable understood Kongque’s apprehension, which was only natural.

As they were speaking, two more constables came upstairs.

“Which one of you is Miss Fuling? Hmm? Big Brother Li, you’re here too? Weren’t you out making an arrest?” The two constables who had just arrived were stunned to see the lead constable.

Big Brother Li replied casually, “We’ve made the arrest and are verifying the details with the victim. What brings you two here, Little Wu?”

“Oh, we just finished interrogating a suspect. According to her confession, she attempted to hire a local thug surnamed Hong to assassinate a young woman named Fuling. We’re also here to verify the details.

“Which one of you is Miss Fuling?”

“I am, I’m Fuling.” Fuling rose from the bed and stood beside her sister, Kongque.

But who wants me dead though?

Big Brother Li, “...”

Little Wu, “...”

Do assassins have some special interest in you two sisters? They seem to be swarming around you.

“Then, could you two young ladies come with us?”

The sisters nodded.

“Miss Kongque, you were lucky to encounter only a Qi Training assassin last night. According to the confession of the assassin we captured, there are Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, and Nascent Soul assassins above him. If he fails, progressively stronger assassins will be sent after you.

“Although it was due to our negligence that an assassin snuck into the inn last night, please rest assured, Miss. Now that we have this lead, a second assassination will definitely not occur.”

If the assassin last night hadn’t confessed everything, the authorities wouldn’t have dispatched three Divine Transfiguration and fifteen Nascent Soul cultivators. As for whether even higher-level cultivators were deployed in secret, Big Brother Li wasn’t aware.

Just like the previous night, the five of them found themselves once again at the yamen.

The guards on duty for the night shift were taken aback to see the same group of people two nights in a row.

“This poor monk wishes to ask, what is the background of the benefactor who threatened Miss Kongque?”

“Apologies, little master. We have regulations; those not directly involved in the case cannot inquire about its details.”

Shi Chan nodded, indicating he understood.

The imperial court was very professional in this aspect. While the Five Great Immortal Sects did hold law enforcement authority, it couldn’t be wielded arbitrarily based on personal curiosity, for that would violate the original intention of granting such power.

Last night, when the three gave their statements as witnesses, they had identified themselves as ordinary cultivators and used pseudonyms, not revealing they were from immortal sects. The authorities wouldn’t scrutinize the identity details of witnesses.

Based on Shi Chan’s experience, if they had announced themselves as cultivators from the Five Great Immortal Sects, it would have alerted the city lord, who would then host them enthusiastically while subtly inquiring about their departure date... After all, the immortal sects also held supervisory authority. If the immortal sects filed a negative report against them, their entire year’s work would be in vain.

The two sisters were taken away by two respective groups of constables to give their statements, while the trio remained in the case-handling area, awaiting the outcome.

“Immortal Fairy, could you help listen in on that interrogation?” Lu Yang couldn’t help but ask.

Currently, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was painting on the walls of the Mahavira Hall. She held a brush and had numerous buckets of pigment at her feet, while her face was smudged with a rainbow of colors.

As for what she was painting, it was too abstract for Lu Yang to decipher.

“Deal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tossed the brush into a bucket and wiped her face with the back of her hand, smearing the colors further. Sharing her immortal consciousness with Lu Yang, she probed the interrogation process of the captured man.

The interrogation room was equipped with arrays specifically designed to block spiritual consciousness, but they were clearly ineffective against immortal consciousness.

~~~

Encaged by multiple layers of arrays in the interrogation room, two seasoned constables stared sternly at the man that had just been arrested.

The man was handsome with a wicked aura. His hands were bound by Spirit-Energy Restraining Manacles, rendering him unable to mobilize his spirit energy.

The two seasoned constables were under immense pressure. The suspect was suspected to be suffering from a mental disorder with abnormal thought processes, though they couldn’t be sure if it was an act or genuine.

“Name?”

The handsome man smiled nonchalantly, habitually moving to fiddle with his nails, but the manacles prevented him from doing so.

“Heh. This is the first time someone dares to ask for this esteemed one’s name so bluntly. There's no harm in telling you. This esteemed one is Ye Xiao.”[1]

“Age?”

“One thousand six hundred years old.”

A constable slammed the table furiously, pointing at the man and shouting, “I advise you to be honest! Stop playing dumb!”

Ye Xiao’s gaze turned gloomy. “If I were you, I wouldn’t do that. You are merely two low-level cultivators. How dare you order this esteemed one around? Summon a Fusion cultivator who is qualified to speak with me.”

The other constable seemed to recall something and held back his partner, asking suspiciously, “Are you an archaic Fusion cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew?”

“Your eyesight isn’t beyond saving.”

Realization dawned upon the two constables. No wonder.

“Specific identity?”

“You don’t even know this esteemed one’s identity, yet you dare arrest me? Quite audacious, huh! This esteemed one is the leader of the Dark Night Pavilion, Ye Xiao.[2] Even the Great Yu Emperor had to treat me with courtesy!”

The two constables rummaged through their historical knowledge. It seemed there was an assassin organization established in the 60,000th year of the Great Yu calendar, which was about 140,000 years ago.

“Then why did you re-establish an assassin organization after dispersing your cultivation to cultivate anew?” Based on the circumstances of this arrest, Ye Xiao was tyrannical and had formed a new assassin organization.

“You are but two insects, yet you dare to inquire about this esteemed one’s plans? There's no harm in telling you.

“In the Battle of the Great Era, an individual’s power is limited. Operating alone to compete for resources is ultimately futile against major factions. That is why this esteemed one re-established the Dark Night Pavilion.

“Do you know what the strongest type of cultivator is? It is not the sword cultivator who breaks all spells with one sword or the physique cultivator with a peerless physical body. Those are merely for frontal combat. Between cultivators, all methods are fair game. Assassination is the best way to victory. Therefore, assassins are the strongest cultivators.”

He slowly rose to his feet. “The Dark Night Pavilion has returned to the world; all of you shall be its sacrifices!

“As for that woman who piqued this esteemed one’s interest, Kongque, was it? She can’t escape from my grasp! This esteemed one has already spoken—she either submits to me, or dies.

“Those who defy this esteemed one haven’t been born yet!”

The constable slammed the table angrily. “Behave! Sit down!”

Ye Xiao pretended he didn’t hear him, continuing as if he was talking to himself. “I dispersed my cultivation to cultivate anew. Someone will naturally guard this esteemed one’s path.”

The two constables’ expressions changed as they realized something. There are accomplices we haven’t captured, and their cultivation isn’t low!

A terrifying oppressive pressure shrouded the City Lord Estate; it was a Fusion cultivator!

In the dark night, that Fusion cultivator extended a giant hand, shattering the layers of arrays encasing the interrogation room, tore off the room, and said respectfully, “Pavilion Leader, I am late.”

“You’re too slow! Receive your punishment when you return!”

The vice pavilion leader had been raised by Ye Xiao since childhood, branded with a master-servant mark. Even though Ye Xiao had dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew and their power levels were vastly different now, the vice pavilion leader must still obey Ye Xiao’s commands.

Suddenly, three more Fusion auras erupted, locking onto the vice pavilion leader. Each of these three auras was more powerful than his.

“The provincial governor really had good foresight. There is indeed someone behind him.”

“Enough talking. Seize him quickly so we can go back and rest.”

“It’s a big fish.”

The vice pavilion leader’s eyes bulged with wrath. “Running dogs of the imperial court!”

It’s a trap! The imperial court had laid an ambush!

The vice pavilion leader turned to flee, but the three Fusion cultivators wouldn’t give him the chance. They acted simultaneously, capturing him.

The two constables heaved a sigh of relief and pressed Ye Xiao back into his chair. “Behave!”

“I’ll confess everything.”

1. “Yexiao” means owl. ☜

2. The “ye” in his name also means night. ☜

Chapter 663: Learning Fist Techniques

Bulletin from Chunjiang City Yamen:

Recently, the victim, who goes by Kong (female), was attacked by an assassin. Three courageous cultivators intervened to stand up for justice and seized the assassin, preventing a malicious assault. Kong is unharmed.

According to investigations, this heinous case is a crime of passion. Following clues provided by the assassin, the yamen immediately launched a comprehensive investigation, secured relevant evidence, and tracked down the assassin organization “Dark Night Pavilion.” All individuals involved have been arrested.

It is reported that the organizer of this heinous incident and the leader of the assassin organization are both the Great Yu cultivator, surnamed Ye, who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew. Relying on the protection from the former vice leader of the Dark Night Pavilion, surnamed Fan, he acted arrogantly and feigned foolishness.

Currently, the yamen has arrested Fan, and Ye is confessing his crimes. According to Ye’s confession, the Dark Night Pavilion is connected to multiple heinous murder cases. Ye will face severe legal punishments.

In the early morning, notices explaining the previous night’s commotion were posted at the entrance of Chunjiang City’s yamen and the city gates. Commoners gathered around them, discussing fervently. After all, no matter how thorough the preparations were, the commotion caused by three Fusion cultivators jointly apprehending another Fusion cultivator could not be small.

“Good job arresting them! These archaic cultivators really have no regard for the law!”

“Archaic cultivators again? Is there an end? I say we should kill them all early. What a hassle!”

“I heard the incident at Hanshui City a year ago was also the work of archaic cultivators.”

“The Hanshui City incident was a major case involving three archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. We can’t compare to that.”

When Lu Yang and his two companions were leaving the city, they happened to spot the notices posted at the city gate.

“Senior brothers, have you heard of the Dark Night Pavilion?” Shi Chan hardly interacted with archaic cultivators and knew little about archaic organizations.

In contrast, Lu Yang possessed bountiful archaic knowledge. “The Dark Night Pavilion was an assassin organization established in the mid-Great Yu era. Its name originates from its founder, Ye Xiao. At that time, the emperor was vying for power with the imperial preceptor. To win the favor of high-level cultivators, the emperor treated the Dark Night Pavilion with courtesy. After Ye Xiao’s disappearance, the Dark Night Pavilion went through three generations of pavilion leaders and declined significantly, eventually replaced by a new rising assassin organization.”

Lu Yang had listened to the entire interrogation record last night.

Ye Xiao indeed had the grounds to be arrogant. His area of activity spanned the nearby cities where the highest cultivation level was only the Divine Transfiguration Stage. With Vice Pavilion Leader Fan, a Fusion cultivator, protecting him, he could be considered extremely safe.

Moreover, according to Ye Xiao’s investigation, the imperial court had not previously captured any archaic reforged cultivators. They had caught a few Fusion cultivators, but that was because those archaic cultivators acted too ostentatiously, specifically provoking Great Xia’s Fusion cultivators.

He, however, was different. He only provoked low-level cultivators.

Based on his experience in Great Xia, he believed Great Xia would assume their faction only had Nascent Soul members. To capture them, Great Xia would at most dispatch Divine Transfiguration cultivators, not Void Refinement or Fusion cultivators.

This went without saying. He had merely taken a fancy to a Qi Training female cultivator and sent a Qi Training assassin to kill her.

Who could have imagined that the assassin sent last night would lead Great Xia to dispatch three Divine Transfiguration cultivators today, as if they grew on trees.

If that were all, he still wouldn’t have been scared. His attitude throughout the interrogation showed nothing but confidence. With the vice pavilion leader around, he was assured he could escape at any time.

However, it was a big shock that Great Xia didn’t play by the rules and secretly dispatched three Fusion cultivators. Had they sent one less person, the vice pavilion leader could have escaped.

Through the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal consciousness, Lu Yang found out even more information.

Last night, only three Fusion cultivators had shown themselves...

Just so they could continue fishing.

When Fusion cultivators were invited to hold the lines but weren’t asked to act, they still required payment. The funds allocated by the imperial court to crack down on organized crime and illegal activities in You Province were plentiful, so they might as well use them.

Furthermore, it was rare for an evil or a criminal faction to show itself; one might not appear for years. This all counted as meritorious achievements. If time permitted, the provincial governor would have considered inviting a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Unfortunately, they overestimated the Dark Night Pavilion—they only had a total of one Fusion cultivator.

“Senior brothers, thank you in advance for instructing this poor monk.”

At the yamen last night, Shi Chan had expressed his desire to learn the Single’s Curse Fist and the Lu-Style Arhat Fist from the two. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t plan to withhold their knowledge and agreed readily.

“Senior brothers, you gifted this poor monk pure-yang blood and are willing to instruct me in fist techniques. I have no way to repay such a favor. Unfortunately, everything I learned is Buddhist teachings imparted to me by my shifu. Without my sect’s permission, I cannot transmit them to others. In terms of creating spells, I am far inferior to you two senior brothers. If the opportunity arises in the future, I am determined to repay this grace.”

Lu Yang laughed heartily, patting Shi Chan’s shoulder. “We’re all disciples of immortal sects. Don’t fret about it. Speaking of which, aren’t you continuing to set up a stall to earn money today?”

Shi Chan shook his head. “Benefactor Zhong Ming has already given this poor monk five hundred taels. It’s sufficient for one visit to the Spring Fragrance House.”

“One more visit is enough to temper your mental state?”

“This poor monk is still uncertain whether it’ll succeed, but I must have this resolve.”

All three were at the Nascent Soul Stage. When performing a set of fist techniques, the wind from their fists alone could topple houses. It was inconvenient to execute fist techniques in the city, so they chose to go outside.

“This place should do.”

The trio selected a spacious, empty area with no one around, ensuring they wouldn’t accidentally harm passers-by.

Lu Yang started first. “Let me state upfront. I’m not clear about why my Arhat Fist causes hair loss. I have yet to figure out the underlying principle. All I can do is demonstrate it a few times for you to observe.”

“That will suffice.” Shi Chan knew the Arhat Fist. He simply wanted to understand the difference between the Lu-Style Arhat Fist and the ordinary one.

Lu Yang assumed a horse stance and began performing the moves with loud shouts. Each punch was powerful and vigorous, accompanied by faint Buddhist sounds—a sign that the Arhat Fist had been cultivated to a profound realm.

Shi Chan watched with a grave expression, carefully observing Lu Yang’s every punch and kick.

Lu Yang concluded the demonstration. “How was it?”

Shi Chan shook his head. “This poor monk is slow-witted and can’t discern the difference.”

“Switch. My turn.”

Meng Jingzhou was eager for someone to learn the Single’s Curse Fist—or rather, for everyone to learn it. When exchanging blows, everyone would use the Single’s Curse on each other, and everyone would be single, creating an ideal world.

“My Single’s Curse Fist originates from the lineage of the Single’s Spirit Root. It’s uncertain if an outsider can learn it. You must be mentally prepared.”

“This poor monk understands.”

Meng Jingzhou executed the Single’s Curse Fist. Setting aside the fist technique’s effect, its power alone made it a terrifying technique comparable to the Arhat Fist.

Shi Chan furrowed his brows tightly. He had some inkling regarding the Single’s Curse Fist—it was a fist technique that was imbued with karma and heavily tested one’s comprehension.

After completing the set, Meng Jingzhou wasn’t even short of breath. “How was it?”

“It encompasses karma and places high demands on the caster’s destiny. Senior Brother Meng, this poor monk lacks your uniquely advantageous conditions and fears it will be difficult for me to learn.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Let’s mark out a field and spar, and you shall explain to me what you mean by “uniquely advantageous conditions.”

Despite studying for an entire day, Shi Chan’s efforts ended in regret.

Even three days later, after Shi Chan had successfully conserved his energy and built up his strength, he still hadn’t mastered either technique.

Shi Chan once again consumed twenty drops of yang-boosting blood, recited the Heart Sutra, and strode into the brothel, his expression aloof and transcendent.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou waited at the inn for the outcome.

They waited until early morning the next day, when Shi Chan finally returned.

On his way back, Shi Chan still recited the Heart Sutra, just like when he had first entered.

The two were quite surprised. This took much longer than last time. Did he persist the entire night?

“Did you succeed?”

Shi Chan stopped reciting and said earnestly, “This poor monk recited sutras, maintaining an empty and lofty mental state. In the latter half of the night, the benefactresses exhausted all their methods and shattered this poor monk’s empty and lofty mental state.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“However, this poor monk gained much from this trip.”

Meng Jingzhou was curious. “What did you gain?”

“This poor monk’s endurance has improved.”

Chapter 664: Immensely Satisfying

At a teahouse.

“There’s a prodigy in the Dao-Seeking Sect named Meng Jingzhou. This person is truly remarkable. He is the eldest young master of the Meng Family, the world’s number one clan, and known as Eldest Young Master Meng in the jianghu!

“Eldest Young Master Meng’s talent goes without saying; he possesses the one in a million Single’s Spirit Root!

“If it were an ordinary person with such talent and background, they would have been content with the status quo and unmotivated to improve. But Eldest Young Master Meng is different. He voluntarily relinquished his comfortable life in the Meng Family and headed to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Passing its numerous trials, he finally became a disciple of the sect.

“Eldest Young Master Meng doesn’t rely on external aids but solely devotes himself to seeking immortality. Such steadfast resolve is truly admirable!

“One day, Eldest Young Master Meng was out on a mission, accompanied by a female disciple from an immortal sect. They pursued a vile jiao-dragon over a great distance and engaged in three major battles before finally slaying the wicked jiao-dragon at the Turquoise Water Pool.

“That vile jiao-dragon was no easy foe. In the battle at Turquoise Water Pool, it fought desperately and released a poisonous gas. As the two immortal sect prodigies’ eyes widened at the realization that they couldn’t evade it, Eldest Young Master Meng pushed the female disciple aside and was hit by the poisonous gas.

“He temporarily suppressed the poison with his cultivation, but once the arduous battle concluded, he could no longer endure the poison.

“Only then did the two discover that this vile jiao-dragon was actually a lascivious one—it had released not mere poison but an aphrodisiac gas! Those afflicted by this poison would lose their reason and seek to vent their urges with the opposite sex until the poison dissipated. It had always been so since ancient times.

“But who was Eldest Young Master Meng? His Dao heart was staunch, and he did not waver in the slightest despite facing feminine charms. He would rather let his whole body swell and turn red than vent the desires in his heart!

“In the end, Eldest Young Master Meng forcefully overcame the lustful jiao-dragon’s poison by relying solely on his willpower!”

This was a rising storyteller surnamed Jin. Rumors in the jianghu spread that the previous storyteller who narrated Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect was nearing the end of his lifespan and had found a successor.

Of course, these were merely rumors in the jianghu. The storyteller, Mr. Jin, had repeatedly come forward to deny this gossip.

Nevertheless, Mr. Jin was indeed qualified to inherit the mantle. His storytelling was riveting and widely praised, his skills second only to the previous storyteller.

“If you wish to know what happens next, please stay tuned for next time!” Mr. Jin struck his gavel, concluding today’s storytelling session.

Dressed in a traditional buttoned jacket, he excitedly rushed backstage to find the Taciturn Daoist Priest. “Big Brother, how was my performance?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest held a horsetail whisk, his clothes spotlessly clean. He set down the teacup beside him and calmly gave an appraisal. “Not bad. There is improvement. It seems you have quite the talent in this area. Your previous lack of eloquence was simply because you hadn’t found a suitable training opportunity.”

“Many thanks for your guidance, Big Brother!” Chieftain Jin looked at the Taciturn Daoist Priest gratefully. Without him, I wouldn’t be where I am today.

He was currently focusing on promoting Meng Jingzhou, hoping the Meng Family would be more lenient when demanding repayment from him.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest added, “However, there are still areas where you need training.”

“Please enlighten me, Big Brother!”

“Your adaptability is lacking. If you wish to train such an ability, you must pay a certain price.”

A hint of ruthlessness glinted in Chieftain Jin’s eyes. “Big Brother, I can pay any price to become stronger.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was satisfied with his attitude. Those who achieve great things must have the courage to burn their boats and cut off their means of retreat. “Then come with me to deceive the world! Back then, we, the Dao-Seeking Nine, could successfully deceive the Nine-Netherworlds Creed precisely because of our deception skills we had honed over the years!”

Chieftain Jin deeply agreed. After all, he was the first one who had been deceived.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest stressed, “You must always remember the ‘fraud of an exceptionally large sum’ stipulated in criminal law. That’s the bottom line that mustn’t be crossed.”

Seeing the Taciturn Daoist Priest speak so gravely, Chieftain Jin also grew nervous and swallowed hard. “What if I cross that bottom line?”

“You’ll be sentenced to life imprisonment!”

Chieftain Jin felt enlightened and nodded vigorously. “I’ll remember it.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest continued, “Different regions have different regulations regarding the ‘fraud of an exceptionally large sum.’ I will tell you about them one by one.”

“Thank you for the reminder, Big Brother!”

Just as the two were about to say more, they suddenly felt a sense of impending doom, as if a sharp executioner’s blade was resting on their necks, ready to behead them at any moment.

Danger!

The bustling streets, the jostling crowds, the hawking waiters, the sugar painting dropped by a child...everything became extremely sluggish, as if time in the world had slowed down.

Only one graceful figure seemed out of place, walking leisurely toward the two men. The graceful figure placed the sugar painting back into the child’s hand and stood before the two.

“I happened to pass by this city and sensed the mark I left, so I came to check on the situation. I didn’t expect to find an unexpected harvest.”

“Ph-Phoenix Ancestor?!”

Chieftain Jin was the first to recognize Jiang Lianyi, followed by the evil and wicked Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The two broke out in a cold sweat. We shouldn’t have offended the Phoenix Ancestor, but judging by her attitude, it certainly doesn’t look like everything is fine!

Jiang Lianyi was passing through when she sensed the mark she had left on Chieftain Jin. Somewhat curious why the Qiongqi Tribe’s chieftain would appear in Great Xia, she followed the trail and unexpectedly found the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Found you.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest felt her gaze, and his scalp went numb.

I’ve always been mindful of not going overboard. When did I provoke this deity?!

Besides, I’ve never even seen her before!

As if she was aware of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s bewilderment, Jiang Lianyi retrieved a book from her storage ring that looked extremely familiar to him.

Dragon Phoenix Transformation.

“I heard you wrote this book?” Jiang Lianyi questioned.

Damn it, I forgot this book exists!

Chieftain Jin stared in astonishment at his big brother. Even he had heard of Dragon Phoenix Transformation.

This is a forbidden book that infuriated both the Dragon and Phoenix tribes, and its author has been a mystery. So you were the one who wrote it?!

“No need to answer. Your expression says it all.” Jiang Lianyi burned the book to ashes.

Lu Yang had kindly reminded me that his shifu is full of lies and his words can’t be trusted.

Jiang Lianyi slowly rolled up her sleeves. “Humiliating my Phoenix Tribe is a crime deserving of death.

“Considering that Lu Yang is my senior brother, and you are Lu Yang’s shifu, it seems we can only handle things separately, lest I go easy later.

“I am currently a guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect. A guest elder beating the sect leader is considered insubordination and breaches etiquette.

“Fortunately, jiejie told me that those who achieve great things shouldn’t bother about minor details; one should temporarily discard rigid etiquette.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was utterly flummoxed as he listened to her. What do you mean, Lu Yang is your senior brother? Isn’t that an act? And what’s this about being the Dao-Seeking Sect’s guest elder? Since when does our sect have a guest elder?

A string of question marks flashed through the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s mind.

Even more nonplussed than the Taciturn Daoist Priest was Chieftain Jin. Piecing the Phoenix Ancestor’s words together, he seemed to have guessed the true identity of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Wait...wait a moment, don’t beat me yet. I still have questions... Ah!”

Chapter 665: Summoning Clouds and Rain

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, was an author and educator. His works included Dragon Phoenix Transformation, The Evolution of Prison Conditions in the Great Xia Dynasty Over Two Millennia, Size At Will (Localized Version), and Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect. He had taken four disciples: Yun Zhi, the world’s most supreme cultivator; Ye Zijin, the enemy of the Buddhist Kingdom; Gan Tian, the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden; and Lu Yang, Young Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed. His achievements in education are everlasting and will be remembered by history.

Due to an indecent matter, he quarreled with the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, and they came to blows. The Taciturn Daoist Priest was no match for the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. He died at the age of over two thousand years, bringing immense satisfaction and universal celebration.

~~~

Time resumed its flow.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest and Chieftain Jin were beaten until they were left hanging by their last breaths. Jiang Lianyi tossed them onto a rooftop to avoid tripping passers-by.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was perplexed. Who exactly had leaked the matter about Dragon Phoenix Transformation?

Big Brother, Old Two, Old Three, Little Zhi...

The scope is too big; all have motives. It’s hard to guess.

Chieftain Jin felt wronged. The Little Ancestor was the mistress, so why beat me? Is it just because I look easy to bully?

Based on the Phoenix Ancestor’s fragmented words earlier, could it be that the Dao-Seeking Sect was established by the ancient Heavenly Court? This would explain why the Phoenix Ancestor is a guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

However, judging by Big Brother Taciturn’s expression, he doesn’t seem to know about this. Could it be a secret even the sect leader is not privy to?

This is a huge secret! The Dao-Seeking Sect is terrifying! It appears to be one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, but in reality, it’s merely a facade presented to the world.

Maintaining a disguise for ten thousand years—the thought of it alone is frightening.

Maybe I should advise the Little Ancestor to stop fighting alone—let’s join either the Qilin Immortal or the Heavenly Court Creed.

Jiang Lianyi shot a glance at Chieftain Jin, who was lost in his wild speculations, but didn’t pay him much attention. With the imprint left by the Incipient Dao Fruit, no matter what he knew, he wouldn’t be able to speak of it and divulge secrets.

~~~

Chunjiang City.

Lu Yang sat beside Shi Chan, waiting for business to fall into their laps.

Their luck was good today; soon, a customer approached.

A handsome young man sought out Shi Chan with a request. “Master, can you pray for rain?”

“Amitabha. This poor monk naturally knows the Rain Summoning Technique.”

“In that case, could you help me make it rain heavily tomorrow evening? The price is negotiable.” The handsome youth stared at Shi Chan eagerly. I’ve finally found a master who can summon rain.

“This poor monk must first ask, for what purpose do you require rain, Benefactor?”

The young man dared not lie to a monk. “I have a date with a close female friend tomorrow. I thought that if it suddenly rains heavily in the evening, and neither of us has an umbrella, we will surely get drenched. That way, I will have an excuse to take her to a nearby inn to change clothes, facilitating further development.”

Shi Chan pressed his palms together and admonished, “Benefactor, please return. This is considered immoral conduct. I urge you to desist from it in time.”

The handsome young man beseeched persistently, “Master, name a price. I can pay any number of spirit stones.”

“This is not a matter of spirit stones. Please return, Benefactor.”

Seeing Shi Chan’s firm attitude, the young man had no choice but to leave in disappointment and search for other experts capable of summoning clouds and rain.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know how to summon clouds and rain?”

“Who doesn’t know that? Although summoning clouds and rain is a method of the dragons, the principle is simple. Even you could learn it.”

“How so?”

“The simplest method is to fill a storage ring with water, then fly up into the sky, toss the storage ring into a spray bottle, and activate the storage ring through the spray bottle. Voila, you have rain.

“If you think one spray bottle isn’t enough, you can use a few more.”

Lu Yang nodded. “It does sound quite simple.”

It doesn’t even require a spell, so I definitely won’t learn it off-kilter. The only drawback is that it wastes too many storage rings and spray bottles.

“All rain summoning techniques evolved from this basic principle. For example, when the Nine-Layers Immortal ascended to an immortal, sweet dew descended from the heavens, golden lotuses sprang from the earth, the sound of the Great Dao resonated, and all manner of chaotic unusual phenomena occurred. The commotion was terribly huge, as if he feared no one would know he was the first to become an immortal.

“Later, he told us the truth. The so-called ‘sweet dew descending from the heavens’ was actually him pouring sweet dew into a spray bottle so that he could pour it on himself after ascending to an immortal.

“And as for the ‘golden lotuses springing from the earth,’ he had planted lotus seeds in the ground and used the Tree-Planting Mantra to accelerate their growth. Breeding these golden lotuses cost him many natural treasures before he succeeded in mutating the green lotuses.

“The ‘sound of the Great Dao’ was more troublesome. He had privately collected the cries of various races, then mixed them together to prevent others from discerning what the sound of Great Dao actually was. People would just think it sounded incredibly impressive.

“He had almost emptied his entire savings to create so many unusual phenomena. He’s the classic example of suffering just for the sake of appearances. Look, when this immortal ascended, there were no unusual phenomena at all—simple and clear.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Nine-Layers Immortal, you heard it, right? The one exposing all your secrets is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Every grievance has its source, and every debt has its creditor. Please don’t come after me; I’m just a bystander.

Not long after, a young man dressed as a scholar approached, though he looked somewhat haggard.

“Master, can you exorcise ghosts?”

Shi Chan nodded. This is a hallmark ability of Buddhist sects. “Of course, I can. Is your house haunted by ghosts, Benefactor?”

“Maybe, but I haven’t actually seen a ghost.”

“What’s the situation?”

The scholar’s face was scrunched up with worry. “Every night, when I’m sound asleep, I keep feeling like someone is beside me. But when I open my eyes, there’s nothing. This has been going on for a long time.

“I’ve also sought assistance from several masters. Some left empty-handed, while others left protective talismans upon leaving, but none were effective.

“I even tried reporting it to the authorities. However, when the bailiffs came, the ghost no longer appeared, and once the bailiffs left, I felt someone beside me at night. The bailiffs can’t possibly stand guard by my side every night.

“Yesterday, I was disturbed by the ghost and lacked energy. I found a friend and bought a three-hundred-year-old lingzhi to nourish my body, and the friend who sold me the lingzhi recommended you, Master.”

“Benefactor, may this poor monk ask, the friend who sold you the lingzhi is...”

“Big Brother Zhong Ming. He said he had enlisted your help in exorcising evil a few days ago.”

“So that’s how it is. That’s indeed so.”

Shi Chan stood up and packed his belongings. “In that case, this poor monk and my two senior brothers will go take a look.”

“That would be wonderful.” The scholar was overjoyed.

“This poor monk has yet to ask for your name, Benefactor.”

“I am Xu An.”[1]

“So it is Benefactor Xu.”

Seeing that there was finally some proper work to do, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou also packed their things and followed behind to check on the situation.

On the way, Xu An briefly introduced his background. He was a scholar and had a wife. His parents had died early, leaving him a substantial inheritance that allowed him to live comfortably. His greatest wish was to study the classics of the sages diligently, become the zhuangyuan top scorer in the imperial examinations, and bring glory to his ancestors.

Xu An led the three through several alleys. “This is the place.”

Xu An’s residence was no smaller than Zhong Ming’s. After all, anyone who could afford a three-hundred-year-old lingzhi that had endured lightning tribulation must be quite wealthy.

1. In a way, the name can be understood as “wishing for safety.” ☜

Chapter 666: Too Many Suspects

“Your residence is quite spacious, Benefactor Xu.”

Xu An smiled sheepishly. “My parents were cultivators and left behind a considerable fortune before their passing. Unfortunately, my talent is limited, and I have never been able to set foot on the path of cultivation. Please excuse my embarrassment.”

Since he could not cultivate, studying the classics of the sages diligently to earn fame and fortune could also be considered not disgracing his parents’ name. Unfortunately, he had likewise achieved no success in the imperial examinations.

Xu An typically didn’t share these matters with others; Lu Yang and his companions were the exception. He had heard from Zhong Ming that Shi Chan and the two protectors were likely great cultivators at the Foundation Establishment or even Golden Core stage. People with such cultivation won’t covet my paltry wealth.

Pasted on the inner side of the Xu residence’s gate was a yellow talisman, left by a previous cultivator to exorcise ghosts. Although it was pretty much useless, having it there provided some peace of mind.

The four entered the Xu residence and came across a young maiden sweeping the courtyard. Judging by her relatively plain clothing, she was a maidservant.

Upon seeing her master enter with three guests, the maidservant quickly moved aside to avoid offending the guests.

The maidservant was rather pretty, and Meng Jingzhou glanced at her a couple of times.

“This is Little Cui,” Xu An said with a smile. “Last year, while traveling to take the examinations, I rested for a night in a mountain temple, where I happened to meet Little Cui. She told me some villains were chasing her and asked me to help conceal her. Sure enough, a few fierce-looking men burst into the temple later. I followed Little Cui’s instructions and covered for her, saving her. She said she had no way to repay such a great favor and became my maidservant.”

“Greetings, lords,” Little Cui uttered timidly in a soft voice.

Meng Jingzhou nodded. This is a female ghost.

The four passed through the Flower-Dangling Gate[1] and entered the second courtyard. A woman dressed in luxurious clothes emerged from a room. “Hubby, you’ve come just in time. The three-hundred-year-old lingzhi you bought has been simmered... Who are these three?”

Xu An called out to her, “Xiangyu, quickly greet the three masters. Haven’t I been saying that my sleep quality has been poor lately, as if I’m haunted by evil spirits, leaving me dazed all day? Those few cultivators I invited were also not effective. Well, Big Brother Zhong Ming, who often deals with cultivators, recommended these three masters. They are genuine experts with real abilities.

“Let me introduce you to my humble wife, Liu Xiangyu.”

“So it is Benefactress Liu.”

“Three masters.” Liu Xiangyu performed a greeting bow.[2] “As a woman, seeing my husband suffer daily pains my heart, yet I am powerless. I must trouble you three masters.”

“Amitabha. This poor monk will do his best.” Shi Chan dared not speak in absolute terms. This is a snake demon.

“Come, three masters, please come inside,” Xu An warmly invited the three into the main hall for proper hospitality.

“That won’t be necessary, Benefactor. We need to study your residence carefully to make the relevant preparations.”

“That’s good, that’s good.” Xu An was overjoyed. Experts are indeed experts—they act swiftly and decisively.

“Little Zhu, come here,” Xu An yelled.

Shortly after, another maidservant put down her work and hurried over.

“Little Zhu, show the three masters around the compound.”

“A-alright.”

Little Zhu had a pleasant appearance with expressive eyes.

Lu Yang saw through Little Zhu’s true form—a fox demon.

Just as Little Zhu was about to lead the three away, Liu Xiangyu brought out a bowl of black soup—the medical decoction simmered from the three-hundred-year-old lingzhi. Given Xu An’s constitution, he couldn’t consume an entire lingzhi at once; only a small portion was used for the soup.

Meng Jingzhou sniffed the air and frowned slightly. He wasn’t sure if it was his imagination, but he detected a faint trace of blood in the black soup.

The three toured the Xu Estate carefully and roughly grasped the situation.

The three-courtyard compound housed five people in total, including Xu An, his wife, and three maidservants.

Simply put, only Xu An was human.

The third maidservant was Little Qiu, an artifact spirit.

When it was time for the vegetarian meal in the evening, Xu An looked at the trio expectantly. “Masters, have you found anything?”

Shi Chan chanted, “Amitabha.” “We have found some clues, but the specifics will depend on tonight.”

There were too many suspects; they weren’t sure which one was responsible.

“The three of us will keep watch by your side tonight to protect you, Benefactor Xu.”

“Then I shall thank you in advance, masters!”

The candle was blown out. The three masters sat in meditation by Xu An’s bedside. At ease in his heart, Xu An was soon fast asleep.

Suddenly, a fragrant breeze wafted by. The trio’s consciousness grew light, and they fell into slumber.

A graceful figure pushed the door open and looked at the three with a giggle.

“And here I thought my savior had invited some great experts. So it’s just three Golden Core kids.” With her spiritual consciousness, she had detected that all three were at the Golden Core Stage.

“I wonder when I’ll be able to reveal my identity to Savior.” The graceful figure gazed at Xu An’s sleeping visage and licked her lips. She removed her clothes and gently kissed him.

Their lips didn’t actually touch. A wisp of yang energy drifted out from Xu An’s mouth and was absorbed by the graceful figure.

Then, she began groping him all over.

Lu Yang’s trio pretended to be asleep but were secretly observing this scene and communicating through their spiritual consciousness.

“Xu An has quite the luck with women. This female ghost’s cultivation is not low.”

“No wonder he feels his yang energy is deficient. It’d be strange if his yang energy is sufficient.”

“So the one sucking Xu An’s yang energy is the maidservant, Little Cui.”

“She was really committed to the pretense.”

Ghosts couldn’t touch physical objects. During the day, when she appeared to be sweeping the courtyard, she was actually just posing and using her mind to control the actions. The trio had noticed this upon seeing Little Cui.

It was the same now. Little Cui was merely absorbing Xu An’s yang energy while entangling with him intimately in his dreams. This was a method commonly used by alluring ghosts.

Meng Jingzhou was particularly sensitive to ghosts, which was why he had glanced at Little Cui a couple of times.

After the amorous session, Little Cui left the Xu Estate, thoroughly satisfied. The trio immediately followed her to investigate.

~~~

It was now late at night, and many shops had closed.

Little Cui arrived at the door of a closed shop. She scanned her surroundings and confirmed no one was around before lightly knocking on the wooden door.

It seemed the other party was expecting someone. As soon as the knock sounded, the door opened.

Little Cui strode into the shop.

Lu Yang looked up at the sign.

One More Time Barbeque Shop: Chunjiang City Branch

“Branch Leader, welcome to our shop for inspection!” the shop attendant said respectfully.

“How many times must I say it? Our Nine-Netherworlds Creed runs a legitimate business. Call me Shop Owner.”

“Yes, yes.”

The shop attendant retrieved an account book. “This is today’s revenue.”

Little Cui opened the account book and checked it item by item. The barbeque shop was the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s primary venture; no mistakes could be tolerated.

Seeing that the branch leader was in a good mood, the attendant suddenly asked, “Shop Owner, do you really plan on being that Xu An’s maidservant forever? With your status, why do you need to go this far? If you ask me, just reveal your identity, tie him up, and bring him here. He'll comply with anything then.” He was anxious watching their branch leader. Our branch leader is an almighty Nascent Soul cultivator, yet she’s demeaning herself to be a maidservant in a mortal’s household.

Little Cui flatly refused. “No, Milord Xu saved my life. How could I treat him like that? As for revealing my identity, that’s even more impossible. If he learns of my identity, he will be considered guilty of harboring a diabolic creed disciple. How will he participate in the imperial examinations in the future?”

1. The chuihua-men, directly translating to “flower-dangling gate” is an iconic door in traditional Chinese courtyards. It separates the outer and inner courtyards. Its name originates from how the eaves do not touch the ground and are often decorated with flower patterns. The design of the chuihua-men can also reflect the family’s power and characteristics. This image shows an example of how such a gate may look. ☜

2. To be more specific, this is a wanfu curtsy, common among women. One slightly bends their knees and lower their head while placing their hands in front of their chest. “Wanfu” means to wish fortune and prosperity to the other party and is typically used as a greeting. This video shows how the wanfu curtsy was performed in the Tang, Song, and Ming dynasties. ☜

Chapter 667: Great Luck With Women

“This barbeque shop is actually run by the Nine-Netherworlds Creed? This poor monk will subdue this ghost immediately. Please lend me your aid, senior brothers!” Shi Chan prepared to reveal himself, but was stopped by Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Stop stop stop! They’re on our side. There’s no need for violence.”

“On our side?” Shi Chan’s eyes were full of confusion. Who is on whose side?

Trusting in Shi Chan’s character, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou decided to divulge some of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s inside information.

“Actually, it’s like this. The Heavenly Court Creed was established by us...” The two patiently explained how they had fabricated the Heavenly Court Creed and how they had deceived the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

After listening, Shi Chan fell silent for a long, long time.

No wonder Shifu often said that disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect are crafty and full of tricks, and that one must be careful when dealing with them.

I didn’t pay it much mind then, but now I know Shifu was right.

The ancient Heavenly Court, which has been all the buzz, is actually fabricated by Senior Brother Lu.

If word of this gets out, I can’t imagine the uproar and waves it’ll cause.

“Many thanks for your trust, senior brothers.”

Since Little Cui was the Chunjiang Branch Leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, she somewhat counted as someone on their side, making it inconvenient to act against her. The trio had no choice but to return to Xu An’s room and continue to pretend they were asleep to avoid any incidents.

The three had just feigned sleep when another graceful figure slipped into the room. Seeing the trio lying unconscious, she breathed a sigh of relief.

It was Little Zhu, one of the maidservants.

“As expected of Little Cui-jiejie. The efficacy of her knockout incense is excellent.

“What a pity. Although my cultivation is on par with Little Cui-jiejie’s, she is a branch leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. I can’t contend with her on human turf.

“But it’s not a big problem. She can only absorb yang energy; she can’t truly engage in bedroom affairs with Savior. The most she can do is to enjoy it in dreams, which isn’t as comfortable as it is for me.

“Originally, I planned for tomorrow night. But since Savior consumed the lingzhi and his yang energy is currently abundant, there’s no harm in me enjoying it as well.”

As Little Zhu spoke, she undressed, revealing a fluffy white fox tail and ears, and pressed herself against Xu An.

Lu Yang’s trio, “...”

“What should we do? Should we intervene?”

“It seems the lingzhi that Xu An ate in the day isn’t wasted. His yang energy is still quite abundant.”

“And she doesn’t seem to have any malicious intentions.”

After the amorous session, Little Zhu left, thoroughly satisfied.

The three were just about to get up when they heard the door being pushed open again. A third graceful figure entered the room, appearing timid and shy.

It was Little Qiu, one of the maidservants.

Like Little Cui, Little Qiu confirmed the knockout incense’s effect and breathed a sigh of relief upon seeing the three lying unconscious.

She lay on top of Xu An, clumsily sucking his yang energy and murmuring into his ear. “Master, Little Qiu likes you.”

The three secretly communicated via their spiritual consciousness.

“I can tell this is an artifact spirit. Can either of you discern her true form?”

“This poor monk’s eyesight is limited; I can’t identify it.”

“It’s a jade pendant crafted by a Nascent Soul artifact-refiner, and it’s a magical treasure that can be upgraded.” Although Lu Yang’s eyesight was on par with Meng Jingzhou’s, he had an immortal’s assistance.

“I remember Xu An mentioned his parents were ordinary Qi Training cultivators. A magical treasure with an artifact spirit doesn’t seem like something Qi Training cultivators could obtain.”

Magical treasures with artifact spirits were rare. The most top-tier one Lu Yang had seen involved refining a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s soul into a magical treasure.

Little Qiu’s origin wasn’t that exaggerated, but an artifact spirit like her still wasn’t something a Qi Training cultivator could acquire.

“Maybe his parents chanced upon it from somewhere, like the black market we visited. They bought it without knowing what treasure it was and left it to Xu An as an inheritance. Since Xu An wore it for a long time, the pendant instinctively absorbed his yang energy or vitality, and then it got activated.”

This would explain why Little Qiu’s attitude toward Xu An was so intimate.

Just as Little Qiu was intoxicated in sucking Xu An’s yang energy, the other two graceful figures returned.

It was Little Cui and Little Zhu. Thinking today’s opportunity was hard to come by, they figured they should enjoy themselves once more, and that was when they bumped into each other at the door.

“Little Qiu, what are you doing here? You are a cultivator?”

Little Qiu panicked instantly.

Little Cui and Little Zhu were astonished. They knew about each other, but they didn’t know that Little Qiu wasn’t human either.

“Wait, you’re an artifact spirit. Could you be the jade pendant Savior lost?”

They recalled their savior mentioning that his parents had left him a jade pendant. To express his longing for them, he poured his feelings into that keepsake, wearing the jade pendant day and night.

But one day, for some unknown reason, the jade pendant had inexplicably disappeared. No matter how he searched, he couldn’t find it, which brought him immense distress.

So the pendant was here.

They weren’t aware in the past, but now that Little Qiu was absorbing yang energy, her true form was revealed.

Little Qiu nodded awkwardly, confirming the two sisters’ guess, and moved away from Xu An.

Little Cui gnashed her teeth. “I wondered why Savior was still frail even though I was mindful of how much yang energy I absorbed. So it was because of you!” Worried that her savior wouldn’t recover, she had only dared to sneak here once every four days.

None of the three would yield; each wanted to continue doing the deed with Xu An. Their auras clashed, and Xu An unconsciously let out a moan, which frightened the three into stopping.

The three maidservants could only leave in disappointment, abandoning their plans to proceed with bedroom affairs.

Just as they stepped out of the room, they saw Liu Xiangyu standing in her courtyard, her beautiful face contorted with anger.

“You...you all...so none of you are human!” Liu Xiangyu spoke through gritted teeth.

Seeing her husband grow haggard these days, she had assumed it was because she had been too vigorous and disrupted his yin-yang balance, draining him. That was why she had reduced their bedroom affairs.

As for her husband’s talk of ghosts, while she pretended to be afraid on the surface, she was calm inwardly, knowing it was impossible.

As an almighty Nascent Soul snake demon, how could there be other ghosts absorbing my hubby’s yang energy right under my nose?

I never would have imagined there actually are!

Little Cui is a Nascent Soul ghost!

Little Zhu is a Nascent Soul fox demon!

Little Qiu is a magical treasure artifact spirit!

If not for their auras clashing earlier, I truly wouldn’t have realized.

She had always believed her husband’s weakness to be her fault. A few days ago, she met a mysterious person selling yang-boosting blood in the black market. She bought a drop and diluted it in the lingzhi soup, planning to enjoy herself tonight.

As for Lu Yang’s trio, it didn’t matter as long as they were kept unconscious.

Who would have thought that before I even stepped into the room, I’d sense the three maidservants competing in my hubby’s room?

So the yang-boosting blood I spent a fortune on was for you three to use?!

The three maidservants had long known Liu Xiangyu’s true form. After all, Liu Xiangyu had focused all her attention on hiding her identity from Xu An, not expecting that the three maidservants were also secretly watching her.

“Mi-Mistress, let me explain,” Little Qiu, the most timid of them all, tried to defend herself.

Liu Xiangyu tossed a Soundproofing Array around Xu An’s room and set up another array isolating the Xu Estate from the outside world. Her tone was emanating iciness.

“Spare me the talk. According to the rules of the cultivation world, the one with the bigger fist gets the final say. Today, I’ll make you understand the consequences for maidservants who secretly dare to covet a man who isn’t theirs!”

Little Cui was not afraid. As an almighty branch leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, the largest underground force in Chunjiang City, why would I fear an outsider snake demon like Liu Xiangyu?

“I’m indebted to Xu An. I won’t leave him!”

Little Zhu’s stance was also resolute. “An ancestor of Xu An saved my life. Such great favor cannot be repaid; I can only repay his descendant after achieving human form!”

Although Little Qiu was timid, she was firm when it came to matters involving Xu An. “Master awakened me. I’ll belong to Master for my whole life!”

In the courtyard, four Nascent Soul cultivators stood their ground, unwilling to yield. A great battle at the Nascent Soul Stage was about to erupt at any moment.

The three pretending to be asleep were also encountering such a situation for the first time and were momentarily at a loss for ideas.

“What should we do?” Lu Yang asked the other two for their opinions.

Meng Jingzhou clenched his teeth so hard that sparks almost flew. “Let’s get rid of Xu An first!”

Chapter 668: Suppressing the Snake Demon With the Pagoda

Meng Jingzhou felt that he hadn’t encountered a single good thing ever since he started selling his blood.

First, there was Shi Chan testing his Chan heart in the brothel, and now, there is Xu An’s harem in turmoil.

The key point is that both of them had used my blood!

No wonder I had sensed a bloody smell from the lingzhi soup Liu Xiangyu brought over. So it’s because it was my own blood!

What to do when one’s harem is on fire? Eliminate the root cause and culprit, and everything will be resolved.

Or I could spare Xu An’s life and just deliver a set of the Single’s Curse Fist.

In the courtyard, the snake demon, the ghost cultivator, the fox demon, and the artifact spirit were locked in a chaotic brawl. Fortunately, the array temporarily concealed the situation here; otherwise, the patrolling constables would have come to investigate long ago.

Liu Xiangyu transformed into a white snake that was dozens of zhang long and thicker than a water vat. It hissed, flicking its forked tongue while its cold pupils fixed on the three maidservants.

“My husband and I felt we had known each other for a long time upon our first meeting. We pledged our lives to each other in the spring rain of Qingming. How dare you demons and ghosts come between us!”

The snake writhed, shaking the earth. Cracks appeared in the ground as it opened its gaping maw, intending to swallow the three maidservants whole.

Little Cui spread her arms. Countless shadowy black ghosts merged with the darkness, their forms indistinct. Her nascent soul even left her body to block the white snake’s ferocious mouth.

“So what if you felt like you had known each other for a long time upon your first meeting? Love without life-and-death trials is empty talk!

“That day, my identity was exposed, and I was pursued by the authorities. Fortunately, I met Savior, allowing me to use his Vast Righteous Qi to conceal my form. That was how I survived!

“If not for my special identity and the risk of affecting his imperial examinations had I told him the truth, I would have married him long ago. How could it be your turn to become his legitimate wife!”

Little Zhu revealed her true demon form—a snow-white fox. It was like a spirit in the snow, nimble and agile.

“Snow, come!”

Suddenly, flurries of snow blanketed the courtyard. The temperature plummeted, breaths turned to frosty mist, and water droplets froze instantly.

“I am a snow fox who gained intelligence and became a demon spirit. Over a hundred years ago, an ancestor of Savior saved me from an animal trap. I accidentally stumbled into a forbidden area, consumed an unknown fruit, and awakened an ancient bloodline. Using the power inherited within that bloodline, I cultivated a human form.

“I originally intended to find Savior’s ancestor to repay him after assuming human form. But by the time I arrived, he had long since turned to dust. Since that was the case, I decided to repay the favor to Savior instead!

“If not for worrying that Savior couldn’t accept my identity, I would have confessed to him long ago!”

Liu Xiangyu sneered. “Each one of you sneaks in at night for a secret tryst and drains my husband’s energy, yet you still have excuses! I was the one who found out about the lingzhi, and I was the one who bought the pure yang blood. What did you three do?!

“If not for the three of you appearing together tonight, I wouldn’t have known that none of you are human! And you even made my husband invite three Golden Core cultivators from outside!”

The white snake whipped up a fierce gale. The icy wind was bone-piercing as it roared, causing one to shiver.

Little Qiu deployed a barrier, temporarily blocking Liu Xiangyu’s attack. Her true form was the jade pendant, a defensive-type magical treasure.

“Mistress, please quell your anger. Master awakened me, but I didn’t know how to face him, which is why I haven’t been able to find a chance to reveal my identity. I didn’t deliberately conceal it.”

Just as a second round of battle seemed like it would erupt at any moment, a Buddhist sound startled the four women, and they stopped simultaneously.

“Amitabha. Four benefactresses, could you please give this poor monk face and cease attacking?”

Shi Chan walked into the courtyard, followed by his protectors, one holding a sword and the other clenching his fist.

“You three are awake? Wait, you were never unconscious?!”

The expressions of Liu Xiangyu and the other three shifted, somewhat stricken with panic. None of them had realized that the three men their savior had invited had been awake all this time.

“This...this shouldn’t be! The knockout incense I used would have made an unprepared Basic Nascent Soul cultivator unconscious for six hours!” Little Cui reacted most strongly; she knew how potent her knockout incense was. It’s definitely not something Golden Core cultivators can resist.

More importantly, these three now know our true identities!

What should we do if Savior finds out?

“You were pretending to be asleep all along!”

The four women’s cheeks flushed with shame. Did that mean the three men had witnessed everything we did with Xu An in bed tonight?

In a rage, the four women attacked simultaneously.

The white snake rolled and thrashed, the night parade of a hundred ghosts appeared, the snow fox summoned snowfall, and the jade pendant manifested its power.

“This poor monk has no intention of provoking conflict.”

Despite facing the combined assault of the four women, Shi Chan remained unruffled. He retrieved a nine-story pagoda and tossed it into the air. The pagoda emitted a pale golden light that enveloped the four women, rendering them immobile.

“Wh-what kind of magical treasure is this?”

The four women were astounded. They had never seen such a divine treasure. Little Qiu, the jade pendant, found the suppression from this superior treasure even more strongly.

“Four benefactresses, you can’t defeat the three of us.” Shi Chan sighed and withdrew the suppression.

A golden Dharma Body materialized behind him. In its left hand was a vajra scepter, and in its right hand was a dharma wheel—it was the most orthodox Sixteen-Foot Golden Body.

The Qingfeng Sword in Lu Yang’s hand gleamed with a cold light. Merely looking at it felt like a thousand needles were pricking one’s eyes. Its sword qi was so sharp that none dared to gaze upon it directly.

Meng Jingzhou executed Three Heads Six Arms. His six brawny arms were poised to strike, capable of punching the sky and splitting the earth. His three faces were malevolent-looking, his eyes glowering in wrath.

“Nascent Soul... No, wait, Divine Transfiguration Stage?!”

The faces of Liu Xiangyu and the three maidservants turned pale instantly. Although these three men’s cultivation seems similar to ours, the aura they display clearly shows the might of the Divine Transfiguration Stage! Even without the nine-story pagoda, any one of them could subdue us single-handedly!

Aren’t there only two Divine Transfiguration cultivators in Chunjiang City, with both from the authorities? Where did hubby find three Divine Transfiguration cultivators?

Seeing that the four women had become docile, Shi Chan retracted his Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, while Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou also withdrew their techniques.

“This poor monk was entrusted by Benefactor Xu to resolve the matter of his yang energy deficiency. Please do not make things difficult for me, four benefactresses.”

The four women naturally agreed, becoming extremely well-behaved.

Liu Xiangyu returned to human form and invited the trio to the main hall for a chat.

“Before discussing matters, allow this poor monk to introduce himself. My dharma name is Shi Chan, and I am a disciple of the Hanging Monastery.”

The four women’s expressions changed again, and they grew tense. To think he’s an accomplished monk from the Hanging Monastery.

The Hanging Monastery hardly had any disciples, and rumors about them were scarce. To the outside world, the Hanging Monastery was absolutely mysterious. The four women couldn’t gauge Shi Chan’s attitude.

Little Cui was the most anxious. I’m a branch leader of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed. If my identity is exposed, I’m afraid I can’t even escape.

“Benefactress Liu, if this poor monk is correct, you are from the White Snake Tribe of the Demon Region?”

“You are truly discerning, Master.”

“Benefactress Liu, listen to this poor monk’s advice. Your relationship with Benefactor Xu is really inappropriate.”

Liu Xiangyu’s face turned deathly pale, a sense of foreboding washing over her. “Master, are you saying that my husband and I are of different races and that we ultimately cannot be together?”

Shi Chan shook his head. “It is not so. This poor monk means that your race needs to be verified when registering your marriage. Benefactor Xu is unaware of your identity, indicating that the two of you are only husband and wife in name.

“This poor monk suggests that you two go to the municipal office to register.”

Chapter 669: Senior Brother Lu Yang’s Words Are Not Wrong

Liu Xiangyu didn’t dare to tell Xu An her true identity, so the two had never registered their marriage.

Xu An wasn’t someone particular about formalities. If his wife was unwilling, so be it; it didn’t matter to him.

Upon hearing this, the three maidservants’ eyes lit up.

All along, Xu An and Liu Xiangyu had addressed each other as husband and wife. The three maidservants hadn’t expected the couple to have never officially registered.

That’s right. To register a marriage with the authorities, at the very least, both parties’ identities must be verified. Savior doesn’t know Liu Xiangyu is a snake demon, which means they haven’t registered their marriage.

Then what kind of legitimate wife are you?

Since you, Liu Xiangyu, haven’t gone to register, doesn’t that mean we’re all standing on the same starting line?

Master is truly a master—he’s able to see the details we had overlooked.

“As for the four of you taking turns engaging in relations with Benefactor Xu and causing his yang energy deficiency, that is beyond this poor monk’s ability. However, this senior brother of mine can solve your problem.”

Shi Chan solemnly introduced Meng Jingzhou.

“My elder brother here possesses yang-boosting blood. I believe Benefactress Liu isn’t unfamiliar with it.

“Benefactor Xu is a mortal. A single drop of yang-boosting blood must be diluted thousands of times before consumption. From a long-term perspective, this poor monk suggests the four of you purchase a few drops of yang-boosting blood.”

Meng Jingzhou kept a deadpan face as he retrieved several small bottles containing his yang-boosting blood.

“One hundred thousand spirit stones per drop.” He jacked up the price on the spot.

After the hot sales at the black market, Meng Jingzhou realized he had been selling it too cheaply.

This is the blood of the strongest Single’s Spirit Root cultivator in history, with effects like boosting yang and nourishing the kidney, prolonging one’s lifespan, rendering one impervious to a hundred poisons, enhancing the memory, and improving one’s constitution. It is a treasure that can’t be bought with spirit stones alone. Is one hundred thousand spirit stones per drop expensive? Not at all.

“I’ll buy five drops!” Liu Xiangyu went all out. These three maidservants are seeing an opportunity and are bent on vying with me for the position of legitimate wife.

If I lose my status as the legitimate wife, I’ll have to compete with the three maidservants for bedroom affairs in the future. Whoever buys more blood today will have more confidence and leverage in future disputes.

“I’ll buy six drops!” Little Cui shouted. She was the wealthiest among the four women. The barbeque business is booming, and as the shop manager, I’ve received a substantial cut of the profits.

“I-I’ll buy three drops.” Little Zhu lacked confidence. She came from an unorthodox background and didn’t have enough spirit stones.

As for Little Qiu, she was even more miserable. She was just an artifact spirit and didn’t even have a single spirit stone.

Meng Jingzhou left behind fourteen vials and kept the rest, accepting one million four hundred spirit stones in passing.

Tch. Earning spirit stones like this doesn’t give me any sense of accomplishment.

“Then this poor monk will return to Benefactor Xu’s room with my two elder brothers and wait for dawn. Four benefactresses, please clean up traces of the battle in the courtyard.”

Little Zhu had summoned a snowstorm, and the courtyard was still freezing enough to make one shiver.

A few hours later, Xu An woke up feeling quite well. “Masters, did you gain anything last night? I feel much more energetic getting up today.”

Meng Jingzhou remarked inwardly, Yeah, man. If you hadn’t drunk my yang-boosting blood, after your activities with a ghost, a demon, and an artifact spirit last night, you’d be too weak to even get out of bed today.

“Amitabha. We had some gains last night. The problem has been resolved. You will no longer suffer from yang energy deficiency in the future, Benefactor.”

Xu An was overjoyed. The experts Big Brother Zhong Ming recommended are truly impressive. “You have worked hard, masters. As for the fee...”

“Five hundred taels of silver will suffice.”

Xu An was startled, not because it was expensive, but because the price was far too cheap.

I’ve sought out so many experts without success. In contrast, the masters resolved it in one night, yet they’re only asking for five hundred taels of silver? As he had his parents’ inheritance, five hundred taels of silver was nothing.

“Then what exactly was the cause for my constant lack of energy?”

“You will naturally know when destiny arrives.”

“Ah, oh.” Xu An thought, This master is being cryptic and mysterious.

He straightened his clothes, planning to have breakfast and continue studying the classics from the sages. The moment he stepped out of his room, he saw his wife and the three maidservants standing at the gate.

The four said in unison, “Hubby/Savior/Master, actually, I’ve been keeping a secret from you. Actually, I am a snake demon/ghost cultivator/fox demon/artifact spirit.”

The four women each revealed their true forms: a several-zhang-long white snake, a ghost cultivator surrounded by chilling yin-winds, a fluffy fox, and an artifact spirit whose form morphed into the phantom of a jade pendant.

Xu An’s eyes rolled back, and he fainted on the spot.

Lu Yang sighed. His courage is really a no go. But the subsequent matters have nothing to do with us anymore.

The trio took advantage of the sparse morning crowds to return to the inn.

A pair of eyes hidden in the shadows silently watched the three figures disappear into the inn, then turned to instruct the subordinates. “Inform His Excellency that they have returned to the inn. We can act now.”

After all the ups and downs last night, even the trio felt exhausted, and they needed proper rest.

About one hour later, a knock came from Lu Yang’s door.

“Is anyone in?”

Lu Yang had been sitting cross-legged. He opened his eyes, still somewhat listless and not fully rested.

Who’s looking for me?

Using his spiritual consciousness, he detected many people standing in the hallway. Judging by their clothing, they were from the authorities.

Lu Yang got up and opened the door. A somewhat portly middle-aged man stood outside.

Upon seeing Lu Yang, the portly man’s face broke into an enthusiastic smile. “You must be Lu Yang, Nephew Lu from the Dao-Seeking Sect, right? Allow me to introduce myself. My surname is Liu. I am the city lord of Chunjiang City.”

Lu Yang was stunned. Why does the city lord know I’m here?

He immediately realized. When I was showing off and keeping up lofty airs in front of Boss Hong, I had announced my name! Boss Hong must have revealed it during the interrogation!

Damn it! I was too focused on showing off at the time and didn’t think about the consequences.

City Lord Liu also summoned Meng Jingzhou and Shi Chan from next door, inviting them both to Lu Yang’s room.

City Lord Liu said amiably, “You three nephews came to Chunjiang City without even a greeting. You’re really standing on ceremony. May I ask if the three of you are in Chunjiang City on a mission for your immortal sects?”

“Amitabha. This poor monk and the others came to Chunjiang City for some personal matters.”

Hearing it was personal matters, City Lord Liu’s smile grew wider. “If you three nephews don’t mind, how about coming to my estate for a simple meal tonight?”

Personal matters? That’s even better! I’ll help you resolve them quickly so you can leave quickly.

Lu Yang suddenly spoke up. “Originally, it was for personal matters. But we happened to discover clues about a diabolic creed here in Chunjiang City.”

Hearing it was related to diabolic creeds, City Lord Liu visibly tensed. “Do you need me to send people to assist?”

Lu Yang shook his head, declining the offer. He stated solemnly, “We are investigating in private. If the authorities also act, the situation will become complicated and may alert the enemy.

“Based on current leads, we found traces of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed operating in Chunjiang City, and this has been going on for some time.
