Our initial assessment is that the leader is a ghost cultivator who enjoys absorbing the yang energy of men. One man has already fallen victim. Fortunately, we arrived in time, and he survived.

“We also discovered that the ghost cultivator was involved in a chaotic battle between four Nascent Soul cultivators. The various parties tussled and were unwilling to yield, making the situation extremely complex.”

“Senior Brother Shi Chan, is that correct?”

“Amitabha. Monks do not speak of falsehood. Senior Brother Lu’s words are not wrong.”

Chapter 670: Unforeseen Circumstances

Before coming, City Lord Liu had already inquired about the identities of the immortal sect disciples visiting Chunjiang City.

Among them, the most notable is this Lu Yang.

A disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the most popular character in the storytelling performances, and likely the future sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Since he is the fourth disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the probability that he’s telling the truth should be assigned a question mark.

Hence, when Lu Yang claimed they had found clues about a diabolic creed in Chunjiang City, City Lord Liu was skeptical.

But after Shi Chan confirmed it, he believed Lu Yang’s words.

Shi Chan is an almighty disciple of the Hanging Monastery, a pure and proper monk; he wouldn’t lie.

“In that case, I must trouble Nephew Lu to continue investigating the diabolic creed in our city. After all, this concerns the safety of the city’s million inhabitants. If you three nephews need anything, please raise it. I will do my best to satisfy your requests.”

Confirming that Lu Yang’s trio had genuinely found leads about a diabolic creed in Chunjiang City and that it involved four Nascent Soul cultivators, he had to take this matter seriously.

One slip-up could cause major casualties, and whether I could remain city lord would be up in the air.

“You’re too polite, City Lord Liu,” Lu Yang said righteously, as solemn as a general rushing to the battlefield. “Eradicating evil and upholding the Dao is our duty. How can it be called ‘trouble?’”

Meng Jingzhou also chimed in. He clenched his fists forcefully, his eyes flickering with righteous brilliance. “Rest assured, City Lord Liu. With the three of us senior and junior brothers here, the diabolic creed will not stir any waves!”

Witnessing this, City Lord Liu inwardly sighed in admiration. They’re truly young talents!

Shi Chan kept replaying Lu Yang’s earlier words in his mind.

Every word Senior Brother Lu Yang said is true; it indeed doesn’t constitute ‘falsehood.’ Yet, why do I feel like it’s somewhat inconsistent with the objective facts?

“Never mind. Since you three nephews still need to track down the diabolic creed, I shall not disturb you further. I must return to prepare for receiving an important personage.”

“An important personage?”

“One-Qi Venerable Lord of the Qi-Commanding Sect. The Dark Night Pavilion members will be sent to the imperial city at noon today. The provincial governor was worried about unforeseen circumstances and specifically invited One-Qi Venerable Lord to escort them.”

Lu Yang nodded in understanding.

He had seen the One-Qi Venerable Lord at the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th year celebration. The One-Qi Venerable Lord was one of the Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors invited—a bona fide seasoned expert. A half-baked Transcendent Tribulation cultivator like Lu Baqian couldn’t compare at all.

Lu Yang’s trio saw City Lord Liu off.

Returning to the second floor of the inn, they saw Fuling and Kongque cautiously peeking out.

“Are they all gone?” The two sisters had never seen a big shot like the city lord before; hearing he had come nearly scared them to death.

“They’re all gone,” Shi Chan replied.

“Young heroes, just who are you three...” Even if they’re Nascent Soul cultivators, it shouldn’t warrant a personal visit from the city lord, right?

“Immortal sect disciples.”

“Immortal sect disciples?!” the sisters exclaimed, their beautiful eyes widening slightly. Only then did they remember that Lu Yang and his companions had helped them many times, yet they still didn’t know their names.

“This poor monk’s dharma name is Shi Chan. These two are my senior brothers, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.”

“The Lu Yang from Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Lu Yang? That Prodigy Lu who could challenge Divine Transfiguration cultivators while only at the Foundation Establishment Stage?!

“The Meng Jingzhou from Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Meng Jingzhou? That Eldest Young Master Meng who has a Dao heart of iron and remains unmoved even with beauties in his embrace?!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Although it’s the truth, why does it sound so strange?

And why are you two sisters reacting so strongly?

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou rarely listened to storytelling and didn’t know they were currently the most popular figures among the common folk.

To promote Meng Jingzhou, Chieftain Jin had even fabricated and embellished many stories about him. Examples were as follows:

The Holy Maiden Threw Herself Into His Arms, but Eldest Young Master Meng Remains Unmoved Even With Her in His Embrace

Eldest Young Master Meng Was Accidentally Poisoned by a Lascivious Jiao-Dragon and Endured the Lust Poison Through Sheer Willpower—Unprecedented in History

When Meng Jingzhou Travels, All Ghosts Retreat

Someone Plagued by Ghosts in Their Dreams Received Advice From an Expert and Hung a Picture of Meng Jingzhou Capturing Ghosts on Their Wall, and From Then On, the Ghostly Disturbances in Their Dreams Ceased

Meng Jingzhou Eats Three Little Ghosts Every Day

The list went on.

After hearing his own legends, Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened. What kind of nonsense is this?

In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy let out a soft sound of surprise and poked Lu Yang’s back. “Ask these two girls who they’ve met.”

“Is something the matter?”

“Someone left a dreamscape mark on them, and that person’s cultivation isn’t low. It feels like they harbor malicious intentions.”

Lu Yang was taken aback. This doesn’t sound good.

He hurriedly asked, “Did you two encounter any strange people or strange things today?”

The two sisters were puzzled. Why is Young Hero Lu suddenly asking this?

“Now that you mention it, on our way back after the business negotiation, there was indeed a person who walked toward us, acting mysteriously and saying he hoped we’d have a sweet dream.”

“What did that person look like?”

“Tall and thin, like a bamboo pole.”

~~~

“Venerable Lord, everyone is here.”

City Lord Liu brought out all the Dark Night Pavilion members from the dungeon. They wore shackles that sealed their spirit energy and were guarded day and night by several Fusion cultivators to ensure no accidents.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord nodded steadily. He swept his gaze over Ye Xiao and the others, causing their scalps to tingle.

Having a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator escort us? You think too highly of us.

City Lord Liu ordered his subordinates to load them into the prison cages and seal them with paper strips.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord nodded. “Let’s go.”

Suddenly, an ethereal and sinister voice came from the air. “Hehe, taking away the people I’ve set my sights on won’t be that easy.”

“Who’s there?!”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord extended his spiritual consciousness, scanning every inch of his surroundings.

A tall and slender black figure emerged from the void, looking at the One-Qi Venerable Lord with an ambiguous smile.

“Transcendent Tribulation cultivator of Great Xia, stay here.”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord abruptly waved his hand, sending City Lord Liu and the others flying. “Leave this place quickly!” This person knows who I am, yet he dared to act; he’s clearly come prepared!

“Leave?” The black figure sneered.

An invisible force spread throughout the city.

“I’d like to see which of you can leave this place.”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord instantly grew wary. Suddenly, his vision swam. Before he could react, the scenery before his eyes changed.

It was still Chunjiang City, but all the colors had faded.

~~~

Outside the city, travelers about to enter Chunjiang City watched with their eyes wide and mouths agape as the city vanished into thin air, leaving behind a massive crater.

~~~

“Where is this place?!” The One-Qi Venerable Lord was on high alert, still not understanding what had happened.

Everyone, be it City Lord Liu or the Dark Night Pavilion members, was all here; they hadn’t even moved. But here, everything, be it people or objects, was dull, as if they had been bleached of color.

The black figure spread his arms. “Transcendent Tribulation cultivator of Great Xia, welcome to my world. I call it the Void Realm!”

Hearing the words “Void Realm,” the One-Qi Venerable Lord recalled a piece of historical knowledge and immediately figured things out. He summoned his life-bound magical treasure. “The power of an Incipient Dao Fruit—you are a half-immortal!”

Chapter 671: Void Emptiness Supreme Lord

“So, what exactly has happened?”

In the inn, Lu Yang and his two companions looked at each other in confusion. In the blink of an eye, the colors in their surroundings had darkened. Pushing open the window, they realized it was also the case for the streets outside.

Lu Yang extended his spiritual consciousness to observe the surrounding objects. He didn’t detect any changes in either material or density. The color changes only informed them that some unknown event had occurred here.

“Immortal Fairy, do you know what’s going on?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy carefully sensed their surroundings. “Hmm, all of you have probably been pulled into another space. This is a space completely controlled by an individual. The entire city has been dragged into this space, severing all connections with the outside world.

“Those people left outside the city would probably see the original Chunjiang City vanish, leaving only a massive crater in the ground.

“It resembles the power of a certain Incipient Dao Fruit, but not one that appeared in ancient times. I haven’t seen it before.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why did another half-immortal pop up?

“Old Lu, what’s the situation? What did the immortal say?” Meng Jingzhou asked Lu Yang secretly.

“We’ve been caught up in something big.”

Suddenly, a power fluctuation came from the distance.

“It’s from the direction of the dungeon!” Lu Yang’s senses were the sharpest.

“Let’s go take a look.”

“Benefactresses, please remain here. We will return shortly.”

~~~

“Void Realm?” The One-Qi Venerable Lord stared fixedly at the shadowy figure while holding his precious gourd.

According to historical records, toward the end of the Great Yu era, the world was in turmoil, with various heroes and warlords vying for supremacy. Before the Jiang and Meng factions had fully risen, there was one major faction that was highly likely to win the empire.

That was the largest sect of the late Great Yu era—the Void Nothingness Sect. The founding ancestor was a half-immortal named the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

Unfortunately, the Void Nothingness Sect was no match for the Jiang and Meng ancestral clans, which jointly exterminated it, and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s whereabouts became unknown.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s Incipient Dao Fruit was called the Void Realm Incipient Dao Fruit. It could create a brand-new space, with the ability to forcibly pull people into this new space. As for what would happen after entering this space, it was not recorded in ancient texts.

This brand-new space was called “Void Realm.”

“You are the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord?”

The slender and tall black figure was slightly surprised. “Oh, I didn’t expect anyone to remember me. I don’t see any records about me in books available in the market. It seems your Great Xia higher-ups have some internal documents.”

Since someone had recognized his identity, the black figure no longer hid his true appearance. The black substance covering him peeled away layer by layer, revealing a handsome visage.

“Jiang Ping’an[1] established Great Xia with national fortune as its foundation. The national fortune is based on stability and strength. Nothing undermines stability more than establishing an assassin organization.”

Jiang Pin’an was the first Xia Emperor.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord sighed somewhat ruefully. “It’s a pity your Great Xia’s control is too strict; I couldn’t find a suitable assassin organization, forcing me to search among archaic cultivators, and I happened to find this Dark Night Pavilion.

“I can make use of this opportunity to take over the Dark Night Pavilion and eliminate you, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator of Great Xia!”

“Brazen words!” The One-Qi Venerable Lord opened his precious gourd. An endless stream of purple qi shot forth like a sash, sweeping toward the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

This was the Innate One Qi he had cultivated since childhood. When soft, it could form chains to bind people, and when hard, it could cleave mountains, part seas, and shatter space.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord leaped backward, evading the attack.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord felt somewhat regretful. This attack was merely a feint against the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord. The true goal was to shatter space, break the Void Realm, and escape. Unfortunately, the Void Realm lived up to being a product of an Incipient Dao Fruit—it couldn’t be broken by the Innate Purple Qi.

Sensing the Void Realm’s slight tremor, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord sneered coldly. “I didn’t expect the Innate Purple Qi to possess such power. Congealing and refining innate true qi and returning to simplicity—the cultivation method of the qi-training path is indeed extraordinary. It’s a pity the legacy will end here.”

If I hadn’t been careful, I might have been injured by the Innate Purple Qi.

He thought for a moment, then flicked his finger, breaking the shackles and cages confining the Dark Night Pavilion members. “Go kill as you please in the city and divert his attention.”

The Dark Night Pavilion members felt as if they were granted amnesty. Who would dare disobey orders from a half-immortal powerhouse? Moreover, those who joined an assassin organization enjoyed killing.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord flew into a rage. “How dare you! I hereby establish the rule: All members of the Dark Night Pavilion shall not move!”

The restraints he expected did not manifest. The Dark Night Pavilion members could move freely.

“Exterminate them!” City Lord Liu shouted.

The constables sprang into action. The civilians were like lambs to the slaughter against these assassins, utterly defenseless.

“Did I permit you to move?” the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord said lazily.

With a thought, a colossal black cage materialized, imprisoning City Lord Liu and the others.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord’s face was so dark that water could drip from it. He hadn’t seen how the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord created the black cage.

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy observed the battle, realization dawned upon her. “So that’s how it is. This place is that half-immortal’s home ground. Rules don’t work here. He can also create objects from the empty void by relying on his mind. This is his ability within the Void Realm.”

Lu Yang hastily transmitted an auditory message to One-Qi Venerable Lord. “Venerable Lord, rules are useless here. The opponent’s ability is likely creating objects from the empty void by relying on his mind. We’ll stop the people from the Dark Night Pavilion!”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord didn’t expect Lu Yang to be here.

Lu Yang’s trio boldly took action, intercepting the Dark Night Pavilion’s assassins.

“Three mere Nascent Soul cultivators, yet you dare to block our way!” The vice pavilion leader of the Dark Night Pavilion, Ye Xiao’s protector, sneered and extended a large hand.

Smack.

Another large hand appeared out of nowhere, blocking the vice pavilion leader.

“Leave this person to me!”

A figure flew out from the city. It was one of the three people who had ambushed the vice pavilion leader previously. After the successful ambush, the subsequent matters weren’t his responsibility, and he had been vacationing in Chunjiang City, not expecting to encounter this situation.

Although he was stronger than the vice pavilion leader, he wasn’t strong enough to decide the outcome immediately.

“They’re just three Nascent Soul cultivators. Attack together!” The Nascent Soul assassins of the Dark Night Pavilion didn’t take Lu Yang and his companions seriously.

A Sixteen-Foot Golden Body shot up from the ground and crushed a Nascent Soul assassin with one palm strike, leaving a pile of debris in its wake.

Meng Jingzhou executed Three Heads Six Arms, charging into the crowd of assassins and sweeping through them. An assassin tried to launch a sneak attack from behind but realized his dagger couldn’t even pierce Meng Jingzhou’s skin.

“Sword-Cleansing Pond, come!” Lu Yang commanded softly.

The Sword-Cleansing Pond flew out from his storage ring and directly crashed into a Nascent Soul assassin, killing him. Two swords shook off the pond water and flew to Lu Yang’s side like protectors.

“Clone!”

Lu Yang split off a wooden clone. Between the two, one wielded the Qingfeng Sword, while the other wielded the Mingyue Sword. The two swords combined, their sword qi plowing the ground and radiating resplendent brilliance, hacking the assassins into pieces.

The assassins who had survived for the time being were petrified. These three aren’t Nascent Soul cultivators at all!

1. “Ping’an” literally translates to “safe.” ☜

Chapter 672: Chunjiang City—Teeming With Hidden Dragons and Crouching Tigers

The civilians near the dungeon were scared out of their wits when they saw the assassins swarming out.

These assassins all possessed cultivation; killing the commoners would be as easy as flipping one’s hand!

But what these civilians didn’t know was that while they were afraid, the assassins were even more afraid.

Although the Dark Night Pavilion had many assassins, none were a match for Lu Yang’s trio. Even Nascent Soul assassins couldn’t withstand one move, much less the Golden Core, Foundation Establishment, and Qi Training assassins below them. A single strike could kill several assassins at once.

“Split up and run!”

The assassins were horrified. They liked killing people, but they didn’t like killing themselves. These three were simply not opponents they could handle.

Anyone with eyes could see that surviving this battle meant they could latch onto a half-immortal’s thigh to achieve a meteoric rise, commanding the winds and rain and getting whatever they wanted in the future. Their prospects would be boundless.

They absolutely couldn’t fall into these three’s hands!

“Trying to run?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a glance and acted simultaneously, circling the assassins.

“Draw Underground Prison!”

“Draw Ground as Prison!”

Before most assassins could react, they were trapped in cages—either above ground or below ground!

“What move is this?!”

The assassins panicked. The cage below ground was indestructible; daggers broke upon contact. The one above ground was not a cage but a luminous circle; no one could leave the circle’s range!

Some quick-witted assassins recognized they couldn’t win against Lu Yang and the others and fled early.

“Split up and chase!”

Shi Chan retracted his Sixteen-Foot Golden Body. His feet seemed to grow wings as he strode through the air, covering a hundred zhang with each step, almost like it was teleportation.

One of Buddhism’s Six Divine Abilities—Divine Foot Ability.

As a physique cultivator, Meng Jingzhou wasn’t known for flying speed, but relying on the explosive power of his legs, he was many times faster than flying.

He just couldn’t match Shi Chan’s speed.

“This won’t do. It’s still too slow.” Meng Jingzhou hesitated. I originally didn’t want to use this move, but lives are at stake here. It’s not the time to care about my image.

“Very well. I’ll let the world witness the might of the Double Infants Stage!” He withdrew his Three Heads Six Arms and fused his twin nascent souls again, growing six legs from his lower body.

I can’t perform the Six Divine Abilities, but I can grow six legs!

“Stop there, don’t run!” Meng Jingzhou targeted one assassin, all six legs propelling forward as he charged toward him.

The assassin glanced back, and his soul nearly left his body out of fright.

A six-legged monster was rapidly closing in. Then, a fist the size of a sandbag smashed toward him, killing him in one strike.

Meng Jingzhou was brimming with lethal intent. Any assassin who sees me in this form today, every single one of them shall not live to see another day!

Lu Yang controlled his clone to intercept the assassins while he piloted the Sword-Cleansing Pond, the Qingfeng and Mingyue swords flanking him like protectors as he moved.

The moment he spotted an assassin, the two swords would instantly fly forth and claim their heads, or he would simply ram them with the Sword-Cleansing Pond, crushing them into a bloody pulp.

~~~

An assassin realized escape was impossible if things continued like this; they had to find hostages.

He flew into a wealthy household. People living in such places were either rich or noble—perfect candidates for hostages.

“Don't move! I’ll kill whoever moves!” he threatened harshly. Bursting into the room, he stared fixedly at the master of the house.

Four pairs of eyes filled with killing intent stared back at him eerily.

“You dare threaten my hubby?”

Four figures surrounded the assassin, making him break out in a cold sweat. He could sense that each figure’s cultivation surpassed his own.

Before he could react, a massive snake tail swept across, smashing him until not a single bone remained intact, extinguishing his life instantly.

“What exactly is happening?” Liu Xiangyu’s brows were tightly knitted.

Everything had occurred too suddenly. They had no idea about the specifics in Chunjiang City, except that immense energy fluctuations were overhead, far beyond their cultivation levels. It was a battle they couldn’t interfere at all. A single energy wave could crush them countless times over.

“Little Qiu, you have defensive capabilities. Stay here and protect hubby. The three of us will go out to assess the situation and see if we can help.”

“Alright, Mistress.”

~~~

A smarter assassin chose a shop.

“Nobody moves!”

The assassin released the oppressive aura of the Basic Golden Core Stage, which was catastrophic for mortals. Based on experience, once he did so, mortals would tremble and couldn’t even stand.

But reality was completely different.

The shop attendants seemed unaffected by the oppressive pressure. They looked up simultaneously, staring at the assassin with odd expressions.

“Oh ho, you have quite the guts, don’t you? Daring to even threaten us!”

“Close the door. Don’t let him escape!”

“Damn it! Even running an honest business attracts assassins. It’s tough being an honest person.”

The assassin stumbled back two steps, a sense of foreboding seeping into his heart.

He turned to flee, but the shop’s door slammed shut by itself, fitting tightly. No one could see the situation inside through the cracks.

“Help...”

“Gag him!”

Bang!

The assassin burst the door open. He lay on the ground, crawling out arduously.

The shop’s interior was pitch black. Countless hands reached out from the darkness, grabbing the assassin’s ankles and dragging him back in.

The assassin desperately scraped the ground with his nails, yet he could only leave white scratches.

The door closed again, and after that, there was no more noise.

Perhaps the door was shut too forcefully; the signboard reading “One More Time Barbeque Shop: Chunjiang City Branch” swayed twice.

~~~

There were also beggars who suddenly turned violent, grappling with the assassins.

Witnessing such a scene, Lu Yang recalled what Yun Zhi had once said. Real beggars were rare nowadays; the ones seen nowadays were cultivators training in the mundane realm.

Although these cultivators weren’t as powerful as Lu Yang and the others, they were more than enough to deal with the assassins.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord laughed heartily upon seeing Lu Yang’s trio rout the assassins until they pissed their pants. “This is the assassin organization you wanted to preserve?”

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was a major figure who had experienced the struggle for dominion in the late Great Yu era; such matters wouldn’t disrupt his mental state.

Without a word, he conjured countless magical treasures out of thin air: sabers, spears, swords, halberds, precious cauldrons, divine pagodas, jade vases, cattail-leaf fans—all at the Transcendent Tribulation level.

The Void Realm was his home ground. He could create anything below the level of immortals. If he attained an immortal Dao Fruit, he could even turn illusion into reality, making the Void Realm a brand new world—not a small world like a cave domain, but an enormous cosmic world.

At that time, he would be the bona fide leader of that world.

The Transcendent Tribulation-grade treasures fell like rain, but were all blocked by the purple qi that stretched thirty thousand li. The Innate Purple Qi was riddled with holes after this onslaught of attacks.

“I’d like to see how many attacks your purple qi can block.”

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord conjured another batch of numerous Transcendent Tribulation magical treasures suspended in the air. He hurled them toward City Lord Liu and the others, forcing the One-Qi Venerable Lord to bear the brunt of the attacks.

He had imprisoned City Lord Liu and the others instead of killing them precisely for the aim of tying down the One-Qi Venerable Lord!

“Void Emptiness Supreme Lord!” the One-Qi Venerable Lord bellowed in rage.

“What, you want to beg for mercy...” The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord sneered, but before he could finish, a boundless force sucked him into a gourd.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord hurriedly covered the gourd’s opening.

The precious gourd had a purple base adorned with golden patterns. If one answered when their name was called, they could be sucked inside.

This was the Purple-Gold Gourd.

Chapter 673: Buddhist Prayer Beads

“So the Purple-Gold Gourd is Senior One-Qi’s magical treasure.” Everyone in Chunjiang City looked up at the battle and awaited its outcome; Lu Yang was no exception.

He had only heard Yun Zhi mention the name Purple-Gold Gourd. It contained dual energies of yin and yang. Anyone sucked inside would be torn apart by the two energies in mere moments.

But he didn’t know who possessed this magical treasure.

Previously, at a stall in the black market, he had seen a magical treasure claimed to be the Purple-Gold Gourd, but he could recognize it was a fake at a glance. Even selling the entire black market wouldn’t cover the cost of the real Purple-Gold Gourd’s stopper.

“That’s it? We won?” Lu Yang felt the battle had ended surprisingly quickly.

“You think a half-immortal is so easy to defeat? This guy’s Incipient Dao Fruit can create objects from thin air. Even if he is trapped inside the gourd, he can still use that ability.

“Don’t underestimate any half-immortal. His ability might not be significant in the outside world, but once he’s in the Void Realm, few half-immortals can beat him.”

“That strong?”

Lu Yang was taken aback. Doesn’t that mean the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord hasn’t even gotten serious yet?

Sure enough, just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had predicted, the Purple-Gold Gourd shook violently. No matter how the One-Qi Venerable Lord tried to suppress it with spells, he couldn’t stop the shaking.

Bang!

The gourd’s stopper was forced open by an endless stream of magical treasures, and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord escaped successfully.

“Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, looks like you aren’t completely useless.”

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was jet black, protected by countless layers of armor. The armor was scarred and battered, clearly damaged by the yin-yang dual energies.

Layer by layer, the armor fell away, while the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord himself was completely unharmed.

~~~

“Senior brothers, I sense that the protective prayer beads I gave Benefactress Kongque have been activated; she’s in danger. I’m going to check.” Shi Chan transmitted an auditory message, startling Lu Yang.

“Be careful! We haven’t seen Ye Xiao at all; he has likely gone to kill Miss Kongque. Old Meng and I will head over there too!”

~~~

Lu Yang’s guess hit the mark. After Ye Xiao broke free, the first thing he did was to rush to the inn and kill Miss Kongque.

I’ve said that whoever I set my sights on must either submit to me or die!

I keep my word.

“Huff, huff... Who gave you this magical treasure?” Ye Xiao was panting heavily. Kongque was right in front of him, but no matter what method he used, it was blocked by the prayer beads in front of her chest.

The creator of this magical treasure must be an extremely powerful existence—no weaker than myself!

“You don’t need to know!” Seeing that Ye Xiao couldn’t harm her, Kongque breathed a sigh of relief, grateful for the magical treasure Shi Chan had gifted her. I could never afford a magical treasure that can block attacks of the Nascent Soul Stage for a quarter of an hour.

“Since I can’t deal with you for now, this younger or elder twin sister beside you is in danger!” Ye Xiao revealed a cruel smile. He could already imagine Kongque’s twisted and grief-stricken expression after he killed Fuling.

“Younger Sister, run!” Kongque hastily yelled. She stood before Fuling to shield her from Ye Xiao’s attack.

However, her reaction speed was far slower than Ye Xiao’s. He only needed to circle one round, and she could no longer protect Fuling.

Ye Xiao transformed into a shadow, appearing behind Fuling. She was wide open, the veins on her neck clearly visible.

Success!

A giant golden hand abruptly appeared between Ye Xiao and Fuling, blocking the fatal blow.

“Benefactor, your heart is consumed by killing intent.”

With his strike foiled, Ye Xiao hastily retreated. This person’s cultivation isn’t low—facing him head-on might be disadvantageous. As an assassin, I’m skilled in ambush; frontal assault isn’t my forte.

“Master Shi Chan!”

The sisters were overwhelmed with emotions upon seeing Shi Chan’s arrival, as if they had seen a beacon of hope.

“Little monk, you’re the one who gave Kongque the prayer beads!” Ye Xiao regarded Shi Chan as a mortal enemy.

Without the prayer beads, I would have succeeded long ago!

“Amitabha. You have good eyes, Benefactor. This poor monk had an epiphany during the Advanced Golden Core Stage and refined the sandalwood prayer beads with vow power.”

“Nonsense! That’s impossible!” Ye Xiao was enraged. If you had refined this magical treasure at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, how could it have blocked my Basic Nascent Soul attacks?

“Quell your anger, Benefactor. Monks do not speak of falsehood. Ever since I began my journey, I have only experienced one defeat. Losing to this poor monk is not embarrassing.” Shi Chan spoke the truth. His only defeat was when he went to the Dao-Seeking Sect and challenged Yun Zhi.

Ye Xiao grew angrier. I’m an almighty reforged cultivator and the Dark Night Pavilion Leader who has instilled fear in the hearts of numerous cultivators. How could I not defeat a little monk from a later era?

It must be a psychological tactic!

“Little monk, I’ll make sure you know the consequences of provoking an assassin!”

Boom!

The Sword-Cleansing Pond that was over two meters long smashed through the wall, plunging headfirst into the inn’s hallway. Ye Xiao only felt a tremendous shockwave before he was sent flying. Several of his bones snapped as he crashed through the wall on the other side.

“How is it? Are the two young ladies injured? Where’s Ye Xiao?” Lu Yang was worried that Shi Chan couldn’t handle Ye Xiao and hastily flew over on his pond.

I gotta say, piloting a pond is much faster than flying by myself.

Shi Chan pointed toward the hole in the opposite wall and pressed his palms together. “He was sent flying by you, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

Immediately after, Meng Jingzhou walked in through the other wall, carrying someone in his hand. “I saw someone lying on the rooftop when I arrived. He looked badly injured but was still breathing. Does anyone know him? I think he can still be saved.”

“Senior Brother Meng, this is Benefactor Ye Xiao. He was just sent flying by Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

“Ah? So he’s Ye Xiao. Forget it then, I’m not saving him.” Meng Jingzhou disdainfully tossed Ye Xiao to the ground and stepped on him a couple of times for good measure.

What trash—even Lu Yang could beat him.

“What should we do now—” Before Meng Jingzhou could finish, the ground shook violently.

The twin sisters were thrown off their feet, and the inn’s roof was ripped off clean. As the dust dispersed, the aloof figure of the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was revealed. Surrounded by various Transcendent Tribulation-grade magical treasures, he ignored Lu Yang and the others.

Just a few Nascent Soul cultivators—they won’t amount to anything.

With a tap of his finger, he conjured a drop of fine jade wine and dripped it into Ye Xiao’s mouth. The latter regained vitality, and his injuries healed.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was here for two purposes: to reduce the number of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from Great Xia and to have Ye Xiao nurture a group of Fusion Stage assassins. Both methods aimed to destroy the Great Xia founded by Jiang Ping’an.

Lu Yang exclaimed inwardly, This is bad. It means One-Qi Venerable Lord had lost.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s Incipient Dao Fruit’s ability is a secret. His pulling everyone into the Void Realm signifies that everyone had witnessed his methods. He never intended to leave anyone alive!

“Supreme Lord.” Ye Xiao knew he was no match for Lu Yang and the others and slunk behind the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord casually swept his gaze over Lu Yang’s trio, his brow slightly furrowing as his eyes settled on Meng Jingzhou. “You are from the Meng Family?”

He had been defeated by the combined efforts of the Jiang and Meng families’ ancestors. The Void Nothingness Sect, which he had established with his own hands, was also exterminated by these two major factions. His hatred for the Meng Family was no less than his hatred for Great Xia!

Everyone from the Meng Family must die!

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord reached out a hand. Just as he was about to execute Meng Jingzhou, his expression suddenly changed. He sensed someone attacking the barriers of his Void Realm.

“Who is it?!”

A crack appeared in the sky. A tall, thin man resembling a bamboo pole appeared, staring coldly at the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

“Damn it! I finally found a lead on the Twins River. I’d like to see which rascal without eyes dares to touch the people I’ve marked!”

Chapter 674: Turning Illusion Into Reality

Everyone present was startled by the turn of events, especially the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, whose face was so dark that water could drip from it.

The Void Realm was his territory and blocked external perception from the outside world. In theory, no one should be able to find this place, let alone enter.

The Void Realm’s exterior was more fragile than its interior. Breaking in from the outside required one’s cultivation to be at least on par with the One-Qi Venerable Lord’s, in other words, the Advanced Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Sensing the flickering marks left on the twin sisters’ hands, he figured out what had happened. The other party had left marks on these two sisters and followed them to find me.

Although I don’t know what the Twins River is or how these two sisters are connected to it, since this person has come to the Void Realm, they shall leave their leaves here!

Anyone who enters the Void Realm may find out about my Incipient Dao Fruit’s ability; absolutely no one can leave! Once my ability is leaked, opponents can devise countermeasures and significantly diminish the advantage of my Incipient Dao Fruit in the future.

It doesn’t matter whether this tall and thin bamboo pole is at the Advance or Apex Transcendent Tribulation stage or even a half-immortal; I’m confident I can keep this person here!

“Twins River?” Hearing the familiar term, Lu Yang confirmed with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Immortal Fairy, is that the Twins River you created, the one where drinking its water allows one to conceive twins? Were Fuling and her sister born after their mother drank from the Twins River?”

Lu Yang recalled the twin sisters mentioning that their mother had gone to the Ancient Forest Temple to seek Master Yuxin and pray for children. The process was unknown, but she eventually gave birth to the sisters.

So, did Master Yuxin make the sisters’ mother drink water from the Twins River?

“Now that you mention it, it might really be possible.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed softly, then carefully examined the twin sisters, but she couldn’t discern anything.

“Immortal Fairy, you can’t tell whether these sisters are products of the Twins River?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “Who could tell that? It’s not like I gave birth to them. But if these two lasses are really connected to the Twins River, it might be possible to track down the Twins River through them.”

“How?”

“That’s simple. This immortal can just cast a minor origin-tracing spell to locate it. But only I can use this method. That tall and thin bamboo pole who just popped up definitely can’t.”

“Then what is his method?” Lu Yang stole a glance at the two figures confronting each other in the air. Both were arrogant individuals confident in their own strength; it was unlikely that a few simple words could resolve this.

“Living beings born from consuming the waters of the Mother-Child River or the Twins River have one characteristic—after death, their souls turn into formless energy, return to the river, and become part of it. It’s what people often call ‘falling leaves return to the roots—all things go back to their source eventually.’

“But the premise is that these living beings die peacefully.”

“Why is there such a premise?” Lu Yang was puzzled.

“People are born without inherent good or evil. The Mother-Child River and Twins River must also remain absolutely pure. If there is regret or resentment before one’s death, it would pollute the rivers, affecting living beings born subsequently. Thus, I added this restriction.”

“I see.” Lu Yang nodded. It sounds like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had given it considerable thought when creating the two rivers.

“This thin bamboo pole probably wants these two lasses to die blissfully in their sleep. At that time, their spirits will return to the Twins River. However, he only left a mark and hadn’t fully prepared to put the two lasses into the dream when this kid called Void Emptiness dragged them into the Void Realm.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s conjecture was correct. Upon seeing an outsider intrude, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was filled with killing intent, and the tall and thin bamboo pole wasn’t much better.

Do you know how much effort I’d expended to find the Twins River?

After awakening, he had heard about the matter of Master Yuxin praying for children and realized the latter knew the location of the Twins River. Unfortunately, Master Yuxin had already died of old age, cutting off the clues. He could only settle for the next best option: finding the last twins of the Twins River—Fuling and Kongque.

Killing the sisters directly would result in their spirits carrying resentment, preventing them from returning to the Twins River. Yet, he couldn’t wait a hundred years for them to die of old age. Moreover, as the sisters were twins from the Twins River, they were blessed with great fortune and weren’t easy to kill. Hence, he could only make them die in their dreams.

After finding the sisters, he planned to let them live out their lives in their dreams tonight and die peacefully in their sleep.

Who would have thought that something like this would happen before night fell? This is the Twins River, a creation of an immortal, a legendary item, and an ancient supreme treasure crafted by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. Its value rivals that of an immortal artifact, and it encompasses the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s unparalleled divine abilities and the Dao charms of heaven and earth. Anyone who obstructs me from obtaining the Twins River will have a blood feud with me!

“I’m taking these two away,” the tall and thin bamboo pole stated coldly, disregarding the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was angered by the commanding attitude. “Fellow Daoist, aren’t you disregarding me too much?!”

“Are you releasing them or not?!” Toward someone getting in the way of his fortuitous opportunity, the tall and thin bamboo pole showed no courtesy.

“What if I say no?!”

“Then we’ll settle it with our skills!”

Both had their own pride and refused to yield an inch. Moreover, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord never intended to let the other party leave alive.

“Manifold Creations!” With a thought, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord conjured nearly a hundred different kinds of magical treasures. Each was coated with a deadly, incurable poison—the slightest touch would mean certain death!

“Void Emptiness, collapse!”

The space beneath the tall and thin bamboo pole’s feet distorted like quicksand, and he couldn’t break free. Faced with the onslaught of magical treasures, he had nowhere to evade.

The Void Realm was the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s territory; he could control it at will!

Facing the lethal attacks that sealed his path of retreat, the tall and thin bamboo pole frowned. He hadn’t expected his opponent’s ability to be void creation. He softly uttered, “Enter Dream.”

With that, the entire Void Realm fell into a hazy state between reality and illusion, as though everything was false yet also real. It was as if a veil had been cast over everyone, slowing their thoughts. Even the One-Qi Venerable Lord was somewhat affected, though he regained his senses quickly.

Only two present were unaffected: the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord and Lu Yang.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s going on?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed an excited smile. “Interesting. It seems this bamboo pole’s Incipient Dao Fruit is related to dreamscapes. He’s now merged the Void Realm with a dreamscape. All of you are both in a dream and in reality.

“If this were outside, he would only be capable of pulling everyone into a dream. But here in the Void Realm, which isn’t a true world, his Incipient Dao Fruit’s ability can be further unleashed, allowing dreams to directly affect reality. He’s not far from reaching the realm of ‘turning illusion into reality.’

“That’s not even the most interesting part. Do you know what is?”

“What?”

“These two Incipient Dao Fruits—one creates a Void Realm, while the other creates a dreamscape—both belong to the ‘turning illusion into reality’ lineage, and this lineage has yet to produce an immortal.

“Do you remember why the Qilin Immortal, Lianyi, and Little Ling were engaged in a great battle?”

Lu Yang’s pupils constricted sharply as he understood what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was getting at. “Are you saying that only one of them can become an immortal?”

“Correct. The battle for immortal ascension is a fight to the death!”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord was a beat slower, but also realized they were in a dreamscape, and his heart suddenly skipped a beat. He didn’t know what an immortal ascension battle was or that these two were in a fight to the death, but he guessed the tall and thin bamboo pole’s identity.

“Dreamscape...an Incipient Dao Fruit about dreams... Could he be the Nightmare Supreme Lord?”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord was a figure from the late Great Qian era and wielded the Dreamscape Incipient Dao Fruit. He once contended for the empire with the founding Yu Emperor but narrowly lost.

Chapter 676: The Might of Creed Leader Yun

“Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed?”

The two archaic supreme lords furrowed their brows. As half-immortals revived in the current era, they had meticulously investigated this ancient organization.

The Heavenly Court Creed’s origin could be traced back to the ancient era. Every time it acted, it shocked the world.

First was the battle at Hanshui City, where the Heavenly Court’s ruler, Dou Heavenly Sovereign, manipulated the national fortune’s power with a single immortal thought, overwhelmingly defeating three Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

Next was the Young Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed openly appearing at the Dao-Seeking Sect and challenging the world’s prodigies, ultimately fighting Lu Yang to a draw before swaggering off.

And more recently, the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor was resurrected, defeating the self-proclaimed emperor, Supreme Lord Zhu Tian.

Each move they made demonstrated the Heavenly Court Creed’s tyrannical and unparalleled strength, and they showed not the slightest intention of concealing it, testament to their confidence in their power.

As two supreme lords who had fought their entire lives, they wouldn’t be intimidated by a mere name.

If Dou Heavenly Sovereign had come personally, they would have turned on their heels and fled. After all, Dou Heavenly Sovereign was likely an immortal, a terrifying existence they couldn’t resist.

Since it’s not Dou Heavenly Sovereign, there’s nothing to fear. Be it the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor or Creed Leader Yun, they’re no more than half-immortals.

All the ancient immortals’ names are known, and there were only four of them. The sudden appearance of Dou Heavenly Sovereign is already inconceivable; surely another immortal can’t just pop up.

Since she’s not an ancient immortal, Creed Leader Yun can only be a half-immortal.

“You wish to step on us two to make a name for yourself? Creed Leader Yun, aren’t you afraid you’ll choke on so much gall?!”

Within our combined territory, a half-immortal is nothing.

Judging by how easily she pierced through the Void Realm earlier, her Incipient Dao Fruit should be related to space.

Yun Zhi looked at the two, confusion flickering in her eyes.

“Who are you?”

The two archaic half-immortals’ veins bulged, and they flew into a rage. It had been a long time since they encountered such a provocation. Why did you come here if you don’t know us?!

“You’re courting death!”

“Heaven-Earth Dharma Manifestation!”

“Hundred Weapons Profound Mastery!”

Two towering adepts wielded various divine weapons and positioned themselves for a pincer attack on Yun Zhi, determined to annihilate her and disintegrate her soul.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord’s expression grew graver. It’s unclear whether the Heavenly Court Creed’s Creed Leader Yun is a friend or a foe. A third force entering the fray makes the battle even more unpredictable.

“It looks like these two don’t dare to underestimate Creed Leader Yun either. They’re using their ultimate moves right from the outset.”

City Lord Liu was puzzled. “Didn't they fight like this earlier? This move seems average; it didn’t cause much damage.”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord shook his head, correcting City Lord Liu’s misconception. “They didn’t injure each other earlier because their abilities were similar. If it were any other half-immortal, they absolutely wouldn’t dare to bear the direct brunt of this move!”

Heaven-Earth Dharma Manifestation possessed both offensive and defensive capabilities. It was a supreme dharma body that was similarly renowned as the Unblemished Golden Body from Buddhist sects, indestructible and peerless in defense.

Hundred Weapons Profound Mastery employed a multitude of magical treasures to form an offensive formation that broke through all defenses like cutting through bamboo, clinching victory with quantity and rendering any defense useless!

Yun Zhi raised her hand. The golden bell tied to her wrist chimed, sending out spatial ripples that swept through every inch of space. The two adepts froze as if they were under an immobilization spell, maintaining their poses with weapons raised.

The bell chimed again.

Another layer of spatial ripples emerged. The two were sent flying backward as if they were struck by an immortal hammer, crashing into the spatial barriers until they saw stars.

“So that’s where your confidence comes from! It’s because you’re relying on an immortal artifact!” The two stared fixedly at the golden bell on Yun Zhi. Even using a space-related Incipient Dao Fruit couldn’t have let her neutralize our killing moves so easily.

If we hadn’t used “Cosmos Reversal” to make our time flow backward, that single strike just now would have killed us!

She had employed power beyond the half-immortal level!

“As expected of the ancient Heavenly Court, to think they possess an immortal artifact. Well, that makes sense. They’re backed by Dou Heavenly Sovereign; it’d be strange if they didn’t have any.”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord revealed a greedy expression. Why am I obsessed with finding the Twins River? It’s precisely because it’s also a type of immortal artifact, albeit an unconventional one.

If I grasp the Twins River, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord will be mere bones on my path to immortal ascension!

Originally, the two planned to kill Creed Leader Yun first, then fight each other. But now, it seemed it wasn’t the time to hold back.

Whoever obtains the immortal artifact bell will win the fight between us!

Kill!

~~~

“Immortal Fairy, is that bell on Big Senior Sister’s wrist an immortal artifact?” Lu Yang was surprised. Ever since he met Yun Zhi, she had worn that bell. I thought it was an ordinary accessory, yet it turns out that the golden bell is an immortal artifact?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, lazily reclining on the lotus throne in the Mahavira Hall, propping her head up with one hand. Since Lass Yun has stepped in, there’s no need for me to salvage this desperate crisis.

“It’s an immortal artifact, but it has nothing to do with the attack just now. Lass Yun simply struck with her palm and broke their moves.

“I told you before. A half-immortal is a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator who has comprehended an Incipient Dao Fruit; their physical body doesn’t change. Once they become an immortal, that’s when the gap becomes vast.”

~~~

“Stars and the Big Dipper shift; the sun and moon appear together!”

“The cosmic loop changes, great cataclysmic flood!”

“Cycle of Life and Death!”

“Strip the Five Senses!”

The brilliant sun and the imposing moon appeared simultaneously in the sky, representing the pinnacles of yin and yang. They slowly rotated and formed a genuine Taiji diagram.

This was a move the Nine-Layers Immortal had executed when he was a half-immortal!

The sky was suddenly filled with stars, their positions shifting and changing. They encompassed mysterious power that stirred the past and present, causing the great cataclysmic flood to reappear in the mortal realm, its power identical to that of the great ancient deluge!

A colossal bronze wheel materialized. It was like a heavy millstone, moving slowly yet capable of crushing anything in the world. The wheel symbolized Yun Zhi’s lifespan—each marked scale represented a segment of her life. Once the wheel rotated to its endpoint, it would also signify that her life would reach its end!

It was a temporal life-and-death type of curse.

Stripping the five senses would cause Yun Zhi to lose perception of the outside world, leaving her vulnerable to their attacks.

In the outside world, the two couldn’t perform such heaven-defying moves. But here, in the combined Void Realm and dreamscape, the unique favorable conditions allowed them to unleash their skills wantonly.

The two still felt it wasn’t sufficient. Exchanging a glance, they resolved to simultaneously shout out a move that would cost them a heavy price.

“Time Stop!”

Time came to a halt. The chaotic Chunjiang City became a still frame in the river of time. Only the two archaic supreme lords could look down upon the past and present, moving within this suspended moment.

“Die!”

The moves into which they had poured countless efforts cascaded down. The sun sank, and the full moon plummeted. The great cataclysmic flood that brought nightmares to the ancient forebears descended from the sky, swirled in a heavy aura of death. The bronze wheel spun rapidly, heralding the end of life.

Within the frozen time, Yun Zhi’s eyes shifted upward, glancing at the two half-immortals. Her beautiful and dark eyes carried not a trace of emotion.

The two half-immortals felt their hair prick as a sense of foreboding dawned on them.

How could anyone move while time is stopped?!

Especially when their five senses are sealed!

Yun Zhi moved. She took a step, rending through the passage of time.

Time resumed its flow.

With a casual wave of her hand, the sun and moon shattered, the flood vanished, and the bronze wheel reversed.

It was though the world had been destroyed, plunging everything into deathly silence.

The light and shadow from the shattered sun and moon reflected Yun Zhi’s countenance, devoid of joy or sorrow.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord and the Nightmare Supreme Lord suffered a backlash, vomiting immortal blood. The fear overflowing from their pupils made them forget their injuries.

“She...she is an immortal!”

Chapter 677: One Move

“What did they just say? The Heavenly Court Creed’s Creed Leader Yun is an immortal?” City Lord Liu doubted his hearing for the first time in his life.

In this era where half-immortals don’t appear, an immortal actually showed up?

Even in the battle at Hanshui City, Dou Heavenly Sovereign had shown up as just a wisp of immortal consciousness, not in true form.

Now that we’re in Chunjiang City, not only two half-immortals but an immortal has appeared?

The One-Qi Venerable Lord nodded steadily. “There’s no mistake. Only an immortal could have neutralized those moves so effortlessly.” Now that things had progressed to this point, he had abandoned any thought of a sneak attack.

When facing an immortal, no methods are effective.

Whether the people of Chunjiang City live or die depends entirely on the Heavenly Court Creed’s intention.

~~~

“I didn’t see that coming; to think the ancient Heavenly Court has two immortals.” The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord narrowed his eyes. Various ancient talismanic runes silently crept up his arms. “Fellow Daoist, if we join forces to defeat this person, our names will surely be passed down for millennia. What do you say?”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord showed no fear. This was a once-in-a-millennia opportunity to slay an immortal. If they used words as a delay tactic before launching a sneak attack, they had a chance of success. It was worth a try!

Slaying an immortal will grant us the greatest fortuitous opportunity in the Battle of the Great Era!

“Agreed.”

The two exchanged a glance and acted simultaneously.

Boom!

They attacked each other and then bolted for the outside world.

Both wanted the other to hold off Yun Zhi while they made their getaway.

When facing an immortal, there is no chance of victory!

Not the slightest bit!

Only by fleeing is there a sliver of hope.

The two tore open their respective worlds—one dissolved the Void Realm, while the other dissolved the dreamscape.

Both the Void Realm and the dreamscape were ripped open with gigantic gaps.

Just as half their bodies were outside, Yun Zhi suddenly clapped her hands.

The openings closed, and they were pulled back by a pair of invisible hands.

The vast disparity made them realize escape was impossible. Our only hope is to fight and gamble with everything we have!

“Man follows the earth, earth follows the heavens, the heavens follow the Dao, and the Dao follows nature!”[1]

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord vanished, merging with the Void Realm. At this moment, he was the Void Realm, and the Void Realm was him! The Void Realm would make his wishes come true, including killing Yun Zhi.

This form was extremely dangerous; the slightest misstep could result in being devoured by the Void Realm, becoming its nourishment.

“The Dao is great, Heaven is great, Earth is great, and I am also great!”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord employed a similar method, merging with the dreamscape. While acquiring power, he also risked becoming a part of the dreamscape, never to wake again.

Two enormous faces appeared above Chunjiang City, roaring in unison.

“You forced our hands! You’re destined to have a fatal tribulation, and it shall come to pass today!”

They were the Void Realm and the dreamscape themselves. Every word they spoke was the will of the Void Realm and the dreamscape, imbued with karma. This was not a threat or intimidation, but a genuine karmic curse!

Spirit energy inexplicably became chaotic, forming vortexes that triggered a humongous spirit energy explosion. The odds of this spirit energy disaster occurring were one in hundreds of millions!

In the history of Great Qian, an entire city had perished in such a calamity.

Space warped and became turbulent flows. No physical object could remain intact within the spatial turbulence. The odds of this spatial turbulence occurring were one in thousands of millions!

Once, an Apex Transcendent Tribulation powerhouse lasted only three seconds in spatial turbulence before being shredded into mincemeat.

Phantoms from the past and present appeared: a huge army of a million troops, banners, corpses littering the fields... Time lost all meaning in this moment. The odds of this time travel event occurring were one in thousands of billions!

The descending army charged at Yun Zhi, their banners proclaiming them as Great Yu’s forces. The Nightmare Supreme Lord had slain Great Yu’s million-strong army in dreamscapes during the late Great Qian era.

Statistically improbable events occurred in succession, with the various adversities befalling Yun Zhi.

A massive shadow enveloped Yun Zhi. It was a range of undulating black mountains, entities created from the void. Their density and weight were incalculable, and the space around them displayed signs of collapsing.

Despite facing the misfortunes and black mountains, Yun Zhi remained unmoved. She sighed and extended her delicate hand, delivering a single hand chop.

It was utterly plain and unremarkable, the Great Dao in its simplest form.

The spirit energy disaster, the spatial distortion, the time travel, and the black mountains... All turned to nothingness, as if they had never appeared.

Heaven and earth were cleansed, bringing peace.

Two blood-curdling screams rang out. The Void Realm and the dreamscape were cleaved in two by Yun Zhi. Chunjiang City saw the light of day again, returning to the original world. Colors were restored, and the azure sky reappeared overhead.

The two merged supreme lords were severely wounded and were forced out of their merged states. Bisected, they fell to the ground, creating two large craters.

The One-Qi Venerable Lord swallowed hard.

One move. Just one move. And two archaic half-immortals were crushed.

Is this the power of an immortal?

Back in the original world, the two supreme lords were indignant about giving up. They made their lower halves transform into their appearance while their upper halves turned transparent, flying in different directions.

Right after they had only flown a few zhang, Yun Zhi slapped each of them back to the ground, and they couldn’t even get up.

They wanted to let their primordial soul leave their bodies. When the primordial soul was out of the body, it could travel a thousand li with a single thought, so fast that no one could catch up to it. This was their final life-preserving method. It was thanks to this move that they survived under the hands of the founding Yu Emperor and the founding Xia Emperor.

But as soon as their primordial souls flew two chi high, Yun Zhi pressed them back into their bodies.

“I didn’t expect it to be two half-immortals this time.”

Yun Zhi reattached their bodies, then grabbed the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s ankle with one hand and the Nightmare Supreme Lord’s ankle in the other before vanishing on the spot.

Before disappearing, she transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“After settling the aftermath in Chunjiang City, come find me on the hill thirty li east of the city.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou shuddered.

Although they believed they had acted courageously in the name of justice and performed many good deeds, being summoned by Yun Zhi like this somehow made them feel inexplicably guilty, as if they had done something bad in Chunjiang City.

~~~

“Things...things are fine now?”

“The Heavenly Court Creed Leader is gone?”

Seeing the three figures in the sky vanish, the civilians of Chunjiang City cheered and rejoiced. Having passed by the gates of hell and narrowly escaped death, surviving the ordeal was worth celebrating.

“Did the Heavenly Court Creed Leader save us?”

“Yes, it must have been her!”

“Strange, why can’t I remember what transpired during the battle just now? I clearly remember the fight between the two half-immortals.”

“Now that you mention it, it seems to be the case for me too.”

“Look at your memories. Good thing I recorded it earlier... Strange, why is there nothing on the paper?”

The oblivion trait spread through the city.

~~~

“Venerable Lord, do you remember Creed Leader Yun’s combat style?”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord shook his head. He sighed deeply, feeling an indescribable melancholy. “I can’t remember. It seems the legends are true. No wonder the ancient texts don’t record the details of immortal battles. It’s not because they didn’t want to, but that they simply couldn’t.”

“By the way, where did Ye Xiao go?” City Lord Liu recalled that they were supposed to escort Ye Xiao away.

“Don’t bother looking for him. He was caught in the crossfire of the two half-immortals and turned to ashes. The vice pavilion leader is still alive though. I’ll go find him.”

The One-Qi Venerable Lord stretched his back, thinking it was a good time to regain some confidence by dealing with the vice pavilion leader.

1. A more detailed interpretation of this would be: humans inhabit the earth, where they live, work, and reproduce; the earth gives birth to all things and nurtures them, depending on the whims of heaven, which include the weather and climate; the heavens have to comply with the Great Dao, resulting in various meteorological conditions; the Great Dao is in accordance with nature, where things take its natural course. ☜

Chapter 678: How Did You Two Attract Two Half-Immortals?

“It’s finally over.” Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief. The earlier half-immortal battle had frightened him out of his wits.

“Since when were you so timid?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang in puzzlement. “Back when I fought Lass Yun, I didn’t see you this scared.”

That was a battle between almighty immortals. Compared to our battle, those two half-immortals are nothing, merely a village scuffle.

Lu Yang, “...”

The logic is sound, but I can’t help but feel something is off.

“Thank goodness you summoned Big Senior Sister.” Meng Jingzhou was also quite petrified by the battle. Without Big Senior Sister, that would have been perilous.

“Amitabha. No wonder this poor monk couldn’t defeat Senior Sister Yun.” Shi Chan finally understood why his shifu told him not to provoke Yun Zhi.

Lu Yang had explained the Heavenly Court Creed to Shi Chan, who now knew its creed leader was Yun Zhi.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou turned to Shi Chan in surprise, their faces full of disbelief. “You fought Big Senior Sister?”

Shi Chan answered calmly, “Back when this poor monk went to the Dao-Seeking Sect for studies, I once challenged Senior Sister Yun. Unfortunately, I did not win.”

To think Shi Chan had done such a foolish thing. The two saluted him with cupped fists.

Respect.

As expected of an accomplished monk, his courage is extraordinary.

“Three young heroes, is everything really fine now?” Fuling asked cautiously. She and her sister hadn’t even dared to breathe heavily during the great battle earlier.

Lu Yang nodded. “Chunjiang City is safe now.”

With Big Senior Sister around, no demons, devils, ghosts, or monsters will stand a chance.

“Do you plan to continue tempering your mental state here?” Lu Yang asked Shi Chan.

Shi Chan shook his head gently. The matter was concluded, but given the current situation, the brothel wouldn’t open for a while, and neither were they in the mood to open. Hence, he needed to search for another place to temper his mental state.

“Then I wish you success in advance,” Lu Yang said with a smile and cupped his fists. He and Meng Jingzhou needed to find Yun Zhi later and couldn’t tag along with Shi Chan.

“Senior brothers, this poor monk thanks you for your kind intentions.”

The inn’s second floor had completely become an open-air room, with wooden splinters scattered everywhere and debris messily strewn around.

Lu Yang picked up a wooden plank, likely part of the roof. Using his finger as a sword, he swiftly carved it into the shape of a wooden sword and engraved the characters “Lu Yang” on the hilt.

After carving two wooden swords, he gave them to Fuling and Kongque.

“This wooden sword contains a wisp of my sword qi, which has defensive capabilities. Evil spirits and demons won’t dare approach. If you encounter danger, the unleashed attack is equivalent to a full-power strike from an Apex Nascent Soul cultivator. If you face any difficulties in the future, you can also bring this sword to the Dao-Seeking Sect to find me.”

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, she had cast a spell to locate the Twins River through the sisters, but they wouldn’t sense it. It wasn’t wise to let the sisters learn of the Twins River, else it might easily attract trouble.

The sisters carefully stowed the wooden swords away and thanked Lu Yang. These are priceless protective talismans that can save our lives in critical moments.

Seeing Lu Yang hand them gifts so solemnly, Meng Jingzhou also wanted to give them something. But upon second thought, he only had yang-boosting blood and spirit stones, neither of which was suitable as a gift.

He pondered for a bit and made a promise. “If you two ladies ever need spirit stones in the future, feel free to borrow from our Meng Family.”

After bidding farewell to the sisters, the trio saw the grief-stricken innkeeper.

My fine inn has been reduced to just the first floor being inhabitable. Even if the imperial court provides relief funds to rebuild the inn, that will take considerable time.

The kind-hearted Eldest Young Master Meng gave the innkeeper some spirit stones as compensation for the disruption.

The trio then went to bid farewell to City Lord Liu.

After such events in Chunjiang City, the simple meal they had been promised was out of the question. City Lord Liu was as busy as a spinning top, maintaining order and providing disaster relief within the city while writing reports to his superiors beyond the city.

When the three arrived, they happened to witness the One-Qi Venerable Lord demonstrating his might, vigorously battling the Fusion Stage Vice Pavilion Leader of the Dark Night Pavilion. The One-Qi Venerable Lord fought with great relish, while the Vice Pavilion Leader was beaten black and blue.

The three parted ways outside the city. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou followed Yun Zhi’s instructions and headed to the small hill thirty li east of the city.

~~~

Upon arriving at the small hill, they ran into Yun Zhi conducting a brief interrogation to ascertain the identities of the two archaic supreme lords. Yun Zhi had set up an array around the hill, causing outsiders to subconsciously avoid the area.

“In other words, one of you is the Nightmare Supreme Lord from the late Great Qian era, and the other is the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord from the late Great Yu era?”

“Senior, you flatter me. Just call me Little Dream.”[1]

“Just call me Little Void.”

The two supreme lords were as well-behaved as they could be. Under someone else’s roof, one must bow their head. Both archaic supreme lords were outstanding figures of their eras. They knew when to yield and never acted tough unnecessarily.

In terms of era, Creed Leader Yun hails from the ancient era, earlier than our time. In terms of cultivation, she is an immortal, higher than us.

There’s no problem with addressing her as senior.

“Big Senior Sister, we’ve finished handling our matters.”

Yun Zhi produced the specialty Lu Yang had brought back from the Demon Region—the monarch’s chair. She sat on it and inquired about the events in an unruffled tone.

“Explain what happened. Junior Brother Meng, I recall you had inquired about the black market from Junior Brother Dai before leaving and promised to ‘absolutely not cause any trouble for the next six months.’”

Yun Zhi had heard this from Dai Bufan. Who would have thought that it wouldn’t take six months, but merely half a month to attract a battle between two archaic half-immortals?

Meng Jingzhou protested his innocence, determined to clarify the matter. “Big Senior Sister, please investigate this properly. Old Lu and I are victims!

“Originally, I had the idea of starting my own business independently. I stopped after earning my first pot of gold and left the black market. When Lu Yang bumped into Shi Chan seeking alms, we saw that he was impoverished and struggling with his livelihood. As fellow disciples of immortal sects, we were concerned about him and decided to accompany him in training his heart in the mundane realm.

“In Chunjiang City, the three of us acted courageously for justice. We repeatedly saved a pair of sisters, provided the authorities with leads on an assassin organization, subdued demons and vanquished evil, and peacefully resolved a dispute involving four Nascent Soul demons, ghosts, and spirits, allowing them to coexist harmoniously under one roof.

“Upon learning of our deeds, the city lord even invited us for a meal.”

Meng Jingzhou pointed firmly at the two supreme lords kneeling on the ground and declared loudly, “It was clearly these two who stirred up trouble for no reason, insisting on fighting in Chunjiang City. We are the victims.

“These two battled wantonly, tearing off the roof of the inn we were staying in, completely disregarding the innkeeper’s feelings. Even the innkeeper’s losses were covered by me on their behalf!”

Lu Yang backed him up. “That’s right! These two not only brawled in public but also abducted criminals, openly shielded an evil criminal organization, and attempted to steal ancient treasures... There’s no wicked deed they aren’t capable of, and even bamboo slats aren’t enough to list their numerous crimes!”

1. The term for nightmare in Chinese is made up of the character for “dream” and “nightmare.” ☜

Chapter 679: Twins River

The two supreme lords knelt silently, but the more they listened, the more they felt something was off.

Is the ancient Heavenly Court so well-versed in law?

And shouldn’t they address her as “Creed Leader?” Why are they calling her “Big Senior Sister?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were using their real faces. Priding themselves as noble half-immortals, they primarily focused on understanding the major factions that could threaten them in the current era. Mere Nascent Soul cultivators naturally didn’t catch their eye, let alone the fact that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had become famous during the mere Golden Core Stage.

After listening to Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s explanations, Yun Zhi confirmed that the two supreme lords’ battle was indeed unrelated to her junior brothers.

“Little Junior Brother, you mentioned that these two supreme lords attempted to steal an ancient treasure. What exactly were they trying to steal?”

“Hehe, Second-In-Command doesn’t know much about this. Let this immortal explain.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy darted out of Lu Yang’s body.

The two supreme lords stared at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in bewilderment. Neither of them had detected another person residing within Lu Yang.

This is impossible!

Even if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator resided in Lu Yang, it shouldn’t have escaped their eyes.

Could this woman be a half-immortal?

“Do you remember the sisters those two young fellows mentioned?”

Yun Zhi nodded. The sisters’ experiences are quite bizarre.

“Actually, the two sisters weren’t born to their parents in a normal way. Their mother drank water from the Twins River, which resulted in their birth.”

“What is the Twins River?” Yun Zhi hadn’t heard of it.

“This immortal will have to mention her greatness then.

“Back in the ancient era, I had countless followers. Some sought me out to pray for children, others for twins. I gladly agreed and employed supreme great power to create the Mother-Child River and the Twins River.

“Anyone who drinks from the Mother-Child River will become pregnant.

“Anyone who drinks from the Twins River will conceive twins.”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord’s eyes widened in disbelief. He stared at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in terror, his voice quivering. “You...no... You are the Heaven Mandate Immortal?!”

I’d come here to search for the Twins River, but I never expected its creator to be right here!

The legendary Heaven Mandate Immortal is actually a woman!

Lu Yang, “...”

There’s no need to say more. It’s surely another case of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s deeds being attributed to the Heaven Mandate Immortal due to the altered history.

Yun Zhi was stunned and recalled something. She gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with a strange expression, her feelings complex. She couldn’t really believe what she had heard, and even her tone was different from usual. “You’re saying that...you created the Mother-Child River, and anyone who drinks from it will become pregnant?”

With her inherently naive nature, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t notice Yun Zhi’s odd reaction and nodded sincerely. “That’s right. What about it?”

“Then where is the Mother-Child River now?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “I don’t know. When the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others reconstructed the continents, the terrain changed. I have no idea where they moved the Mother-Child River.”

Yun Zhi’s expression grew even more peculiar. She opened her mouth, wanting to say something, but ultimately didn’t utter those words.

Lu Yang noticed the change in Yun Zhi’s countenance. Since joining the sect, Yun Zhi had always maintained an impassive demeanor. He had never seen her expression change so vividly.

But he didn’t quite dare ask what she was thinking.

“Although we can’t find the Mother-Child River, we can find the Twins River. I had Second-In-Command secretly pluck two hairs from those two lasses. I can trace the origin through their hair and locate the Twins River.”

Lu Yang opened his hand, revealing two strands of hair.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy formed an obscure and elusive ancient spell seal. Only she knew this seal; not even the other four ancient immortals knew it.

The moment the spell seal touched the two strands of hair, they transformed into a wisp of faint cyan smoke that drifted into the distance.

“Let’s go! Follow this smoke, and we’ll find the Twins River!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand and charged ahead, beckoning the others to follow.

Everyone followed.

The cyan smoke drifted for half a day. After passing a temple, its speed slowed.

As Lu Yang passed by, he saw the temple’s name: Ancient Forest Temple.

The Ancient Forest Temple was nestled at the foot of the mountain, with endless ranges of huge mountains behind it. The cyan smoke flew over a dozen mountain summits before hovering around in a maple grove.

“Why did it stop moving?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “The Twins River is in a secret domain. The cyan smoke can’t reach it directly. We need to find the secret domain’s entrance. Judging by the smoke’s circular path, the secret domain should be here.” She took two steps forward and pointed at a very inconspicuous large rock in the maple grove.

The smoke kept circling nearby, and the center of its trajectory was this giant rock.

Yun Zhi flicked her finger, sending a wisp of spirit energy into the giant rock. The smoother side of the rock transformed into a black vortex.

“It’s here.”

Without hesitation, Yun Zhi tossed the two half-immortals into the vortex before stepping in herself. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou followed closely.

Right after everyone entered, the black vortex vanished, and the rock returned to its original appearance. No one could tell it led to the Twins River, an immortal creation.

“Such dense spirit energy!” Lu Yang was amazed.

He stood on a lawn. A wide river meandered, its source unknown. The surface of the river radiated with abundant spirit energy that suffused the secret domain. The vegetation along the banks was lush—ancient trees, shrubs, and green grass—all spirit plants that were now extinct. Moreover, these spirit plants grew in pairs. Irrigated by the Twins River, their medicinal efficacy was significantly enhanced.

On the river surface grew Twin Lotus Flowers, which could help one achieve a first-grade golden core. The Twin Lotus Flower was originally a product of the Twins River, initially named “Beautiful Sisters Flower” before the Heaven Mandate Immortal changed its name to the current one.

The two supreme lords felt it even more keenly. They sensed the immense power within the river—the purest Dao charms. Comprehending by the riverside alone would greatly aid them in condensing their Dao Fruits.

“Yes, this is the Twins River this immortal created.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed at the river gleefully. The environment here was identical to that in the ancient era, filling her with nostalgia.

“I didn’t expect the preservation here to be this complete.” She was slightly surprised. This was almost the entire Twins River. It was hard to imagine it could remain this intact despite the battle that reconstructed the continents.

“Immortal Fairy, is that your cave abode over there?” Lu Yang pointed to a stone chamber by the river.

In ancient script, it read “Immortal Abode.” Judging by its scale, it was probably only part of the immortal abode.

“It really is. But that shouldn’t be the case. I didn’t establish an immortal abode by the Twins River,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured to herself before something suddenly clicked in her. “I got it! That lass Qing He likely helped this immortal preserve it! However, it was too chaotic then, and she didn’t manage to save all of it!”

Be it the Twins River or the immortal abode, Qing He had preserved them during the critical juncture.

“Let’s see what’s inside.”

The immortal abode’s entrance was tightly locked. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy used her soul as a key to open it.

Inside, it was as if time stood still. The interior was spotlessly clean, as though the owner hadn’t left long ago. The shelves were lined with various books, their covers brand new.

“This is where this immortal read.”

Lu Yang noticed a particularly conspicuous booklet on the shelf titled Immortals’ Quotes.
