Out of curiosity, he took it down and browsed through it. Profound and abstruse ancient script greeted his eyes.

This esteemed one was born under the mandate of Heaven!

Those who defy this immortal shall be slain!

How dare mortals oppose immortals?!

This esteemed one harbors immense power within. Do not force this esteemed one to remove the seal!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had thoughtfully annotated who said each quote: Heaven Mandate Immortal, Nine-Layers Immortal, Qilin Immortal, Epoch Immortal.

The cast fully assembled.

Lu Yang silently closed the book and placed it back in its position, pretending he hadn’t seen it.

Chapter 680: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Cultivation Insights

In that moment, Lu Yang wished he had an oblivion spell to make him forget everything he had just seen.

Although I already knew much of the Four Ancient Immortals dark embarrassing history, that was only through witness accounts, leaving room for denial.

But that’s not the case anymore. There is even physical evidence now. The Four Ancient Immortals might destroy me along with the Immortals’ Quotes.

“I’d forgotten I left Immortals’ Quotes here.” Bold due to her immense skills, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy took the book down from the shelf again, feeling rather nostalgic. “This is good stuff. Back when the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others gave lectures, I sat in and recorded the contents of their lessons.”

After entering the secret domain, Yun Zhi hadn’t restricted the two supreme lords’ movements, and they also came to the study. Hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words, their searing gazes burned into the Immortals’ Quotes, their hearts pounding wildly.

Oh dear heavens! This book actually contains the teachings of immortals! The comprehension and insights of immortals are incredibly precious—priceless treasures!

But they had been reduced to prisoners. They could only covet it, their eyes green with envy, but they did not dare reach for it.

Judging by her words, could it be that she isn’t the Heaven Mandate Immortal?

Then who is she? Wait... could she be the ruler of the Heavenly Court, Dou Heavenly Sovereign?

The two half-immortals finally guessed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s identity, their legs trembling.

“Is this the study?” Yun Zhi also noticed the immortal abode.

Upon entering, she was greeted by a dazzling array of ancient books. Ancient texts were extremely precious; any single one would cause a frenzy if put up for auction.

“Yes, this is where this immortal studied and read.”

Lu Yang looked at the mostly brand-new books. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy really likes books—she can’t even bear to read them.

Yun Zhi also noticed this but didn’t comment.

The study had a comprehensive collection of books, covering everything from ancient conditions and customs to cultivation secret manuals. There were even considerable cultivation insights from half-immortals, including those from Zhu Tian and Jiang Lianyi.

The half-immortals’ cultivation insights had been voluntarily provided by archaic half-immortals. Their main purpose was to fill the shelves. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t be bothered to read them.

As the almighty number one immortal of antiquity, who walked an unprecedented path, why would I need to draw on others’ cultivation experiences?

The Comprehensive Culinary Compendium was also here. Naturally, the author was stated to be the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“So you’re all here.” Meng Jingzhou had been exploring the secret domain when he turned and found everyone gone, breaking into a cold sweat. Seeing everyone in the study, he sighed in relief.

“Well, have you found any good stuff here?” Meng Jingzhou nudged Lu Yang with his elbow.

“Yes.” Lu Yang handed the Immortals’ Quotes to Meng Jingzhou and said solemnly, “This immortal text records the words and deeds of the Four Ancient Immortals. It contains boundless profundities that align with the Great Dao. Back then, ancient half-immortals and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators lined up to study it. You should read it carefully.”

“There’s such good stuff?!” Meng Jingzhou was astonished. Lu Yang is truly my good brother. He never forgets about me when there are good things.

Meng Jingzhou flipped through a couple of pages and returned it to Lu Yang.

“Why did you stop reading?” Lu Yang asked.

“It’s all in ancient script. I can’t understand it.”

“...I’ll teach you ancient script when I have the chance.”

“Strange, where did this immortal’s diary go?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked around the study but couldn’t find her diary.

“Immortal Fairy, you kept a diary?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“Of course. With so many fun and interesting things, I naturally recorded them in a diary.”

“What was written in the diary?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang warily. “How can a diary be shown to others casually?”

Lu Yang pouted. She’s quite vigilant. “It’s probably gone. After all, the diary bore a strong personal imprint of you. Just changing the name wouldn’t suffice to frame the Heaven Mandate Immortal. Since the mastermind wanted to erase your existence, the diary proving your existence would naturally be erased too.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was furious. “Damn it! I will surely avenge this grudge!”

The two supreme lords shuddered uncontrollably in trepidation upon hearing this. This conversation seems to include shocking ancient secrets. Will we be silenced?

“This immortal’s cultivation insights are gone too?” She couldn’t locate her cultivation insights either. “It seems they were erased by the mastermind too. After all, my talent is peerless. Attributing those insights to the Heaven Mandate Immortal would seem too fake; he obviously doesn’t have such capabilities!”

Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy strangely. “Immortal Fairy, you had insights for cultivation?”

“Why not? I wrote a thick book of insights, from how to have fun to how to sleep comfortably. It was extremely detailed. It included cited classics and my personal experiences.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, It’s fine even if those cultivation insights are lost. Between losing the book and losing face, you have to choose one.

In contrast, Yun Zhi agreed with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s perspective. “Senior, you possess the pure and innocent heart of a newborn, which is truly rare. Especially after becoming an immortal, remaining like an innocent child is even more challenging. I believe those cultivation insights must be about teaching the world how to maintain a pure childlike heart. You have a lofty sense of righteousness, Senior.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt like she had found a kindred spirit, grinning from ear to ear. “Lass Yun, you understand well!”

Then, she turned to Lu Yang and said fiercely, “Hear that? This is called a pure and innocent childlike heart. Learn more from this immortal in the future!”

Lu Yang, “...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “Lass Yun, pack up. Move this secret domain back to our sect.” Once this is moved back, we can take our time to hang out in the secret domain.

From the Twins River to the study, everything in the secret domain is ours. Even if we move it back directly, Great Xia can’t find fault with us.

“Alright.”

By the time everyone left the secret domain, it was already night, and the mountain forest was pitch black.

Yun Zhi extended her right hand and pressed it against the giant rock, which emitted a faint glow. When she withdrew her hand, a meandering small river lay in her palm.

This was the true Cosmos in Palm.

“Let’s go.”

~~~

With matters concluded, everyone returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Only when they neared their destination did the two supreme lords realize they were heading to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Is the ancient Heavenly Court hidden within the Dao-Seeking Sect?

Or was the Dao-Seeking Sect established by the ancient Heavenly Court?

Either way, it is testament to the brilliant and superior methods of the ancient Heavenly Court.

Yun Zhi first left the secret domain with the Twins River beside the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s kitchen on Heaven’s Gate Peak, then took the two supreme lords to Incarceration Peak.

If I hadn’t arrived in time, these two might have truly destroyed Chunjiang City. I can’t let them off.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou returned to their respective mountain peaks.

~~~

“Little Yun, you’re here? Who did you catch this time?” The childlike grand-shifu asked cheerfully.

He had already come to terms with it. As an elder and a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, I can’t lose composure over a few archaic prisoners.

Yun Zhi placed the two on the ground and reported the gains from this trip. “I caught two half-immortals. One is called the Nightmare Supreme Lord, and the other is called the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord.

Grand-Shifu clutched his chest, almost failing to catch his breath.

Chapter 681: An Old Acquaintance

Last time, you brought the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. This time, you’re directly bringing two archaic half-immortals to Incarceration Peak, huh?

I’m a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, not an immortal.

If this goes on, I dare not imagine what other major figures may be brought back next.

“It’s that kid Lu Yang again?” The childlike grand-shifu suddenly realized the source of the constant unrest since his retirement.

“Little Junior Brother just happened to be present.”

The prisoners of Incarceration Peak sucked in a cold breath in succession.

In the last two years, the prisoners locked up at Incarceration Peak are all connected to this cultivator named Lu Yang.

Moreover, the backgrounds of the new prisoners have been increasingly astounding. First, a Great Yu emperor, then half-immortals who contended for supremacy. If Incarceration Peak could be considered a faction, it could rival the Demon Kingdom.

The Demon Kingdom only had two half-immortals.

They never expected to see the two supreme lords who once vied for supremacy in their lifetimes.

Wu Youdao, the Yu Emperor, avoided eye contact upon seeing the Nightmare Supreme Lord. As the sixth Yu emperor, I know all too well how powerful the Nightmare Supreme Lord is. In my ancestor’s struggle for the empire, the Nightmare Supreme Lord was undoubtedly the biggest obstacle. This is an indisputable fact!

“Nightmare stays here. I’ll take Void Emptiness out for a bit.” Yun Zhi wasn’t afraid of the Nightmare Supreme Lord escaping. She had planted a Thought Seed in him. Once he entertained thoughts of escape, the seed would grow, tormenting him until he wished he could be dead instead.

Learning about the Thought Seed, Grand-Shifu finally relaxed slightly.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord didn’t know where Yun Zhi was taking him. Grabbed by the collar, he was whisked away at breakneck speed until they reached their destination.

The imperial city’s imperial palace!

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s eyes instantly turned red from envy. If not for the Jiang and Meng families, this should have been my territory—no, the entire Great Xia should have been mine!

Before arriving at the imperial palace, Yun Zhi had transmitted an auditory message to the Xia Emperor, asking him to dismiss his attendants.

The Xia Emperor had been handling court memorials about Chunjiang City in the Mental Cultivation Hall. He was initially taken aback but quickly regained his senses, ordering the eunuchs and palace maids to leave.

Yun Zhi dragged the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord to the Mental Cultivation Hall. Seeing the Xia Emperor, whose features somewhat resembled Jiang Ping’an, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s breathing grew unsteady with rage.

“I presume this is the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord who contended with my ancestor for supremacy?” The Xia Emperor marveled as he examined the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord. It wasn’t easy to have a chance to meet his old ancestor’s opponent.

Due to Yun Zhi’s power, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord feared her. But facing his enemy’s descendant, a Xia Emperor with little cultivation talent, he wasn’t so restrained.

“It seems Jiang Ping’an committed many evil deeds, leaving his descendants hardly any years to live!” He saw through the Xia Emperor’s weakness at a glance, which stemmed from a deficient lifespan, and couldn’t help but gloat.

The Xia Emperor’s expression turned unpleasant. This was his greatest sore point.

Yun Zhi suddenly recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioning a natural spiritual root in the form of a peach tree, not categorized as a natural treasure. The peaches it bore could extend one’s lifespan, but its whereabouts were unknown. And in the secret domain where she grew up, there were countless peach trees aside from the Mother-Child River.

Could one of them be that so-called natural spiritual root?

If so, the Xia Emperor can be saved.

This isn’t certain yet, so there’s no need to tell the Xia Emperor, lest it give him false hopes.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s mood inexplicably improved. I initially thought Creed Leader Yun had brought me here to anger me, but now it looks like it’s for my own amusement.

Wait, since Creed Leader Yun knows the current Xia Emperor, does that mean Great Xia is colluding with the ancient Heavenly Court?

I can’t help but feel like something is off.

“Then I’ll take him in to meet someone first,” Yun Zhi said casually.

Hearing this, the Xia Emperor personally opened the door for her.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was puzzled. Who else is she taking me to see?

Yun Zhi didn’t answer, instead grabbing the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord by the collar and bringing him to the palace’s rear courtyard, an area the eunuchs and palace maids called the “forbidden ground.”

Red walls, red doors, blue tiles—this was the palace servants’ impression of the forbidden ground.

As for what it looked like inside, why entry was forbidden, or who resided there, that remained unknown.

The tall red doors were carved with two heads of bronze demon beasts holding ring door knockers in their mouths. Yun Zhi lightly knocked three times.

Clang, clang, clang.

The ferocious bronze demon beasts’ eyes lit up, and the doors opened silently.

Entering the forbidden ground, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord found the interior was different from how it appeared outside.

Looking at the forbidden ground from outside, there were no structures or hills that were higher than the red palace walls.

But inside, it was vast and boundless, complete with mountains and rivers, except that everything was diminutive. The highest peak was only thirty or forty meters tall, like a small earth mound. The rivers were pitifully narrow, and the lakes were as small as puddles after a rain.

It was as if everything from the outside world had shrunk upon coming in. They were like titans walking through a miniature world.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord found one mountain increasingly familiar. “Wait, that is Tai’an Mountain, and next to it is the Bamboo Grove Lake...” He matched the scenery around him one by one, and realization dawned upon him.

This is a miniature version of Great Xia!

“Let me see who Fellow Daoist Yun has brought. Ah, an old acquaintance.” A relatively young voice sounded from the horizon.

“This voice...” Upon hearing it, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s aura leaked uncontrollably as killing intent surged.

A young man dressed in coarse hemp clothes and carrying a hoe landed, looking cheerfully at the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord. The young man had a bright smile and delicate features, easily winning goodwill from others.

“Void Emptiness, it’s been a hundred thousand years since we last met, hasn’t it?”

As soon as his eyes fell on the young man, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord wished he could devour him alive. I will never forget this face for a lifetime! “Jiang Ping’an, you’re still alive!”

If it weren’t for Jiang Ping’an, I would be the current emperor. Great Xia should have been mine!

Jiang Ping’an’s smile widened. “You’re still alive, so why can’t I be?” He cupped his fists and requested, “Fellow Daoist Yun, you can put him down. With you and me here, he can’t escape.”

Yun Zhi released her grip, and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord flipped mid-air before landing steadily.

“Void Emptiness, I know you’re indignant about the results, believing you lost back then only because it was two against one—me and Junzi against you.”

Meng Junzi was the Meng Family’s old ancestor.[1]

“Actually, I could have beaten you alone. It was simply faster with two people.”

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord sneered repeatedly. I’d be a fool if I believe your foolish nonsense.

“How about this? I’m not one to refuse admitting to a loss. It’s rare for us to meet. Since you’re indignant, let’s have a proper rematch, just you and me; I won’t ask anyone to help. How’s that?”

“Fine!” The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord agreed immediately.

“Void Realm, descend!” He shouted, a triumphant smile spreading across his face. As the Void Realm opened up, it enveloped both of them.

Yun Zhi brought out the monarch chair and waited nearby for the outcome.

Soon, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord couldn’t smile anymore.

“Jiang Ping’an, you motherf*cker became an immortal?!”

1. “Junzi” means gentleman or a person of noble character. ☜

Chapter 682: Issue With Form of Address

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was shocked and furious.

This grandson Jiang Ping’an is truly a bastard! You’re already an immortal, yet you still have the shame to propose a one-on-one fight?

I’ll fight you one-on-one, your grandmother!

Yun Zhi hadn’t been sitting in the monarch chair for long before the Void Realm shattered.

The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was beaten by Jiang Ping’an beyond recognition. Abilities like limb regeneration and revival from a drop of blood all failed at this moment. His injuries increased visibly, unable to heal.

Thud. The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was tossed to the ground.

Jiang Ping’an let out a long breath and wiped non-existent sweat from his brow, as if he had just been through a fierce battle. “Void Emptiness, I didn’t use any tricks, this time, did I? It was a one-on-one fight that relied on true skills. You should be completely convinced of your defeat now, right?”

After becoming an immortal, Jiang Ping’an hadn’t had the chance to show off to an old acquaintance. He had waited a hundred thousand years for this opportunity, not expecting to finally achieve it today.

Satisfying.

If the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord wasn’t in so much pain that he couldn’t stand up, he would have pounced on Jiang Ping’an to bite his throat.

“This chair is quite nice. Who crafted it?” Jiang Ping’an noticed the monarch chair that Yun Zhi was sitting on. If I weren’t advocating for a simple life recently, I’d want such an imposing chair.

“A local specialty from the Demon Region, a gift from my Little Junior Brother.”

“I remember your Little Junior Brother is called Lu Yang?” Jiang Ping’an rarely paid attention to matters outside, only hearing Yun Zhi mention him during their conversations.

“Yes, I have high hopes for him. He has already brought me many surprises. For instance, capturing Void Emptiness this time was partly his credit. He will surely have a place in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.”

Jiang Ping’an chuckled. “I’ve never heard you speak so highly of anyone, fellow Daoist.” Hearing that Lu Yang helped capture the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, Jiang Ping’an formed a favorable impression of this young cultivator he hadn’t met.

“There is another person whose future is also destined to be extraordinary.”

“Who?”

“A junior brother sent by the Meng Family.”

Jiang Ping’an clicked his tongue in amazement, sounding envious. “Why can’t our Jiang Family produce such talent?”

Aside from himself, the old ancestor, the Jiang Family’s most talented individual was the First Imperial Prince, Jiang Qun, who reached the Fusion Stage before a thousand years old. However, he was far from earning Yun Zhi’s appraisal of “extraordinary.”

Hearing their conversation, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord suddenly recalled the Meng Family’s descendant he had seen in Chunjiang City.

It’s him?

What luck does Meng Junzi have? His character is nothing special, yet he has such an outstanding descendant!

At the time, he only noticed that Meng Jingzhou was a descendant of the Meng Family and didn’t pay further attention. Judging by her evaluation of him, this descendant of the Meng Family must be a cultivation genius, at least a half-immortal like myself.

“How do you plan to deal with Void Emptiness?”

“His heart is not righteous. Releasing him would be like freeing a tiger back to the mountains, leading to endless future troubles. I plan to strip him of his physical body and suppress his soul at Incarceration Peak.”

Unlike the Everlasting Immortal, a half-immortal without prior offenses and with remorse, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord merely submitted to power temporarily, so he mustn’t be released.

Jiang Ping’an nodded. He had no objection to Yun Zhi’s approach. If it were him, he would do the same. The Void Emptiness Supreme Lord was determined to oppose his rule. Releasing him to the outside world could easily stir up further incidents, destabilizing the national fortune and giving other forces an opening to strike.

“Fellow Daoist Jiang, there’s one more matter I’d like to hear your opinion on.”

“Let’s hear it?” Jiang Ping’an was somewhat surprised. He noticed Yun Zhi’s brow furrowing almost imperceptibly when she said this, something that had never happened before.

“I have a good friend named Yun Mengmeng. Recently, she learned that she wasn’t born to her parents in the normal way. Instead, an immortal with the power to grant life had created an immortal entity, and her mother used it to give birth to her. How should she address this immortal?”

Jiang Ping’an inhaled sharply. Despite having lived a hundred thousand years, he had never heard of such a thing.

“I don’t know either.” Jiang Ping’an pondered for a long while but couldn’t figure out the appropriate form of address.

Having achieved her purpose at the imperial palace, Yun Zhi didn’t linger further. She carried the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord back to the Dao-Seeking Sect as she still needed to interrogate the two half-immortals, especially the Nightmare Supreme Lord.

As a half-immortal from the late Great Qian era, he must know many secrets. Setting aside distant matters, even the situation with the Twins River was previously unknown to Yun Zhi.

Jiang Ping’an waved goodbye. “Take care, see yourself out. I’ll visit in prison when I get the chance!”

~~~

Seeing Yun Zhi return to Incarceration Peak, the prisoners grew tense again.

Without a word, Yun Zhi pressed a hand each on the Nightmare Supreme Lord’s and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord’s foreheads and gently pulled. Just like that, the two felt their bodies lighten as their souls separated from their physical forms.

The childlike grand-shifu smiled, his eyes almost forming slits, as he dragged away the two empty corpses. These are excellent materials for refining magical treasures.

Yun Zhi gazed at the two coldly. “You have two choices now. Either truthfully disclose all the information you know, or don’t expect to keep your souls—they’ll be perfect for refining magical treasures. Using half-immortal souls as materials can count as contributing to the artifact-refining community.”

Having encountered numerous people, they could tell at a glance that Yun Zhi wasn’t bluffing.

“We’ll confess everything.”

Yun Zhi nodded, satisfied with their attitudes. She confined them in separate, isolated rooms for individual interrogation.

She first interrogated the Nightmare Supreme Lord.

“Where did you learn about the Twins River?”

“I saw it in an ancient text. It recorded both the Twins River and the Mother-Child River. But I only learned the Twins River’s location; I have no idea where the Mother-Child River is.”

“Where did you obtain the ancient text?”

“After leading my army to breach the Great Qian imperial palace, I found it in the imperial study.”

Historical texts recorded that the Nightmare Supreme Lord breached the Great Qian imperial palace and proclaimed himself emperor. This resulted in everyone vying for supremacy under the pretext of crusading against a renegade, and he was ultimately defeated by the rising new talent, the Yu Emperor.

Great Qian was the dynasty closest to ancient times. The ancient texts in its imperial study likely exceeded the total of all extant ancient texts today.

“Where is that ancient text now?”

“I burned it after memorizing the contents.” The Nightmare Supreme Lord was very nervous.

“Hmm?” As expected, Yun Zhi wasn’t satisfied with this answer.

The Nightmare Supreme Lord hastily explained, “It’s true! My subordinates can attest to it! At the time, I thought even if I failed to seize the empire, the knowledge would be in my mind, and my opponents would spare my life for that information.”

In fact, this consideration stopped the Yu Emperor and the Imperial Preceptor from delivering a fatal blow; they held back and gave him a chance to escape.

“What were the cultivation levels of the founding Yu Emperor and the first Imperial Preceptor?”

“When they fought me, they were definitely half-immortals. But whether they became immortals later, I don’t know.”

“What do you mean?”

“After surviving the great battle, I didn’t fall into a slumber directly. Instead, I hid in the shadows, watching how Wu Yao rose to an emperor step by step.”

Wu Yao was the first Yu Emperor.

“Wu Yao presided over the nation-founding ceremony. At the grand ceremony, the winds and clouds shifted, and various unusual phenomena arose. Thunder clapped incessantly, and even heaven and earth were lit up with tribulation lightning. The scribes recorded that as a symbol of Wu Yao’s brilliance and the Great Yu Dynasty’s establishment aligning with the will of heaven and earth."

Chapter 683: Wu Yao

Creating great fanfare artificially during founding ceremonies was a common practice. Whether it was Great Qian, Great Yu, or even Great Xia, all generated considerable commotion during their founding ceremonies.

Tracing the origin, it could be linked back to when the Nine-Layers Immortal became an immortal. Therefore, neither Yun Zhi nor Jiang Ping’an paid much attention to the details of founding ceremonies.

Who would have thought Wu Yao would use the nation-founding ceremony as an opportunity to undergo the Immortal Ascension Tribulation?

Originally, the Nightmare Supreme Lord prided himself on his status as a half-immortal and believed that it was by chance that he was defeated by Wu Yao and the Imperial Preceptor the first time. He trusted that he still had the opportunity to stage a comeback.

But he never expected Wu Yao might have become an immortal. The mere possibility was enough to make him back down, not even daring to test the waters.

If I test the waters, it’ll give Wu Yao an opportunity to capture me instead; the gains don’t compensate for the losses. I might as well enter a deep slumber and collect different dreams through various eras, eventually becoming an immortal myself.

Unfortunately, my plans are cut short—I’ve become a prisoner, even at the risk of losing my physical body.

“Wu Yao became an immortal?” Yun Zhi was slightly puzzled.

If this is true, it begets another question.

Half-immortals in slumber have only woken now because their lifespans are limited. But an immortal’s lifespan is infinite—there’s no need for slumber. If Wu Yao became an immortal, how could he have stood by and watched the destruction of Great Yu, with Great Xia replacing it?

After all, during the late Great Yu era, the strongest was the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, who is currently confined next door. There wasn’t even a single immortal. With absolute power, Wu Yao could have prolonged the Great Yu Dynasty.

But he didn’t. Why?

He didn’t even act under such circumstances, which implies that he had ulterior motives. It’s just that his goals remain unknown for now.

An immortal hiding in the shadows was horrible news for Great Xia. Even these two half-immortals before them could wreak havoc, let alone immortals.

“What was Wu Yao’s Dao Fruit?” Since Wu Yao was identified as a hidden enemy, understanding him was crucial for planning their next step.

“I don’t know his Dao Fruit, only his Incipient Dao Fruit,” the Nightmare Supreme Lord replied truthfully.

“Tell me.”

“His Incipient Dao Fruit was called the Replacement Incipient Dao Fruit. It can be understood as equivalent exchange or sacrifice. Through exchanges, he could obtain tangible things like magical treasures, spirit plants, or a powerful attack, or intangible things like destiny and karma. It’s very complex to use.

“After it became a Dao Fruit, I don’t know what level he achieved.”

“What techniques and moves did Wu Yao possess?”

“He knew a lot, and they were flashy. Even within dreams, he could fight me for several rounds by relying on those moves.

“For example, the Qimen Liujia Technique could command supernatural beings, pray for ghosts to be exorcised, and divine the past, present, and future.

“Another was Upright Without Shadow, where entering a void ethereal-like state could nullify all attacks. Its effects were comparable to that of an Immaculate Immortal Physique that achieved major success.

“And there was the Buddhist Six Divine Abilities. I recall him using the Heavenly Eye Ability, Heavenly Ear Ability, and the Divine Foot Ability. As for whether he knew the remaining three, I have no idea.

“Oh, right, right! He could also deploy the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array. Once he activated it, any living being under it would involuntarily submit. Even I fell for it once myself. It’s incredibly powerful.

“Rumor has it that this sword array was inspired from ancient immortal techniques and has a shockingly great origin.”

Yun Zhi, “...”

~~~

Outside, news of the battle in Chunjiang City spread throughout the cultivation world at terrifying speeds.

The city disappearing and reappearing was an unconcealable fact. Hearing about the appearance of two archaic supreme lords and their fierce battle made people’s scalps tingle. Formidable historical figures recorded in texts coming to life felt like time flowing backward, creating a sense of disorientation that attracted the attention of many.

Furthermore, the Heavenly Court Creed’s most mysterious Creed Leader Yun had finally made a move, fighting one against two and displaying power beyond the half-immortal level!

Creed Leader Yun was actually an immortal!

Due to the immortal trait, no one could remember the details of the battles. However, the memory of her appearance and her defeat of the two archaic supreme lords remained.

In the streets, alleys, teahouses, and restaurants, anyone with cultivation discussed the event.

The Refreshing Heart Restaurant was the largest restaurant in several nearby cities. It was overseen by a Nascent Soul spirit chef. Their signature dish “Cool Breeze Ballad” was unparalleled, its fragrance wafting for ten li.

In the past, patrons would eagerly pick up their chopsticks once dishes were served. But today, even after the dishes were served, the cultivators at the table continued fervently discussing the events in Chunjiang City.

“Have you heard about the incident at Chunjiang City? Something big happened!”

“Who doesn’t know about Chunjiang City? It was a battle between two half-immortals! Someone checked historical texts and confirmed they were the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord!”

An uninformed cultivator gasped upon hearing the names, not even noticing the food on the table. “Heavens! The Nightmare Supreme Lord who destroyed the Great Qian Dynasty? And the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord is the one who contended with our old ancestor for supremacy?”

“It’s precisely those two! They moved Chunjiang City to another space, then fought for some reason. Even the seasoned Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the One-Qi Venerable Lord of the Qi-Commanding Sect was not a match!”

“So who won between them?”

The person telling the story shook his head and stopped. “Lend me your magical treasure for two days.”

The person listening to the story was impatient. He didn’t want to lend his magical treasure but was eager to hear the rest of the story. After a moment of hesitation, he gritted his teeth. “Fine, I’ll lend it!”

“Neither of them won.”

“How is that possible?”

“How is that not possible? It’s because the Heavenly Court Creed intervened.”

“Was it Dou Heavenly Sovereign? Only a suspected immortal like Dou Heavenly Sovereign could stop a battle between two supreme lords, right?”

This time, the person telling the story didn’t keep his listeners in suspense. “It was the Heavenly Court Creed’s Creed Leader Yun! Although the details of the battle weren’t circulated, it’s certain that Creed Leader Yun captured the two supreme lords alive!”

The cultivators at the table were stunned, stammering. “This...this can’t be! Unless Creed Leader Yun is...is...”

“An immortal!” another companion yelled.

“Doesn’t that mean the Heavenly Court Creed has two immortals?”

A cultivator swallowed hard. “Dang, as expected of a major force from ancient times, producing two immortals at once!”

“You don’t say! Some are now saying the Heavenly Court Creed is the current number one faction.”

In a corner, three guests leisurely enjoyed the signature dish “Cool Breeze Ballad,” as if they hadn’t heard the discussions.

“Senior, is the meal to your satisfaction?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest inquired gingerly. Beside him, Chieftain Jin looked at Jiang Lianyi expectantly.

Jiang Lianyi wiped her lips and commented indifferently, “Average. It’s not as good as my cooking.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest lamented about his hardships inwardly. Jiang Lianyi had been following them since she beat them up, but they didn’t dare shake her off or drive her away. They hadn’t been able to embark on their grand deception undertaking for a long time.

Among the three, only Chieftain Jin was flabbergasted by the fact that “Creed Leader Yun is an immortal.” But since Jiang Lianyi didn’t care, he didn’t dare to show too much interest either.

Having fought Yun Zhi to a “draw,” how could Jiang Lianyi not know Yun Zhi’s cultivation level?

“What a pity. Not following Senior Brother Lu Yang back then meant missing the chance to fight half-immortals from later eras.”

Chapter 684: Transcendence and Omniscience

At Heaven’s Gate Peak, the exquisite, mellifluous notes of a qin drifted elegantly, like a babbling brook flowing by one’s ears. It was ethereal and light, as if floating amidst soft clouds. An indescribable sense of comfort permeated every meridian.

Lu Yang lay lazily in the grass, hands behind his head, and a blade of foxtail grass between his teeth. Listening to Gan Tian’s qin melody, he felt the fatigue from his trip to Chunjiang City nearly vanish. While listening, he picked a lotus seed from a plate and tossed it into his mouth.

A connoisseur would recognize these as lotus seeds from the Twin Lotus Flower. The Twins River’s surface was covered with them, and Lu Yang had picked several lotus seed heads before leaving.

Gan Tian was truly a cultivator proficient in music. Lu Yang had no expertise in this area and couldn’t distinguish the five notes of the Chinese pentatonic scale,[1] but from a layman’s perspective, it sounded wonderfully soothing.

“Senior Sister, what is the name of this melody you’re playing?”

Gan Tian smoothed her hand over the qin strings, and the music faded, the surroundings returning to silence. “This is an ancient melody bestowed upon me by Senior Lianyi. It’s called Phoenix Rests by the Brook. Senior composed it when she was resting by a stream and felt inspired.”

Jiang Lianyi used a jade flute as her weapon and was unmatched in the domain of music. Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who competed for first in everything, had to concede defeat.

“Senior Sister, how did you become our shifu’s disciple back then?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

Gan Tian sighed, which was rare for her. “My parents were only Golden Core cultivators and didn’t know much about our sect. The entrance trials back then were organized by our shifu. He saw my exceptional talent and wanted to take me as his disciple.

“At the time, I didn’t know what kind of person our shifu was, only that he was the sect leader. Since the sect leader wanted me as his disciple, I was naturally willing.

“Who would have thought... after just two lessons, the teaching location changed.”

“Where did it change to?”

“The prison. At that time, Big Senior Sister was in seclusion, and Second Senior Brother had entered the Buddhist Kingdom. I could only attend lessons with our shifu during visiting hours in prison. Studying was truly arduous. The prisoners back then praised me for being a filial daughter.

“Fortunately, Big Senior Sister emerged from seclusion later, and the learning environment improved significantly.”

“Did Big Senior Sister teach you?”

Gan Tian shook her head. “Big Senior Sister acted as a guarantor and fished Shifu out of prison. She isn’t adept at music and couldn’t teach me.”

“Our shifu knows music too?”

“Yes, and at a higher level than mine. He could sing while plucking his sword. His voice varied greatly and could even imitate various instruments. I heard he developed this skill when performing pingshu performances in his youth, telling stories while playing accompaniment to liven things up.”

Lu Yang didn’t expect his shifu’s abilities to be so extensive.

Gan Tian resumed playing, and Lu Yang enjoyed the music until a discordant voice disrupted his peaceful mental state.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snorted coldly, feeling that Lu Yang underestimated her. “Who says this immortal doesn’t know music? My repertoire invigorates the spirit.”

“Immortal Fairy, thou know music too? I’ve never heard thee play though?” Considering the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had just found the Twins River and was in high spirits, Lu Yang temporarily showed her more respect, switching from “you” to the honorific “thee” and “thou.”[2]

“A mere Nascent Soul cultivator like you isn’t qualified to listen to this immortal’s music. When I perform, no immortal artifacts are used. The rhythms of Dao serve as strings, shaking heaven and earth, resonating with the Great Dao, imposing and unparalleled through the ages. Anyone who hears it will tremble with excitement.”

Lu Yang grew even more curious. “Then how do you perform?”

“Self-detonation.”

“...No wonder they tremble.

“Speaking of which, Immortal Fairy, didn’t you have time to self-detonate when you were assassinated?”

Given the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s nature, her first reaction should have been self-detonation—capable of injuring the attacker and preserving her life.

“Now that you mention it, you have a point. Why didn’t this immortal self-detonate?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, trying to recall the events, but it remained a blur. Was it due to the mastermind’s tricks, or was my condition off then?

“Damn it! If nothing had happened to this immortal, I would have already broken through beyond the level of immortals! The Nine-Layers Immortal was the first immortal; it’s my turn to be the first for once.”

Hearing this topic, Lu Yang perked up, forgetting to eat the lotus seed at his lips. “Are you referring to what you mentioned before—about severing all karma to advance a step further in cultivation and reach the realm beyond immortals?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “That’s the theory from the Nine-Layers Immortal and the others. What I advocate is that the more the karma, the higher the cultivation, thereby enabling breakthroughs.

“According to their theory, the realm beyond immortals is called ‘Transcendence’—untouched by all karma and surpassing all existence.

“According to this immortal’s theory, the realm beyond immortals is called ‘Omniscience’—connected to all things in the world, achieving omniscience and omnipotence. It perfectly matches my intelligence and capabilities!”

Lu Yang sized up the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. After returning to the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Mahavira Hall in his mental space had vanished, reverting to a plain room. As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained the realm above immortals, she was rolling around, her hair disheveled, her clothes unkempt, while giggling loudly. It’s hard to associate her current appearance with terms such as “intelligent” or “omniscient.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grabbed her little feet, then bolted upright into a cross-legged position, swaying like a roly-poly toy. “If only my cultivation insights were still around; maybe reading them would help me recall what happened back then.

“By the way, I suggest you take that plate and run far away. You might save the lotus seeds that way,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly said.

Lu Yang froze. “What do you mean?”

The qin music stopped, and Gan Tian suddenly said to Lu Yang, “Little Junior Brother, quickly leave this area. Your senior sister is about to break through.”

As she spoke, dark clouds gathered above Heaven’s Gate Peak, and faint sounds of thunder rumbled.

Lu Yang immediately reacted. Third Senior Sister is breaking through the Void Refinement Stage. This is the tribulation lightning she attracted!

After the Nascent Soul Stage, every breakthrough at subsequent realms would attract lightning tribulations. This was a rule established by the Heaven Mandate Immortal!

Run!

Without another word, Lu Yang sprinted down the mountain, not even bothering about the lotus seeds on the plate.

Having just seen the Immortals’ Quotes, he now feared encountering lightning tribulations the most!

Lu Yang ran fast, but the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was faster, overtaking him in the blink of an eye.

Lu Yang, “...”

When the Unbeatable Nascent Soul reached the foot of the mountain and stopped fleeing, Lu Yang also halted in his tracks. This means the Unbeatable Nascent Soul deems this the safest spot.

“Why the sudden breakthrough?”

“It’s not exactly sudden. This lass was playing Phoenix Rests by the Brook given by Lianyi. Unlike this immortal’s self-detonation, this is a melody that calms one’s mental state. The Void Refinement Stage fluctuates, and this music is perfect for stabilizing one’s realm. Along with her originally being on the verge of a breakthrough, it’s logical that it’s happening now.”

1. This is the pentatonic scale used in ancient Chinese music. The notes are gong, shang, jue, zheng, yu, which roughly correspond to the western do, re, mi, sol, la. There are more nuances to this, so those who are interested in music can definitely look up the musicology! ☜

2. As you might have already guessed from the context, but there are two versions of “you” in Chinese. Normally, people use “你”, which is why the Chinese greeting you’ve heard is probably “nihao.” However, in formal situations or when you are speaking to a person of a higher status (e.g., age, seniority, position) or simply trying to be polite (i.e. with clients/customers), people would use “您” instead, or “nin.” There are other languages with a similar system too. ☜

Chapter 685: Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye

“Someone is about to break through?”

“Judging by the direction of the tribulation clouds, is that Heaven’s Gate Peak?”

“Is Big Senior Sister about to break through?”

“What nonsense! How could Big Senior Sister’s breakthrough cause such a small commotion?”

“Is it the sect leader then?”

“How long has the sect leader been gone?”

“Junior Brother Lu... No, that’s not right either. He just broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage.”

“It’s Senior Sister Gan Tian!”

In the Dao-Seeking Sect, disciples and elders noticed the tribulation clouds above Heaven’s Gate Peak. The River Spirit peeked out from the water, looked up at Heaven’s Gate Peak, and temporarily opened a gap in the Great Sect Defense Array to allow the lightning tribulation to pass through.

With the Great Sect Defense Array active, the lightning tribulation would strike the array, not Gan Tian. This counted as external interference, which could cause the lightning tribulation’s power to grow, potentially damaging the array.

Lu Yang recalled his Unbeatable Nascent Soul, having no choice but to admit that this little thing was fast. Even at full speed, he couldn’t catch up, regrettably ending up second.

Gradually, a crowd gathered at the foot of Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Even if they were in the Dao-Seeking Sect, witnessing a Void Refinement cultivator’s lightning tribulation was rare. Every time it happened, it would draw crowds of people interested in observing and learning.

“Junior Brother Lu, who is breaking through?”

“Third Senior Sister.”

“So it really is Senior Sister Gan Tian.”

The disciples, elders, and even a lamb skewer vendor eventually arrived.

“This is the fifth disciple to reach the Fusion Stage, right?” Fourth Elder smiled.

The other four were Yun Zhi, Ye Zijin, Dai Bufan, and Fourth Elder’s eldest disciple, Ji Hongwen.

“Whoa, so spectacular! Even my uncle’s breakthrough from the Void Refinement Stage wasn’t this grand,” Meng Jingzhou marveled. He had seen his uncle break through from the Void Refinement to the Fusion stage, but he was young then and had only caught the gist, not even understanding the type of lightning tribulation.

He was halfway through recounting his amazing adventures in Chunjiang City to the old horse when he noticed the situation at Heaven’s Gate Peak and rushed over to watch the spectacle.

A deep and unfathomable voice sounded behind Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “I was just looking for you two.”

They spun around to see Dai Bufan, who wore a strained smile.

Heavens knew how Dai Bufan felt upon hearing the news about Chunjiang City. It was only twenty li from the black market I had told Meng Jingzhou about!

And yet you promised with such conviction that you wouldn’t cause trouble for six months?

That said, after Dai Bufan finished reading the report, he knew he couldn’t truly blame the two.

But aren’t you two too good at stirring up trouble?

“Make sure to behave for a while. The recruitment for new disciples is in a few months. You need to become role models,” Dai Bufan warned them.

The two “honest” individuals nodded vigorously.

“Look, the lightning tribulation is descending!” Lu Yang pointed at the sky and shouted.

Bluish-purple tribulation lightning surged like raging waves and slanted down as a dark mass. Even space warped, contorting like mahua (fried dough twist).[1]

Gan Tian stood directly below the lightning tribulation, not moving an inch and not even removing her eyepatch.

Dai Bufan commented by the side, “Junior Sister Gan is very confident. Her eyes are unique; they’re a major lethal weapon. Not removing her eyepatch during the lightning tribulation indicates she plans to tough it out.”

“What’s special about Third Senior Sister’s eyes?” Lu Yang asked.

“That’s the legendary Immortal Dao Heavenly eye. They’re said to be eyes only immortals possess. It can see through the true forms of demons and ghosts and shoot forth golden light that splits mountains, cracks stones, and parts waves. As for what other mysteries it holds, I don’t know.”

“Immortal Fairy, have you heard of the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye?” After asking Dai Bufan, Lu Yang turned to ask the great Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“This Dai fellow is right. She does possess the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye, though calling it an immortal’s eye is an exaggeration. What cultivation level is this lass at? Her body can’t withstand an immortal’s eye.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had known about Gan Tian’s eyes since meeting her. Merely covering the eyes with a black cloth couldn’t evade an immortal’s senses.

“The Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye is indeed extraordinary. You can think of it as a special constitution, like an immortal physique. Cultivators who possess it are truly powerful.”

As they spoke, the lightning tribulation descended. Without relying on any magical treasures, Gan Tian resisted the lightning tribulation with her physical body, the crackling sounds causing Lu Yang’s scalp to tingle.

“This is the best way to undergo tribulations. Using magical treasures is the inferior option; leveraging the lightning tribulation to temper the body is the proper path—at least, that’s how the Heaven Mandate Immortal designed it back then.”

The power of the lightning tribulation suddenly spiked. Gan Tian was caught off guard, and blood trickled from her lips before it was quickly drowned in the lightning.

Fortunately, that wave passed. The surge was a sign that the lightning tribulation was nearing its conclusion.

“Be careful, there’s a second wave!”

An azure dragon formed from lightning coiled in the air. Its five talons were incredibly sharp, easily shattering space by lightly clenching them.

Dai Bufan’s expression was plagued with worry. “Oh no, this should be the Nine Heavens Azure Dragon Tribulation. Rumor says it’s a lightning tribulation that heaven and earth modeled after the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.”

This implied that the Dragon Ancient Ancestor was so formidable that her power was recognized by heaven and earth, leaving an eternal imprint on the world.

In fact, Lu Yang knew that it wasn’t recognition from heaven and earth. The Heaven Mandate Immortal had simply used his younger sister-in-law as a reference for lightning tribulations.

The world wasn’t aware that the Heaven Mandate Immortal controlled lightning tribulations and assumed they were trials from heaven and earth. Admittedly, this theory must have pleased the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Suddenly, a golden phoenix emerged, as if born from the music. It soared up to clash with the Nine Heavens Azure Dragon.

The sight elicited exclamations from the crowd. “Dragon and phoenix contending! This is a marvel that hasn’t been witnessed in millennia!”

“Is this what Senior Sister Gan Tian gained in the Demon Region?”

“Cultivation has always had symbolism. Does this mean Senior Sister Gan Tian will soar like the dragon and phoenix, becoming a supreme existence in this world?”

“That’s very likely!”

Lu Yang watched silently, offering no comment.

To him, it looked less like a contention between a dragon and a phoenix but more like a feud between the Qilin Immortal’s wives.

The battle between dragon and phoenix concluded, and both vanished.

The lightning tribulation gave Gan Tian no chance of respite. Black lightning resembling a cage descended, sealing off Gan Tian’s escape routes.

“A prison has descended! Oh no, this is the Heart Devil Tribulation!” Dai Bufan’s expression changed. During such a tribulation, a cage will cut off one’s means of retreat, forcing one to overcome it!

Dai Bufan watched Gan Tian with deep concern. The latter was trapped in the Heart Devil Tribulation. The Heart Devil Tribulation isolates all information from the external world, and no reminders can be given. She can only rely on herself!

“Senior Brother, what is the Heart Devil Tribulation like?” Lu Yang hadn’t experienced one before.

Dai Bufan replied solemnly, “During the Heart Devil Tribulation, your beloved ones will appear—perhaps it might be your best friend, your Dao partner, your elder, or someone you can’t let go of. Even if you recognize them as heart devils, they seem no different from the real person, and you will still find it hard to strike!”

The heart devil’s form gradually manifested within the prison cage.

It held a horsetail whisk and exuded the ethereal and dignified air of an immortal, carrying the bearing of a lofty expert.

“Shifu?” Lu Yang’s expression turned odd. Why does Shifu appearing in prison not feel out of place?

“I wonder if Third Senior Sister can bring herself to strike Shifu.”

Just as Lu Yang was worried for Gan Tian, she showed not the slightest bit of hesitation. Grabbing her guqin, she smashed it toward the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Then, she removed her eyepatch, revealing sacred, profound eyes that shot forth golden light!

1. Mahua is a Chinese snack fried in peanut oil, and it can be sweet or savory. Its origin can be traced back several thousand years. It was invented as a tasty snack that was easy to make and preserve. There are many variations of mahua today, and various provinces are known for their different mahua versions. You could even find museums about mahua. ☜

Chapter 686: True Lord Gan Tian

In the sky above Heaven’s Gate Peak, Gan Tian didn’t hold back at all. She hadn’t activated the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye in the Demon Region, but it blazed forth the instant she laid eyes on the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Boom!

The heart devil incarnation of the Taciturn Daoist Priest had no time to react before a golden beam shot from the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye sheared off one of his arms, drastically reducing his combat power.

Gan Tian pressed her advantage, her beautiful eyes now as crimson as blood—a sign that the Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye was pushed to its limit.

A thicker and sharper golden light burst forth. The heart devil incarnation of the Taciturn Daoist Priest hastily rolled to the side, but Gan Tian jerked her head, maintaining the relentless assault.

“Hiss—” Observing from below, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou inhaled a cold breath of air. Third Senior Sister really doesn’t hold back.

“No wonder Third Senior Sister dared to roam the Demon Region alone. With a move like that, few Fusion cultivators would probably dare to face her head-on.”

Behind them, Fourth Elder lamented. “This is the benefit of being Old Nine’s disciple—there’s no reason to hold back when facing a Heart Devil Tribulation. This was also how Ye Zijin underwent his tribulation back then.

“But speaking of which, this Immortal Dao Heavenly Eye is genuinely powerful. A special constitution comparable to an immortal physique truly cannot be underestimated.”

The Heart Devil Tribulation stood as a tremendous obstacle before all cultivators, yet one need not fear it as long as they were a disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Although heart devils could sometimes manifest as one’s parents, Gan Tian’s parents were merely at the Golden Core Stage. Having them exhibit Fusion Stage power during the tribulation would appear blatantly fake, making them unsuitable to be part of the test.

Lu Yang, “...”

I no longer fear Shifu appearing in my Heart Devil Tribulation; I fear that the one appearing won’t be Shifu.

“I didn’t expect Third Junior Sister’s heart devil to be Shifu, just like Second Junior Brother’s.” Yun Zhi’s voice rang beside Lu Yang, startling him.

“Big Senior Sister, why are you here?”

Yun Zhi looked at him with a slightly peculiar expression. “Third Junior Sister is undergoing her tribulation. I naturally came to watch.”

“Have you finished interrogating the two half-immortals?”

“Not yet. Those two know many secrets; the interrogation won’t be over so quickly. However, we’ve already gained much. For example, we’ve identified the owner of the Immortal-Exterminating Immortal Array you learned.”

“Who was it?” Lu Yang recalled that Yun Zhi had beaten the sword array’s owner to death. Given the circumstances at the time, capturing him alive was challenging, leaving her no choice but to kill him, so his identity had remained unknown until now.

“The first Yu Emperor, Wu Yao.”

“Wut?” Lu Yang’s mind went blank for a moment.

Mistaking that Lu Yang hadn’t heard clearly, Yun Zhi repeated herself. “The first Yu Emperor, Wu Yao.”

Lu Yang had heard it perfectly well; he simply couldn’t process it immediately.

The founding emperor of Great Yu was quietly beaten to death by Big Senior Sister just like that?

Don’t you find that too disgraceful for an immortal?

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is better than you.

“Senior Brother Lu, Senior Brother Meng, it’s been a long time.” A pleasant voice tinged with joy sounded.

Turning around, they saw it was Tao Yaoye.

“Junior Sister Tao, it’s been a while.”

It had indeed been a long time. From the start of their journey to the Demon Region to the conclusion of the battle in Chunjiang City, over half a year had passed without them meeting.

Cultivation knows no time—this was truly not an empty phrase.

Tao Yaoye had become more beautiful. Graceful, slender, and with a tenderness similar to flowing water, she wore a sweet smile, resembling an immortal fairy banished from heaven. Just by standing there alone, she formed a picturesque scene.

“Have you had any results with comprehending the Metamorphic Immortal Physique?” Lu Yang remembered inviting Tao Yaoye before the trip to the Demon Region, but she had been at a critical juncture in comprehending the Metamorphic Immortal Physique and couldn’t leave.

Now, it appeared she had not only succeeded in comprehending the Metamorphic Immortal Physique but had also broken through to the Nascent Soul Stage. Her entire demeanor was different from before.

Tao Yaoye was delighted that Lu Yang noticed the changes in her, her eyes curving into happy crescents. “That’s right.”

Since she heard of Lu Yang’s return from the Demon Region, she had been wanting to meet him but found no opportunity until Gan Tian’s tribulation drew a crowd of disciples.

The Metamorphic Immortal Physique was an immortal body that allowed its bearer to borrow power from their future self. During this process, one’s body would undergo a transformation, becoming pure, sacred, and immortal-like. In the early days of the establishment of the cultivation system, when someone with a Metamorphic Immortal Physique borrowed power from the future, light rays would coalesce into feathers around them, as if they were becoming an immortal. The ancient forebears termed this process “feathered metamorphic ascension,” hence the name “Metamorphic Immortal Physique.”

However, such “feathered metamorphosis” came at a price. Apart from entering a prolonged period of weakness afterward, since one was borrowing power from their future self, that future self in that specific moment would become frail. If that particular future self happened to be in a battle, it would spell certain death. Therefore, bearers of the Metamorphic Immortal Physique throughout history wouldn’t deploy this move lightly.

“This lass’ talent is not bad. I reckon she’s stronger than that Metamorphic Immortal Physique I encountered back in my day.”

“Immortal Fairy, you’ve encountered one too?” Lu Yang pondered and found it reasonable. In the glorious ancient era, with countless prodigies competing, all manner of constitutions would emerge.

“Of course! That fellow was a Holy Son from some sacred ground. I can’t remember the name. He looked presentable, but his methods were really underhanded. He saw my rising fame and wanted to step over me to spread his reputation.

“It turned out it was all big talk. I utterly trounced him. Seeing he was no match for me, he lost his cool and activated his Metamorphic Immortal Physique, borrowing power from his future self. His cultivation realm skyrocketed from the Apex Nascent Soul Stage straight to the Void Refinement Stage!”

Lu Yang, “...”

I don’t need the Immortal Fairy to continue to roughly guess what happened next.

During the time they spent catching up, the heart devil incarnation of the Taciturn Daoist Priest was defeated. The tribulation lightning dissipated, and Gan Tian’s cultivation realm stabilized at the Fusion Stage.

She had become the fifth disciple to become a Fusion expert.

Witnessing her achievement, everyone offered their congratulations.

Dai Bufan stepped forward, cupping his hands. “Congratulations, Junior Sister Gan Tian! From now on, we can address you as True Lord Gan!”

“Senior Sister Gan Tian is impressive!”

“Senior Sister Gan, you’re so amazing!”

“Senior Sister, your eyes can shoot light!”

Gan Tian thanked each of them in turn, remaining humble and unflustered as she put the blindfold over her eyes again.

Yun Zhi stepped in front of Gan Tian. “Alright, that’s enough. Third Junior Sister has just broken through and needs peace to consolidate her cultivation realm.”

Her voice was not loud, but who would dare not listen? After offering their congratulations, the crowd obediently dispersed.

Seeing that Gan Tian had successfully weathered her tribulation without any incidents, the various elders also departed.

With the tribulation ended, the River Spirit closed the gap it had opened in the Great Sect Defense Array.

“What a pity about this qin.” Gan Tian stroked the charred guqin, her heart somewhat aching. It had been struck several times by lightning when she used it to deal with the heart devil, and its strings had snapped.

“It’s fine. Since you’ve reached the Fusion Stage, I will find suitable materials another time and refine a new one for you as a congratulatory gift,” Yun Zhi said calmly.

The two supreme lords had disclosed the locations of their hidden treasure sites. The collections of half-immortals were incredibly bountiful, so there would definitely be materials within that were far more suitable for crafting a guqin.

In truth, the best material for crafting a guqin was the Epoch Immortal, but Yun Zhi felt that would be somewhat disrespectful to the remains of this senior, so she didn’t mention it.

Chapter 687: Inverting Yin and Yang, Defying Heaven Changing Fate!

“Why don’t we break off a branch from the Epoch Immortal’s body to refine the qin?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proposed. Naturally, she had conveyed this through an auditory message; Gan Tian was still not privy to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

The Epoch Immortal’s original form was colossal, resulting in much thicker branches and leaves.

“Wouldn’t that be somewhat disrespectful to the Epoch Immortal?” Yun Zhi hesitated slightly.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t bothered in the least. “Aiya, what respect? The Epoch Immortal often used parts of his body for refining artifacts. Branches and leaves were the Epoch Immortal’s hair. Plucking a single strand for refining artifacts is nothing. He would use his own body for artifact refinement, whether he had a reason or not.”

When it came to the best artifact refinement materials, it still had to be the Epoch Immortal. As the most ancient existence between heaven and earth, what material could surpass his body?

“The Nine-Layers Immortal also considered using his body for artifact refinement. He wielded the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, after all. Yin and yang represent change. When yin and yang harmonize, the Dao gives birth to the infinite, orchestrating creation. He could use the power of his Dao Fruit to create people.

“Originally, he wanted to pull out one of his own ribs to create a person. But then he became troubled, contemplating whether the person created this way would be his younger sibling or child. In the end, he abandoned the idea.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Were you people in the ancient era all this fierce and boorish?

“Eh, now that you mention it, this immortal might have a way to improve the Meng boy’s situation.” Something seemed to have sparked in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Improve what?”

“Have you heard of ‘Inverting Yin and Yang, Defying Heaven Changing Fate?”

Lu Yang had a vague impression of it. It seems to be an impressive divine ability.

“Correct. It’s a divine ability capable of defying heaven to alter one’s destiny. However, it can only be used on oneself, not on others. If the Meng boy masters this technique, he might be able to change his Single’s Spirit Root constitution and perhaps even improve his luck.”

“Immortal Fairy, you know it?”

“Of course, I do. How about this? I’ll teach it to both of you. Whether you can master it will depend on your capabilities.”

Hearing that he had the opportunity to learn such a great divine ability, Lu Yang couldn’t keep the grin off his face.

Lu Yang relayed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s idea to Yun Zhi, who also found it feasible. The only issue was the extreme difficulty in learning this particular divine ability—it wasn’t something Nascent Soul cultivators could master.

“We can give it a try. Senior, could you describe how you perform this move? Let’s compare our methods.” Yun Zhi also knew this technique, but she hadn’t considered the possibility of applying it to Meng Jingzhou.

“Alright.”

The two briefly communicated through auditory messages. Yun Zhi confirmed that their divine abilities were the same, and only then could she rest reassured.

After Gan Tian reached the Fusion Stage, she went into seclusion to consolidate her cultivation realm. Heaven’s Gate Peak was only left with Yun Zhi, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou, who had left with the crowd but was later called back by Lu Yang.

Upon hearing this news, Meng Jingzhou was over the moon.

Heaven must have pitied me; is it finally my turn to defy fate and change my destiny?

Lu Yang said earnestly, “If you feel grateful, you can kowtow to me twice. I’ll accept it on the Immortal Fairy’s behalf.”

“Get lost.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy drifted out from Lu Yang, her expression serene and peaceful, akin to an immortal from one’s imagination.

She formed an orchid hand gesture[1] by pinching her fingers and spoke unhurriedly. “This immortal sees your extraordinary talent and that you are destined for greatness. I hereby bestow upon you a wisp of immortal affinity today. Whether you can grasp it depends on your providence.”

“I, Meng Jingzhou, thank the Immortal!”

At the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi had temporarily postponed returning to Incarceration Peak to resume the interrogation, instead observing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s teaching process.

“Inverting yin and yang can cause heaven and earth to lose their order and the sun and moon to lose their regularity. It is akin to inverting right and wrong and mixing black and white. Even among divine abilities, it ranks as one of the top few supremely powerful techniques. If you two wish to learn it, you must prepare yourselves mentally...

“Having the mind and spirit within the heart is the key to mastering this move. To overcome fate, one must first believe in fate...

“When you learn the rudiments of inverting yin and yang, you can only transform a part, perfect for transforming your Pure Yang Spirit Root into a Yin-Yang Spirit Root...

“Beware of using excessive force when executing this move; otherwise, you might transform your Pure Yang Spirit Root into a Pure Yin Spirit Root...”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were extremely well-behaved, sitting obediently on the ground listening, striving to memorize every word the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said.

“In fact, if you wish to learn how to invert yin and yang, the best reference is right before your eyes.”

“What is it?” the two asked simultaneously.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed overhead. “It’s the sun.

“Daytime is yang, nighttime is yin. Whether it’s the alternation of the sun and moon in our era or the changes of the sun and moon now, they are the best examples of inverting yin and yang. It’s a pity few in the world can comprehend this.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sighed, as if lamenting the ignorance of the world.

Meng Jingzhou seized the chance to butter her up. “That’s why you’re an immortal, Senior—you can comprehend what ordinary people cannot.”

“Oh, this immortal didn’t comprehend it either. The Nine-Layers Immortal was the one who told us this principle.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

It took a full day for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to properly explain the principles of this divine ability.

“I’ve explained all the principles. As for whether you can comprehend them, that depends on your providence. I suggest you observe intently during the transition between the sun and the moon. It will aid you in learning this divine ability.”

“Understood,” the two chorused in unison.

For the next few days, the two did nothing else but focus solely on studying and comprehending according to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s method.

Inverting Yin and Yang, Defying Heaven Changing Fate lived up to its reputation as a top-ranked divine ability. Even with Lu Yang’s talent, he couldn’t master it immediately.

On the dawn of the fifth day, during the transition between the sun and the moon, the two brothers gazed up at the sky. The argent room, representing Lunar Yin power, shed its original color, donning a veil of crimson. The hue of red deepened and completely dyed the moon red, transforming it into the brilliant great sun representing Solar Yang power.

In that moment, Lu Yang felt an epiphany, as if a pane of paper in his heart had been pierced. He gradually closed his eyes, continuously envisioning the magnificent sight of the sun and moon alternating at dawn and dusk.

A confident smile spread across his face.

I have mastered it.

He felt that his fate profile had changed.

Meng Jingzhou scratched his head in frustration. My talent for spells can be considered first-rate, but learning such an overpowered divine ability is still too hard.

He turned and asked his good brother. “Lu Yin, have you mastered it?”

Lu Yang’s confident smile froze on his face. “...Wait, what did you call me?”

“Lu Yin.[2] Is there a problem?”

Lu Yang quickly turned to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Yun Zhi. “What’s my situation?”

Unlike Meng Jingzhou, both the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Yun Zhi had detected the change in Lu Yang. A mysterious power had shrouded him, altering his name to “Lu Yin,” as if he had been born with that name. Even the name on his identity jade tablet now read “Lu Yin.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head. “Inverting Yin and Yang, Defying Heaven Changing...Name?

“That counts as mastering it...right?”

1. The lanhuazhi is a hand gesture that is typically used in traditional dances. The most common version is where the thumb and middle finger are pinched together, while the rest of the fingers are extended. You can see them in Chinese dances or xiqu (Chinese opera) performances. If you’re curious about other hand gestures, you may refer to this image. ☜

2. The “yang” in Lu Yang’s name is the same as the “yang” in yin and yang and the “yang” in sun. The characters also look somewhat similar. “Yang” is 阳, and “yin” is 阴. ☜

Chapter 688: Karmic Divine Ability

Despite having lived for eighteen years, Lu Yang never imagined a day would come when his name would change.

The spell is a genuine spell, and defying heaven is genuinely heaven-defying.

“Does this count as me having mastered it?” Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously. No matter how I think about it, this seems off.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared with conviction, putting forth her logical arguments, “Why wouldn’t it count? Don’t you know that one’s name represents their destiny? Changing your name is changing your fate. By altering your name, your future destiny will be different.

“Taking a step back, curse techniques are often executed through a name. By changing your name, you alter your karmic ties. You are no longer the you of before. The change in your name on your identity jade tablet is a symbol of this; curse techniques can no longer befall you.”

When a curse technique is activated, it will lock onto the identity “Lu Yang.” After Lu Yang becomes “Lu Yin” and abandons his previous identity, the curse technique will no longer find its target and will naturally not affect him.

Yun Zhi also agreed with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s viewpoint. “Little Junior Brother, although it’s unclear why the effect of your cultivation deviated slightly from the expected outcome, the fact that it directly altered your name at the karmic level proves this technique is indeed a karma-type divine ability.”

Mastering a karma-type divine ability at the Nascent Soul Stage was an unprecedented feat.

Only Meng Jingzhou was completely befuddled. What karma-type divine ability? What mastered?

Did I miss something?

Lu Yang explained, “It’s like this. Weren’t we both cultivating the divine ability Inverting Yin and Yang? I succeeded. Previously, I was called Lu Yang. Now, I am called ‘Lu Yin.’”

“...Wait a moment, let me process this.” Even with Meng Jingzhou’s quick-witted mind, he couldn’t immediately accept this reality.

“So you’re saying that you were previously called ‘Lu Yang,’ and now you’re called ‘Lu Yin,’ and even the name on your identity jade tablet has changed?”

“That’s right.”

Meng Jingzhou inhaled sharply. This spell is too heaven-defying. I didn’t even detect any signs of Lu Yin performing a divine ability.

Yun Zhi stared at Lu Yang for a moment longer before adding, “Little Junior Brother, this move of yours is truly remarkable. It fundamentally altered your own name. If you encounter a Fusion cultivator unfamiliar with karmic arts, you could potentially hoodwink them.”

Karmic and temporal spells were notoriously abstruse and unfathomable. Most cultivators could cultivate diligently for over a decade without seeing any results. Among Fusion cultivators, those who understood karmic divine abilities were exceedingly rare. Even among Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, most only had a rudimentary understanding. Someone like Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor, who formed an Incipient Dao Fruit based on karma, was fairly uncommon.

The prerequisite for possessing an Incipient Dao Fruit was significant accomplishments in the domain of karma, which highlighted the Imperial Preceptor’s superb talent in karma.

After Lu Yang mastered the technique, Yun Zhi stayed for another seven days. During this time, Lu Yang consolidated his learning, while Meng Jingzhou continued his comprehension.

After seven days, Lu Yang found that he had little left to consolidate, whereas Meng Jingzhou found that every aspect of the spell still required deeper comprehension.

Meng Jingzhou was forced to admit he couldn’t master this move. Never mind. Let Lu Yang change his name. This young master doesn’t need a change of name.

Seeing that the two were no longer cultivating, Yun Zhi flew back to Incarceration Peak to resume interrogating the two supreme lords.

~~~

At the headquarters of the Radiant Sun Creed, the walls were adorned with a glowing sun totem, which illuminated the meeting room.

Creed Leader Chi had gathered the higher-ups to discuss major matters. Everyone remained silent, listening to Creed Leader Chi speak.

“I have called everyone here today primarily to discuss two matters.

“First, as all of you know, our creed’s research into the sun’s power has recently stalled. The main reason is that our multiple attempts to land on the sun have resulted in several fellow Daoists being burned to death.”

This was not the sun from the ancient era, which was formed from Jinwu crows. The surface of the current sun was scorching hot. Even though it was shielded by great arrays, one could still feel its terrifying heat. A Fusion cultivator could only endure for a few seconds in such an environment before being reduced to ashes.

If they continued these experiments to land on the sun, the next batch might very well include the higher-ups themselves.

“Therefore, I was wondering if we should switch our approach. Perhaps we could attempt landing on the moon at night? The sun and moon share the same body; we could indirectly research the sun.”

His speech was immediately met with opposition from everyone.

The vice creed leader was the first to step forward and rebuke Creed Leader Chi’s disloyal proposal. “The sun and moon never appear simultaneously, indicating that even if they share the same body, there is a gap between them. Our creed believes in the power of the solar yang; how can we submit to the power of lunar yin? This is absolutely unacceptable!”

An elder expressed his loyalty. “Those fellow Daoists who were burned to death must have lacked sincerity and failed to receive the sun’s approval. I may be an old set of bones, but I have believed in the sun my whole life. I can definitely withstand the trials and set foot upon the sun. How about this? Count me in for the next sun expedition team!”

Creed Leader Chi felt helpless about the fervor of the higher-ups, each more zealous than the other.

I can understand and even respect that you don’t fear death. But if all of you go and immolate yourselves on the sun, who will be left to lead the Radiant Sun Creed?

I knew this suggestion wouldn’t gain everyone’s approval.

“The sun-landing project shall be set aside for now. We’ll be moving on to the second issue.

“The Heavenly Court Creed’s Holy Son, Long Jingzhou, has overwhelming pure yang power, even surpassing that of someone with a Pure Yang Immortal Physique. It’s probably because the ancient Heavenly Court possessed unique methods to groom their members.

“Moreover, I discovered that Long Jingzhou and Young Creed Leader Lu seem to be at loggerheads with each other, likely related to the issue of succession within the ancient Heavenly Court. We can exploit this by secretly winning over Meng Jingzhou and stirring up internal conflict within the Heavenly Court Creed, thereby reaping benefits from the situation!”

One of the elders was puzzled. “How do we do that? The ancient Heavenly Court is immensely powerful and wealthy. They have Dou Heavenly Sovereign, an ancient immortal, and the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, a half-immortal who defeated Supreme Lord Zhu Tian. Threats and coercion are out of the question, and even if we want to entice them, our resources can’t outmatch them.”

Creed Leader Chi shook his head. “You’ve mistaken one thing. It’s the ancient Heavenly Court that is immensely powerful and wealthy, not Long Jingzhou. Within any organization, there exists an uneven distribution of resources. Long Jingzhou undoubtedly receives fewer resources than the Young Creed Leader. This is our opportunity.

“If our entire creed supports Long Jingzhou, wouldn’t that be better than the resources allocated to him by the ancient Heavenly Court?

“Furthermore, we have researched the sun for tens of thousands of years. Our findings are greatly beneficial for cultivation. I refuse to believe Long Jingzhou won’t be tempted.”

The higher-ups felt that Creed Leader Shi made some sense.

“We can give it a try. If we can secretly pull Long Jingzhou to our side, it will facilitate our future operations considerably.”

“Indeed, indeed. We can attempt it.”

While everyone was discussing, Creed Leader Chi’s personal guard hastily burst into the meeting room and handed an intelligence report to him.

The report detailed how Creed Leader Yun had demonstrated her mighty prowess in Chunjiang City, capturing two archaic supreme lords, whose whereabouts were currently unknown.

Creed Leader Chi placed the report down. “The plan to reap benefits by stirring up internal conflict within the Heavenly Court Creed is hereby void. We’ll change the second discussion topic.”

The higher-ups turned their gazes toward Creed Leader Chi at once.

Creed Leader Shi said earnestly, “Should our Radiant Sun Creed consider joining the Heavenly Court Creed?”

Chapter 689: Creed Leader Chi

The moment Creed Leader Chi saw the intelligence report, while his expression remained neutral, he was inwardly breaking out in a cold sweat.

So the Creed Leader Yun we met at the barbeque shop is actually an immortal. This implies that the Heavenly Court Creed has two ancient immortals.

What’s the point of trying to sow discord within the Heavenly Court Creed to reap benefits? We should just join them directly.
