Now that the Nine-Netherworlds Creed is wholeheartedly focused on barbeque, there is a lack of distractions to divert the imperial court’s attention. Our Radiant Sun Creed was nearly discovered by the imperial court during several operations.

If this goes on, getting exposed is inevitable.

Creed Leader Chi made copies of the report and distributed them, letting the higher-ups of the creed understand the true strength of the Heavenly Court Creed.

With two immortals presiding, they can even overturn Great Xia. They’re on a completely different level compared to a diabolic creed like ours, which is constantly hounded by Great Xia.

The Radiant Sun Creeds were clearly shocked by Creed Leader Yun’s might. This was simply not a force they were qualified to scheme against.

We’d likely be wiped out without a trace of our souls remaining before we even start plotting our schemes.

“Another immortal... The ancient Heavenly Court is truly terrifying.”

“Remember the Phoenix Ancestor? She is one of the Four Regents, which implies the other three are also half-immortals.”

“I heard from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed that the ancient Heavenly Court’s enemies were the Four Ancient Immortals. If that’s not a lie, it’s likely the ancient Heavenly Court has methods yet to be revealed.”

“So we should join the Heavenly Court Creed? Preposterous! Just because they are powerful, we should directly hand over our creed’s foundation and legacy?”

“Do they even believe in the power of the sun? Will they help us spread the faith and make the world revere the sun’s power?”

“It’s not directly handing it over! We’re just seeking protection; it’s not as severe as you imagine!”

“No? I’m afraid that when the time comes, it’ll no longer be up to us!”

The higher-ups argued vehemently, each holding their own viewpoint and unwilling to yield.

The most senior elder stroked his beard and said slowly, “The ancient Heavenly Court Creed indeed has its strengths, but that does not mean we must join them. The Radiant Sun Creed has its own pride. How can we live off others? If we submit to the Heavenly Court, whether we become members or canon fodder is up in the air!”

This elder’s speech garnered the agreement of many.

“Indeed, we cannot entrust our destiny to others. Moreover, once we achieve a research breakthrough and make the world believe in the power of the sun, we can emulate the ancient forebears and use the power of faith to grant life to the sun. At that time, with a supreme sun god protecting us, our creed might not necessarily be weaker than the Heavenly Court!”

The founder of the Radiant Sun Creed was an archaeologist. He discovered that in an era more distant than the era of the Four Ancient Immortals, when forebears were exploring the cultivation system, their faith power could bestow life upon the objects of worship, which they called “deities.” This was also the turning point in the research that led to the “Divine Transfiguration Stage.”

From the Radiant Sun Creed’s inception, it had set the goal of drawing power from the sun, propagating its greatness, making the world worship the sun, and transforming it into a true deity.

Creed Leader Chi also felt it made some sense. “Since everyone can’t reach a consensus, perhaps we can each take a step back. Let’s approach the Heavenly Court Creed by making contact with the Holy Son, Long Jingzhou. How about that?”

This time, Creed Leader Chi’s proposal received unanimous agreement from the higher-ups.

~~~

After the meeting adjourned, Creed Leader Chi let out a long sigh. The meeting is finally over.

“I wonder when my days of being creed leader will end.”

When he was still a minor cultivator, his favorite pastime was gazing at the stars and the moon at night. However, his cultivation was too low at the time to see them clearly.

By chance, he discovered that observing objects through two lenses made them appear larger. Based on this discovery, he invented the telescope, which allowed him to see the stars clearly. After applying for a patent, he heard about an astronomy enthusiast group nearby and tracked them down.

Only after joining did he realize it was a damn diabolic creed.

Once someone joined a diabolic creed, there was no breaking free—leaving the sect meant death. He had no choice but to obediently join.

Originally, he wanted to keep a low profile and live out the rest of his life peacefully. However, the higher-ups heard about his invention of the telescope and deemed him a talent, putting much effort into grooming and promoting him rapidly. Before he knew it, he had joined the higher-ups.

As a member of the higher-ups, he thought he would coast along for the rest of his life. However, when it was time to elect a new creed leader, he was unexpectedly elected by a landslide vote. The reason was that his bald head resembled the sun.

Back then, he consoled himself, thinking that becoming creed leader wasn’t so bad—at least no one could keep him in check anymore.

Then, he realized the position of creed leader was a massive trap. Put nicely, he was the creed leader; put bluntly, he was a sacrificial offering.

Whenever the Radiant Sun Creed suffered a major setback, such as failing in sun research or the court raiding several of their bases, the higher-ups would interpret it as a punishment from the sun, requiring the creed leader to perform a sacrificial rite to heaven.

This wasn’t merely the creed leader kowtowing to the sun a few times. It meant the creed leader had to be the sacrifice and personally perform a sacrificial rite to heaven. This was allegedly a custom left by the first creed leader.

Take the sun-landing experiments as an example; if they failed again, the next person sent to land on the sun would likely be him.

His promotion from a higher-up to the creed leader had been too swift. He hadn’t even had time to inquire about how the previous creed leader met his end. Only after becoming the creed leader did he learn that the sun used to dominate the sky and that the stars were mere phantom images. The Radiant Sun Creed had always considered this a symbol of the sun’s greatness.

One day, the stars were suddenly no longer illusions but tangible celestial bodies, and the sun was no longer the sole entity in the sky. This event caused a panic within the Radiant Sun Creed. They deemed it an ill omen and sacrificed the previous creed leader.

After hearing this, Creed Leader Chi was filled with trepidation, fearing the higher-ups might sacrifice him for the same reason. Fortunately, they were somewhat rational and didn’t consecutively sacrifice their creed leaders. The higher-ups were all at the Fusion Stage, with the most veteran elder at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Creed Leader Chi stood no chance of resisting.

During his tenure, he had encountered several major incidents that typically required sacrificing the creed leader. He had survived unscathed because of his own method.

As he had invented the telescope, patent royalties rolled in, providing a substantial source of wealth. According to regulations, this required tax payment.

When a situation arose that demanded the sacrifice of the sect leader, he would deliberately not pay his taxes, letting the imperial court arrest him. The imperial court didn’t know he was a diabolic creed leader and dealt with him as they would an ordinary Fusion cultivator evading taxes.

Generally, such offenses resulted in several decades of imprisonment. Once those decades passed and he was released, he would resume his position as creed leader, and the higher-ups would drop the matter of sacrifice.

“If only I could join the Heavenly Court Creed.” The Heavenly Court Creed can’t be more dangerous than this damned place.

He fished out a command token. This was the Radiant Sun Creed Token. Similar in principle to the Nine-Netherworlds Token, it was capable of long-distance communication.

During the last meeting with the Heavenly Court Creed, he had given one token each to their members.

“This one should belong to Holy Son Long Jingzhou.”

Chapter 690: Young Creed Leader Lu Seemed to Have Said That Creed Leader Yun and Yun Zhi Fought to a Draw

In a pitch-black room at the Nine-Netherworlds Creed headquarters, four pairs of eyes gleamed like wolves.

Since Creed Leader Qin’s time, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had advocated for simplicity in all things. As Fusion experts, the presence or absence of light made no difference to them; there was no need to light lamps.

This was an internal meeting between the higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, presided over by Mu Baiyi, with the three vice creed leaders in attendance. The primary purpose was to summarize the creed’s gains for the quarter.

Shi Huagu held the quarterly report for the barbeque business. As a veteran great devil, he could barely contain the joy in his eyes upon seeing the quarter’s earnings.

“The report has already been distributed to everyone. I believe everyone has reviewed them prior to the meeting.

“The barbeque business’s profitability is positive. Especially after our creed’s collaboration with Fellow Daoist Tao Yaoye of the Dao-Seeking Sect, where we inserted advertisements before the opening of her ‘Dreamlike Bubble Mirage,’ the barbeque business’s reputation has increased drastically. It can be said that even if someone hasn’t eaten our barbeque skewers yet, they’ve certainly heard of us.”

Tao Yaoye was only at the Nascent Soul Stage. By convention, she wasn’t qualified for Shi Huagu to address her as a “fellow Daoist.” However, Shi Huagu didn’t care about such rules and formalities. Anyone who could help him make money was a “fellow Daoist” to him.

With the rise of the barbeque restaurant, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s previous ventures—such as the zoo, funeral services, smuggling, and tomb raiding—were gradually being scaled back. These industries were under Vice Creed Leader Xiang’s purview. Among them, the smuggling and tomb raiding operations provided a steady annual output of “talent” to Great Xia’s prisons.

Of course, they were merely being scaled back, not shut down entirely.

Mu Baiyi was well aware that for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s finances to develop healthily, relying on the barbeque business as their sole pillar was insufficient. They needed multiple pillars to walk steadily.

Rumors circulated privately that Shi Huagu would soon replace Vice Creed Leader Xiang as the new Executive Vice Creed Leader. Whether this was hearsay or insider information remained unknown.

Vice Creed Leader Xiang’s greatest regret now was not being the first to make contact with the Heavenly Court Creed back then, allowing Shi Huagu to seize the initiative. The barbeque business’s profits made everyone drool with envy. Shi Huagu guarded it like a precious treasure, allowing no one else to interfere.

He wasn’t joking. This was his lifeline money. He would fight anyone who tried to touch it.

“Since the income is so substantial, I wonder when the funds for constructing Fengdu Ghost City will be approved?” Vice Creed Leader Shi asked Mu Baiyi directly. He was the vice creed leader specifically in charge of Fengdu Ghost City’s construction.

Mu Baiyi coughed twice. “While constructing Fengdu Ghost City is undoubtedly important, our creed is currently in a period of rapid development. Vice Creed Leader Shi, please prioritize the bigger picture and temporarily set the Fengdu Ghost City project aside.”

Fengdu Ghost City’s construction was temporarily on hold until they secretly paid off their debts.

Seeing that Mu Baiyi’s tone brooked no objection, Vice Creed Leader Shi did not raise the issue again.

Mu Baiyi asked Shi Huagu, who sat opposite him. “Vice Creed Leader Shi, I notice our barbeque business pays rather high taxes. Is there any way to reduce the taxes?”

Hearing this question, Shi Huagu’s face was plagued with frustration. “I’m finding a way. However, we’re considered to be in the food manufacturing industry. The imperial court doesn’t have any significant tax relief policies in this area.”

“Is that so...” Mu Baiyi was slightly regretful. Then, he produced another report. “This is a report from the Chunjiang Branch Leader. It just reached me before the meeting. Everyone, take a look.”

The three vice creed leaders read the contents of the report. Their hearts trembled, and even their voices quivered.

“This...this...the Heavenly Court Creed Leader is an immortal?!”

The report was written by the female ghost Little Cui. It detailed the battle between the two supreme lords in Chunjiang City, how Creed Leader Yun demonstrated her mighty prowess to capture both supreme lords alive, and how the barbeque shop acted courageously for justice by killing the Dark Night Pavilion assassins, earning a commendation banner from the authorities.

When Mu Baiyi first learned of this intelligence, his reaction hadn’t been much better than the three vice creed leaders’. He never imagined that the Creed Leader Yun they had met at the barbeque shop’s headquarters was a legendary ancient immortal. It was just that they didn’t know her title.

Shi Huagu’s brows were tightly furrowed as he recalled something Young Creed Leader Lu had mentioned. “No, there is another piece of intelligence hidden within this report.”

“What is it?” Vice Creed Leader Xiang hadn’t spotted anything amiss.

“When I first met Young Creed Leader Lu, he told me that their creed leader once fought Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect...” Shi Huagu paused, as if uttering these words might attract a calamity, but he continued, “...and the result was a draw.”

“What? How is that possible?!”

“Old Shi, are you saying the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Yun Zhi is also an immortal?”

Mu Baiyi rapped the table loudly with two fingers. “Quiet. Everyone, quiet. You are all Fusion cultivators. Have you forgotten the most fundamental notion of cultivators? When a fact occurs, we ought to accept it, not question it!

“Don’t forget, the Heavenly Court Creed has never deceived us. If Young Creed Leader Yu said it is so, then it is so! This is intelligence worth more than thousands of gold. Who else in the world knows that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Yun Zhi is this powerful?

“We’re the only ones.

“I believe this was intelligence the Heavenly Court Creed offered us as a goodwill gesture. Unfortunately, our vision was too limited to recognize their intent before today!”

The three vice creed leaders hung their heads in shame.

Mu Baiyi’s expression was grave, his expression brooding. “If the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Yun Zhi is an immortal, the imperial court’s strength is even more terrifying than we had imagined. The Dao-Seeking Sect has an immortal, yet they show no intention of vying for power with the imperial court. This suggests that the imperial court may also have an immortal!”

The three vice creed leaders fell silent. If that were the case, even if their Fengdu Ghost City’s construction was completed, they would not be a match for the righteous path.

Mu Baiyi was the calmest. “The situation isn’t that dire. The righteous path has two immortals, and the Heavenly Court Creed also has two—Dou Heavenly Sovereign and Creed Leader Yun. They are evenly matched.

“We can get closer to the Heavenly Court Creed by presenting gifts to Young Creed Leader Lu. As Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s disciple, he will surely oversee the Heavenly Court’s affairs in the future. Now is the perfect time to invest!”

~~~

“You’re saying that people from the Radiant Sun Creed are looking for you?” Lu Yang looked at the Radiant Sun Token in Meng Jingzhou’s hand with slight bafflement.

The Radiant Sun Token reflected a message from Creed Leader Chi to Meng Jingzhou:

Holy Son Long, our creed has gleaned some insights regarding cultivation methods to enhance the absorption of the sun’s power. Would you be interested? Please come to Poyang City in Yu Province for a discussion.

“Are they planning to share cultivation secret manuals with you?” Lu Yang was even more befuddled after reading the message. Isn’t this overture to express goodwill too obvious?

“Could they have heard about the Chunjiang City incident and want to curry favor with me?”

Lu Yang mulled over it and found it plausible. As for why they contacted Meng Jingzhou after a delay of over half a month, the Radiant Sun Creed probably thought that a longer interval might make it seem like they weren’t approaching Meng Jingzhou because they feared Creed Leader Yun.

Before Lu Yang could speak, he felt movement from the Nine-Netherworlds Token in his robe. He pulled it out for a look.

“What is it?” Meng Jingzhou craned his neck to see.

Lu Yang openly showed the Nine-Netherworlds Token. “The Nine-Netherworlds Creed is looking for me.”

“...What should we do? Split up or gather both creeds together?”

Lu Yang rubbed his chin. “Don’t be in a rush to reply. Let’s go get some intelligence from Senior Brother Dai first.”

With Li Haoran around, they knew a lot about the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, but their knowledge of the Radiant Sun Creed was limited.

~~~

In the Great Mission Hall, Dai Bufan looked the two up and down with a peculiar expression.

“You’re saying the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed are each trying to bribe you in private?”

Chapter 691: Accepting Bribes

It was Dai Bufan’s first time hearing about a diabolic creed voluntarily offering benefits. Do the diabolic creeds treat you two as their protective umbrellas or something? How come I fight diabolic creeds every day but never see them begging for mercy or trying to bribe me?

“That can’t be called a bribe. It’s just that they insist on giving it to us, and we’re too thin-skinned to refuse,” Meng Jingzhou corrected. “Moreover, the crime of bribery applies to imperial court officials. Old Lu and I are legitimate civilians.”

Lu Yang concurred. “We are enduring humiliation as part of our mission to infiltrate the enemy and are forced to accept the gifts.”

Dai Bufan gave up. “Fine, fine. Here is all the intelligence on the Radiant Sun Creed. You two study it.” He shoved a large stack of documents to the two, telling them to read them here and return them when finished.

I’ll just treat it as grooming the future hall leader and vice hall leader in advance.

He still had a pile of matters to attend to himself. In a few months, it would be the Dao-Seeking Sect’s new recruitment cycle. Due to the lack of preparation last time, it resulted in recruiting good juniors like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou who kept him on edge daily, while promising seedlings like Bai Ming and Lan Ting were recruited early by other sects.

This time, Dai Bufan was determined to identify a few candidates with excellent character, temperament, and talent in advance. His current task was to find these individuals from the vast sea of intelligence.

~~~

Much information about the Radiant Sun Creed couldn’t be concealed—for example, periodically sending a couple of Fusion cultivators to die on the sun, their desire for everyone to worship the sun, their treatment of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace as a hypothetical enemy, and so on.

The Radiant Sun was founded sixty thousand years ago and had been researching the sun all these years. One could imagine the profound depth of their research into cultivation techniques based on solar power.

However, no matter how profound, it definitely couldn’t compare to what Lu Yang knew. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s study, which they had recently acquired, clearly contained the Nine-Layer Immortal’s understanding of the power of lunar yin and solar yang. Regardless of how powerful the Radiant Sun Creed was, could they possibly surpass the Nine-Layers Immortal, who possessed the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit?

After studying for three full days, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou finally grasped all the intelligence on the Radiant Sun Creed.

“Finished reading?” Dai Bufan raised an eyebrow. With a thought, the Radiant Sun Creed files automatically returned to their original positions.

“More or less.”

“How many elders do you need to accompany you?” Dai Bufan certainly wouldn’t let two Nascent Soul cultivators meet a diabolic creed leader alone; it was too dangerous.

“Four elders.”

“Alright, wait here, I’ll help you contact them.” Dai Bufan stood up and left the Great Mission Hall to visit the various mountain peaks and request the elders’ assistance.

~~~

Upon hearing there was another opportunity to serve as heavenly king protectors, the elders’ enthusiasm was overwhelming to the point a fight nearly broke out. Fortunately, under Dai Bufan’s persuasion, they agreed to settle it by drawing lots.

In the end, Grandpa Ba, Third Elder, Fourth Elder, and Seventh Elder were selected to accompany Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

~~~

Meanwhile, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou took out their respective tokens to notify the two creed leaders and promptly selected a restaurant for the meeting scheduled two days later.

Regarding meeting gifts, the Heavenly Court Creed held the initiative.

The two creed leaders quickly responded, assuring they would attend.

~~~

Two days later, they had the entire restaurant reserved, and the three creeds gathered once more.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou sat in the main central seats, with four heavenly king protectors standing behind them like iron towers. The heavenly king protectors’ tiger-like eyes were wide and round, naturally imposing and exuding a subtle pressure.

Neither Mu Baiyi nor Creed Leader Chi had expected to see one another here, leading to a moment of awkwardness.

Creed Leader Chi also hadn’t anticipated that Young Creed Leader Lu would be present. Didn’t they say Young Creed Leader Lu and Holy Son Long have friction between them? Why is Young Creed Leader Lu tagging along when I’m trying to give gifts specifically to Holy Son Long? Could some unknown change have occurred during this time?

“It has been many days since we last met. Both of you remain as impressive as ever, hahahaha.” Creed Leader Chi cupped his hands and greeted them as peers, breaking the awkwardness first.

Behind Creed Leader Chi stood two young delicate-looking female attendants, their skin so tender that one could almost pinch water from it.

Creed Leader Chi gave a signal with his eyes. The two young female attendants obediently walked over to Meng Jingzhou’s side and were completely docile, causing Meng Jingzhou’s eyelid to twitch.

“Creed Leader Chi, what is the meaning of this?”

“A small token of goodwill. Since we both cultivate pure-yang-type cultivation techniques, we ought to vent the fire periodically. Consider these two lasses a meeting gift. Please accept them, Holy Son Long.” Creed Leader Chi felt that offering just cultivating techniques might not be enough to move Holy Son Long, so he decided to increase the stakes.

Meng Jingzhou naturally wouldn’t accept them and feigned anger. “Are you using this as a pretext to plant two spies by my side?!”

Creed Leader Chi hurriedly replied, “Please quell your anger, Holy Son Long. I absolutely have no such intention.”

No matter how Creed Leader Chi tried to persuade him, Meng Jingzhou remained vigilant and refused to accept the two female attendants.

Seeing Holy Son Long’s firm stance, Creed Leader Chi had no choice but to relent and recall the two female attendants.

Meng Jingzhou narrowed his eyes. “Creed Leader Chi, do you really have a method to enhance the absorption of the sun’s power?”

Creed Leader Chi hadn’t expected his previous action to create a rift with Holy Son Long, which went against his original intention.

Lu Yang laughed heartily and patted Meng Jingzhou’s shoulder. “You’re overthinking it. How would Creed Leader Chi dare to scheme against us? That can’t be.”

Seeing Lu Yang smoothing things over for him, Creed Leader Chi looked at him with a hint of gratitude, then took out a wooden box with seals on its surface. He opened the seals. Inside the wooden box were several books—the cultivation techniques for utilizing solar power.

Fourth Elder stepped forward and browsed the cultivation manuals before respectfully turning to Meng Jingzhou. “Holy Son, these are indeed cultivation techniques for utilizing solar power. They can be used for reference.”

Meng Jingzhou casually replied, “Mmm, then accept them,” and waved his hand impatiently.

Creed Leader Chi hadn’t prepared a gift for Lu Yang and could only hastily take out precious natural treasures from his storage ring at the last minute. “Please kindly accept this, Young Creed Leader Lu.”

Lu Yang swept a glance over them. Recognizing their origin, he smiled. “Hundred Herb Pill, True Dragon Molted Exuvia, Ginseng King Beard... Creed Leader Chi, you’ve put thought into this. I won’t stand on ceremony then.”

Seventh Elder stepped forward from the side and accepted these treasures on Lu Yang’s behalf.

Seeing the effort Creed Leader Chi was putting in, Mu Baiyi knew that if his offerings were inferior, it would easily leave a bad impression on the Heavenly Court Creed. I’m afraid this is the reason the Heavenly Court Creed gathered both creeds together.

With his heart aching, Mu Baiyi retrieved his treasured items from his storage ring and presented them to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, who accepted them all.

After the two creed leaders had handed over their gifts, they suddenly spoke simultaneously. “I have a matter I’d like to consult.”

The two glared at each other.

Lu Yang chuckled and raised his hand, gesturing for them not to be anxious. “There’s still plenty of time. One at a time.

“How about this? Since Creed Leader Chi spoke first last time, let Creed Leader Mu speak first this time. What do you both think?”

Creed Leader Chi had no choice but to agree.

Mu Baiyi asked, “Our barbeque business is booming, raking in mountains of gold daily. It’s just that the imperial court’s taxes are too high. I wonder if you have any solutions, Young Creed Leader Lu?” He first pulled Lu Yang into the same camp.

The four heavenly king protectors frowned inwardly. This is an unexpected question. How should we respond?

Lu Yang smiled but did not answer. Instead, he turned to Creed Leader Chi. “And you?”

“It’s like this, Young Creed Leader Lu. As you know, our Radiant Sun Creed has been researching solar power all this time to make the world worship the sun. Recently, our multiple attempts to land on the sun have failed. I wonder if you have any solutions, Young Creed Leader Lu?” Creed Leader Chi was anxious. If the sun-landing attempts fail again, I’ll have to evade taxes and get locked up in prison for decades to seek refuge.

The four heavenly king protectors frowned inwardly again. What solutions can there be? The sun is the embodiment of extreme yang; whoever touches it dies. Does the Radiant Sun Creed want Yun Zhi to intervene?

Hearing this, Lu Yang interlaced his fingers and placed them on his chest as he leaned back slightly against the chair.

“The problems faced by both your creeds can actually be solved with a single method.

“Creed Leader Chi, have you heard of solar energy?”

Chapter 692: Solar Energy

“Solar...energy?” Creed Leader Chi was stunned. As the creed leader of the Radiant Sun Creed, he was well-versed in all matters related to the sun. But what exactly is this “solar energy” Young Creed Leader Lu mentioned?

“Interpreted literally, it seems to refer to the sun’s energy?” Creed Leader Chi probed.

“In a superficial sense, yes, that’s the idea.” Lu Yang suddenly brought up another matter. “You mentioned earlier that the sun-landing plan has failed repeatedly. I assume that this is a plan initiated only in recent years and that you were researching the sun’s power from a distance before that.

“In that case, why are you now attempting to land on the sun to study it?”

Creed Leader Chi sighed. “Young Creed Leader Lu, you may not be aware, but our research into the sun’s power has hit a bottleneck. The radical faction proposed landing on the sun to study it up close. However, how is the sun easy to approach? Several Fusion cultivators have already been burned alive by the sun.”

Lu Yang reclined lazily against the chair as he picked at non-existent dirt under his fingernails. “Your esteemed creed has quite the courage to dare to land on the sun. Do you know that the stars that fill the sky were originally phantom images? And that over a hundred years ago, a being of supreme power employed a world-shocking method to fill the positions of those stellar illusions?”

How could Creed Leader Chi not know? The previous creed leader was sacrificed to heaven precisely because of this event.

Lu Yang continued, “That supremely powerful being is someone even our Heavenly Court Creed finds troublesome to deal with. Yet your Radiant Sun Creed actually dares to ascend to the heavens and investigate the sun? Aren’t you afraid of violating that individual’s taboos and having your creed wiped out in one fell swoop?”

Creed Leader Chi was drenched in cold sweat after hearing this. If even the Heavenly Court Creed finds this entity troublesome, it means that supremely powerful being is an immortal.

The Radiant Sun Creed landing on the sun is equivalent to causing trouble right under an immortal’s nose. Perhaps a single careless action could offend the immortal and bring a catastrophic calamity upon the creed.

I had opposed the sun-landing plan from the start, but the higher-ups were dead set on throwing away their lives. Great, we can now wait for the immortal to annihilate our whole creed.

“What is your opinion then, Young Creed Leader Lu?”

“The Radiant Sun Creed’s goal is to spread faith, not land on the sun, right?”

“That’s right.”

“Creed Leader Chi, you should know that solar power encompasses both light and heat. Light provides illumination, and heat provides warmth.”

Creed Leader Chi nodded. This was written in The True Treatise on the Sun’s Power, something every member of the Radiant Sun Creed knew; it was a mandatory topic in the end-of-year examinations. The True Treatise on the Sun’s Power was an internal book of the Radiant Sun Creed which all members possessed.

Lu Yang took out a magnifying glass. “This is the cheapest magnifying glass. Just put it under the sun, and the solar power will concentrate at a single point. At a low intensity, it can burn ants to death, and at a high intensity, it can start a blaze. This is a basic demonstration of solar energy.”

Creed Leader Chi continued nodding. Lu Yang was explaining fundamental knowledge, and the magnifying glass was his invention, so he was extremely familiar with it.

“Since the sun possesses energy, why not utilize it?” Lu Yang asked.

Creed Leader Chi replied, “We’re already utilizing it. We research solar power cultivation techniques and methods to enhance the absorption of the sun’s power.”

Lu Yang shook his head. “Not that kind of utilization. Why would cultivators practice the cultivation techniques you write? Is it just because they are solar power cultivation techniques?

“Lunar Yin, Solar Yang, Three Talents, Four Divisions, Five Elements—the variety of cultivation techniques is as numerous as ox hair. Is it necessary for cultivators to choose yours?

“If cultivators don’t choose your cultivation techniques, your faith in the sun won’t be propagated and can’t earn the world’s recognition.”

Creed Leader Chi reflected on the Radiant Sun Creed’s action over the past sixty thousand years. It’s indeed the case. Many cultivation techniques in the world focus on spirit energy as the core. We have painstakingly researched solar power cultivation techniques, yet hardly anybody pays them attention. Spreading our faith is a challenge.

“Please enlighten me, Young Creed Leader Lu.”

“I’ve already mentioned the method, that is, to utilize solar energy—not by writing solar power cultivation techniques but by bringing solar energy into ordinary households. For example, we could store solar energy and use it for illumination.”

“Allowing ordinary civilians to use solar energy? How is that possible?” Creed Leader Chi exclaimed, having never considered this matter.

Lu Yang chuckled nonchalantly. “Why is that impossible? Tao Yaoye of the Dao-Seeking Sect developed ‘Dreamlike Bubble Mirage,’ which even ordinary civilians can afford. Can’t you use arrays to accumulate solar energy and release it at night?

“As for the propagation power of the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage, you are in the best position to speak about it, Creed Leader Mu.”

Mu Baiyi nodded. The wider the dissemination of the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage, the more our barbeque shop’s fame grew, and the more prosperous our business became—an effect directly reflected in our profits.

“If a single disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect could develop such a thing, why can’t the Radiant Sun Creed? If this research succeeds, candles can be replaced. If every household possesses your Radiant Sun Creed’s invention, why worry about being unable to proselytize?”

Lu Yang gazed meaningfully at the Creed Leader Chi. “If you wish to make the world believe in the sun, you must first let the world benefit from it. Creed Leader Chi, you should understand this principle.”

Creed Leader Chi suddenly felt like he had seen the light. As expected of an ancient major faction, their level of understanding is a tier above mine.

Lu Yang added, “Of course, using solar energy for lightning isn’t something achieved overnight. How to collect and store solar energy, how to release it, how to simplify the structure, how to reduce costs, and so on—these are all issues that require in-depth research. Your esteemed creed can work on it step by step.

“Furthermore, this is just a random example I gave. Solar energy can do much more. You can research it slowly after returning, Creed Leader Chi.”

Research was Creed Leader Chi’s forte. It was precisely his invention of the telescope that elevated him to a higher-up of the Radiant Sun Creed. Besides, this plan is far more reliable than the sun-landing plan and will definitely gain the approval of the higher-ups. If we achieve results in this research, wealth and fame will flow in ceaselessly.

This is a once-in-a-millennium opportunity for the Radiant Sun Creed to develop!

I must lead the research myself and keep the results in my hands. That way, the higher-ups won’t dare to sacrifice me to heaven at the first sign of difficulty.

This is an amazing idea that kills multiple birds with one stone!

Creed Leader Chi’s excitement was beyond words.

Is this the wisdom of an ancient major faction’s successor? In just a few sentences, he not only solved the Radiant Sun Creed’s problem but also my own predicament!

If even the successor is like this, how terrifying must the legendary Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s wisdom be?!

Lu Yang cast his gaze at Mu Baiyi and remained silent, imparting a subtle sense of pressure.

After a long while, Lu Yang spoke. “As for the matter of the barbeque business’s taxes, you may want to consider collaborating with the Radiant Sun Creed, Creed Leader Mu.”

“Collaborate?” Mu Baiyi was astonished. Setting aside the fact that our two creeds represent yin and yang respectively and are inherently incompatible in nature, even if we are compatible, where would this collaboration begin?

Noticing Mu Baiyi’s expression, Lu Yang knew the other party hadn’t understood him. “Creed Leader Lu, your understanding of Great Xia’s policies is not as deep as an ancient like me. Do you know that Great Xia implements preferential tax policies for research-oriented industries and that there are substantial tax reductions and even tax exemption policies for the development of new technologies? The same applies to using energy sources other than spirit energy.”

Lu Yang stared at Mu Baiyi as if he were an idiot. And you call yourself a creed leader? You know less than I do.

Chapter 693: Joint Venture of Three Creeds

Mu Baiyi didn’t mind Lu Yang’s gaze, nor did he dare to.

The three questions Lu Yang posed dispelled the murky darkness before him, allowing him to see the light.

“Young Creed Leader Lu, you mean our Nine-Netherworlds Creed can collaborate with the Radiant Sun Creed in operating the barbeque shop?”

“Not a barbeque shop, but a solar technology development merchant guild, with barbeque being one of its enterprises,” Lu Yang corrected.

If it remains just a barbeque business, what tax policies would apply? Only by changing the nature of the establishment can they enjoy preferential tax policies.

To avoid following his shifu’s footsteps in entering prison, Lu Yang had painstakingly studied laws and policies. Only he knew how much effort he had expended.

“Yes yes yes, the Solar Energy Technology Development Merchant Guild.” Mu Baiyi nodded repeatedly. Young Creed Leader Lu’s mind is truly sharp.

Isn’t this precisely the “internal alliance with the Radiant Sun Creed and the Heartless Creed” mentioned in his plot to strive for supremacy?

Young Creed Leader Lu had probably foreseen today’s situation long ago.

What terrifying ingenuity and acumen!

If I had even a fraction of Young Creed Leader Lu’s intellect, why would I have needed to impersonate a follower to take out loans?

I could have built several Fengdu Ghost Cities! Never mind being the creed leader, even the followers would have to worship me as the creed founder!

Great Xia had always encouraged innovation and creation. Both Lu Yang’s flying carriage and Tao Yaoye’s Dreamlike Bubble Mirage had enjoyed preferential tax policies.

Moreover, since spirit energy was essentially considered a strategic resource, Great Xia encouraged the use of energy resources other than spirit energy, hence implementing the series of tax policies as mentioned by Lu Yang earlier.

In Lu Yang’s view, the cultivation world need not follow the step-by-step process of the world in his previous life to undergo an industrial revolution—steam first, then electricity. They could leapfrog to using clean solar energy directly.

This was something he had thought of while reviewing the Radiant Sun Creed’s materials. He just hadn’t figured out how to guide them to this step when the opportunity came knocking on his door.

“By jointly establishing a merchant guild to develop new solar technologies, Great Xia will vigorously support it. With such support, the barbeque shop’s taxes won’t be a problem at all.

“In addition, maintaining true fire for barbecuing requires spirit energy to be continuously channeled into the true fire. If the Radiant Sun Creed’s research yield results, solar energy could be used to sustain the true fire. In that case, the imperial court won’t only reduce taxes—they might even provide subsidies.”

The future Lu Yang painted made Mu Baiyi’s eyes sparkle. Getting to know the Heavenly Court Creed is the most correct decision I’ve ever made in my life.

Seeing Creed Leader Chi lost in thought with his head lowered, Lu Yang smiled and said, “Creed Leader Chi, I know what you’re thinking. You’re simply wondering whether your Radiant Sun Creed can research solar energy by yourselves without the need to collaborate with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, right?”

“No, no, it’s nothing like that.” Creed Leader Chi flatly denied it, though that was exactly what he was thinking.

“It’s fine. People naturally seek profit. It’s understandable. However, Creed Leader Chi, please think carefully. Establishing the Solar Energy Technology Development Merchant Guild first requires a clean identity. Registering a merchant guild of such a large scale has strict requirements regarding the registration fee and the registrant’s identity. At the very least, a Fusion cultivator is needed.

“If I’m not mistaken, among the Fusion cultivators in your esteemed creed, only you, Creed Leader Chi, aren’t wanted by the authorities, correct? Are you planning to register the merchant guild with your identity as a great inventor, and then have your seven convictions for tax evasion get the merchant guild flagged as a prime target for inspection?”

Creed Leader Chi broke out in a cold sweat. He hadn’t expected the other party to have investigated his identity so thoroughly.

In truth, he had always used two identities. One was the inventor of the telescope, Chi Guantian—his public identity, while the other was the creed leader of the Radiant Sun Creed—his hidden identity.

The purpose was to let other members of other diabolic creeds recognize him and secretly report him.

He never anticipated the other party to see through his disguise.

Lu Yang didn’t possess the ability to see through Creed Leader Chi’s disguise; it was Yun Zhi who had seen through it. After their last meeting, Yun Zhi had recognized Creed Leader Chi’s real identity.

“On the other hand, the Nine-Netherworld Creed’s Shi Huagu, the big boss of the barbeque business, has received multiple commendations from the imperial court and earned their complete trust. Having him show himself to establish the guild will surely save a lot of trouble.”

Meng Jingzhou slammed the table and shouted. “Our creed holds sixty percent of the barbeque business’s profits! Creed Leader Chi, are you saying that you’re unwilling to let our creed participate in the affairs of the merchant guild?”

Although Meng Jingzhou was only at the Nascent Soul Stage, his words carried the threat of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in Creed Leader Chi’s ears.

Only then did Creed Leader Chi remember that while the barbeque business was the Nine-Netherworld Creed’s enterprise on the surface, the Heavenly Court Creed was actually the majority shareholder!

This merchant guild isn’t a joint venture between two creeds, but three!

What was I thinking just now? Going solo and blocking the Heavenly Court Creed’s revenue stream? Was I tired of living?

Isn’t this the perfect opportunity to latch onto the Heavenly Court Creed’s thigh?!

Creed Leader Chi smiled obsequiously. “Young Creed Leader Lu, Holy Son Long, you jest. Dou Heavenly Sovereign above, Chi really has no intention of going solo.”

“Is that so? Good then.” Lu Yang smiled, as if it had all been a joke, and patted Meng Jingzhou’s back. “Old Long, calm down. See, Creed Leader Chi doesn’t have that intention.”

“That’s more like it.” Meng Jingzhou snorted coldly, unwilling to say more to these people.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stood up and raised their teacups. Seeing this, the two creed leaders quickly rose and followed suit.

“Then let us toast to the enduring friendship of our three creeds. To my shifu.”

“To Dou Heavenly Sovereign.”

“To Dou Heavenly Sovereign.”

“To Dou Heavenly Sovereign.”

The four downed their drinks, showing the utmost respect to Dou Heavenly Sovereign.

In the mental space, Dou Heavenly Sovereign was very satisfied with the four’s attitude toward her.

“Do the two of you have any other matters?” Lu Yang stretched lazily.

“No more, no more. Thank you for your advice, Young Creed Leader Lu.”

“Chi is dull-witted. Please continue enlightening me in the future, Young Creed Leader Lu.”

Through Lu Yang’s combination of benefits and warnings, the two creed leaders held genuine respect for this young creed leader from the bottom of their hearts. They believed him to be someone to be befriended and never made an enemy.

After the Heavenly Court Creed bid goodbye, the young creed leader and the holy son departed with the four heavenly king protectors.

With their profound cultivations, the two creed leaders had sharper hearing than ordinary Fusion cultivators. Even from a distance, they could vaguely hear the conversation between Young Creed Leader Lu and Holy Son Long.

“Why did you tell them that? Let them solve their own problems. Even if you help them, what can they possibly help us with? Are we short of this bit of money? Or can they assist when we battle with the Four Ancient Immortals in the future?”

“In any case, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed had a good relationship with us before, and there are sun deities in the Heavenly Court. There’s more or less some connection and affinity between us. Seeing how miserable they’re doing, we should help if we can.”

“You make it sound like we’re begging to join the guild. Who cares about that? Isn’t it just so we have a reason to keep guiding them in the appropriate direction after researching solar energy to replace candles? Without us, would the Radiant Sun Creed know what to do next? They don’t appreciate goodwill!”

“Alright, Old Long. Everyone has their struggles. There’s no need to let them know our considerations.”

Finally, the conversation faded into the wind, no longer audible.

After hearing their conversation, the two creed leaders were overwhelmed with shame. If not for the Heavenly Court Creed cherishing past ties, we wouldn’t even have the chance to latch onto their thigh.

Chapter 694: Dai Bufan: I Have A Mission for You Two

“This thing about using solar energy for light and heat sounds familiar. I’ve done something similar before,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented cheerfully on the way back as she stretched lazily.

She had been cultivating by sleeping on her bed, recovering her strength. Now that she was awake, it indicated that her cultivation progress had temporarily paused.

“Immortal Fairy, you’ve worked hard sleeping. Did you also use solar energy in ancient times?”

“I haven’t heard of ‘solar energy,’ but the usage should be roughly the same.”

“How did you use it?”

“There was a period when I enjoyed reading. I’d read during the day and continue at night. Although my vision was excellent, and I could see clearly even in places without light, it lacked the right atmosphere.

“Hence, I invited a jinwu crow. During the day, I let it rest and conserve its energy without shining, and at night, I had it illuminate for me. Let me tell you, it was as bright as daytime.

“Sometimes, when the fire wasn’t strong enough while cooking, I’d invite a jinwu to help blow on the fire and heat things up. Of course, I wouldn’t let it help for free; I always invited it to stay for a meal.”

“...I think the way we use solar energy for light and heat isn’t the same thing,” Lu Yang remarked.

“Is that so? This immortal thinks they’re quite similar though. Look, didn’t I first store the solar power?”

“Yes.”

“And isn’t the solar power released after storing it?”

“Yes.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clapped her hands. “There you have it. Exactly the same.”

Lu Yang patiently tried to distinguish the two for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “The solar energy I’m talking about can not only be used for light and heat but also to heat water, replace horses, and make carts move.”

“This immortal’s solar power can do that too! I can make the jinwu crow boil water or pull me around to fly everywhere and such.”

Lu Yang, “...”

After hoodwinking the two creed leaders as planned, the Heavenly Court Creed members made their way back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Lu Yang was striving to explain to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that solar energy wasn’t what she thought it was.

Meanwhile, Meng Jingzhou was studying the cultivation techniques offered by the Radiant Sun Creed, learning how to maximize the absorption of solar power.

In the cultivation manual, a completely naked man faced the sun with arms spread wide, allowing sunlight to touch every inch of his skin. The illustrations were vivid, lifelike, and easy to understand.

In the margins of the page, the Radiant Sun Creed had added notes emphasizing the necessity of stripping completely and not leaving a single piece of cloth, especially in the crotch area, stating that there was no concept of shame in matters of cultivation.

The reasoning given was quite thorough: If other parts are cultivated, why does the crotch area not need cultivation?

In addition, various sunbathing postures were listed.

The Radiant Sun Creed was considerate; apart from the male version, there was also a female version.

Meng Jingzhou stared at the two books in his hands and fell silent.

The cover of the second book featured a completely naked woman in a seductive pose, seemingly excited from sunbathing. He contemplated whether he should open it.

No wonder nobody studies your creed’s cultivation techniques. Are these even proper cultivation techniques?

The four heavenly king protectors dropped Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou at the sect entrance and returned to their respective mountain peaks.

“Do you feel like there are fewer people in our sect?” Lu Yang remarked. On the way back, he noticed fewer disciples than usual.

“Now that you mention it, it’s indeed so.”

The two went to the Great Mission Hall to report the details of their operation to Dai Bufan.

“Senior Brother Dai, that’s the overall situation of our meeting with the two creeds... Senior Brother Dai?”

After Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou finished their report, they realized Dai Bufan seemed distracted, as if his mind was elsewhere.

Dai Bufan snapped out of it as if jerking out of a reverie. “Ah, right. You did well. The bribes from the two creeds were obtained through your deception skills. No need to hand them over to the sect.”

Then, Dai Bufan looked at the two with a conflicted expression, as if a battle was raging inside him. Hesitant and decisive, he finally gritted his teeth and made a significant decision. “You came at the right time. I happen to have a mission here that needs you.”

“Mission?”

Dai Bufan pushed a small booklet toward them. It contained information on several mortals, all of whom were quite young.

“These people are...”

“These people are potential candidates for the sect’s upcoming recruitment. The plan is to observe their character beforehand—whether they can cultivate and whether they meet our sect’s standards. If they fulfill the criteria, we’ll invite them to take the entrance examinations here on the second day of the second month next year.”

Aside from disciples at critical cultivation junctures, on other missions, staying behind to maintain sect operations, or at the Void Refinement Stage, most Dao-Seeking Sect disciples had been sent out by Dai Bufan to observe the candidates’ characters.

Observing one’s character wasn’t something that yielded results in a day or two. The shortest would take a month, and the longest could take up to a year. Therefore, those dispatched might not have time to execute a second observation mission.

They were truly short-handed, forcing Dai Bufan to assign Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to observe the candidates as well.

And this was precisely what he had been conflicted about.

If he weren’t occupied, he would rather go on the mission himself than send Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Who knows what kind of trouble they might stir up?

“So that’s how it is.” Lu Yang revealed a confident smile and thumped his chest in assurance. “Don’t worry, Senior Brother Dai. Don’t you know us already? We’ll definitely complete the mission!”

Dai Bufan sighed. As usual, he reminded them before their departure, “If you discover someone not on the list who also meets our sect’s recruitment criteria, you can recommend them to me as well.”

“No problem.”

“By the way, do you know our sect’s requirements for one’s character?” Dai Bufan was still not very reassured.

“Be honest and do one’s part.”

“Cultivate steadily and diligently.”

Dai Bufan nodded, feeling slightly relieved. “Good that you know. Off you go.”

~~~

In the carriage, the two flipped through the information in the booklet. There were three mortals in total, all around fifteen years old.

“Let’s go to Jiulong City[1] in You Province first. It’s the closest to us.” Meng Jingzhou pointed to the mortal on the first page.

The mortal on the first page was a young man named Xie An. A senior male had discovered him during a mission in Jiulong City.

It had been a mission to eliminate a red-robed malevolent ghost that had committed numerous atrocities. After a thorough search, that senior male disciple finally tracked down the malevolent ghost’s whereabouts. When the ghost realized it was no match for that senior male disciple and noticed his reluctance to use his full power in areas with many mortals, it deduced he cared for mortals. Hence, it threatened him with mortal lives to secure an escape route.

The person who was held hostage was Xie An.

At the critical moment, Xie An displayed remarkable composure, staying unflustered despite being threatened by the red-robed malevolent ghost. He even used words to provoke the ghost. Enraged, the ghost exposed an opening and was slain by the senior male disciple.

At that time, Xie An was still young and not yet of age to test his spirit root, so his bone foundation was unknown.

“It seems like this kid called Xie An is a suitable seed for cultivation,” Lu Yang said with a chuckle. Remaining calm in danger is something even many cultivators fail to do. Only with such a mental fortitude does one stand a chance of survival in the face of peril.

Old Meng and I possess precisely this kind of mental fortitude.

1. “Jiulong” translates literally to “nine dragons.” ☜

Chapter 695: Immortal Fairy, Can You Say It Earlier Next Time?

Jiulong City in You Province was a moderately developed city. The individual with the highest cultivation was the city lord, at the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage.

It was rumored that a secret domain was hidden outside the city, but no one had ever found it, and it gradually became a legend.

Additionally, there were three locally renowned major sects: the Primordial Ancient Sword Sect, the Daytime Ascension Sect, and the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace. Each of the three was presided over by a Nascent Soul old monster.

Cultivators like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, who were at the Double Infants Stage, could practically strut through Jiulong City without anyone stopping them. But they weren’t troublemakers. They were here on a mission and had to observe from the shadows to determine their target’s character.

“It should be in this direction.” Meng Jingzhou left the old horse at the stable and went with Lu Yang to find their target.

“The intelligence says Xie An has no parents and lives in a dilapidated temple outside the city.”

Following the instructions, they arrived at a rundown temple. The temple’s memorial archway was crumbling, its inscription illegible. It was unclear when the temple was built or why the monks had relocated.

The temple was small and drafty from all sides. The lotus platform was empty, devoid of even a Buddha statue. Dry grass spread before the lotus platform, with an extinguished fire pit in the middle.

Xie An was nowhere to be seen. Only an old beggar lay lazily on the ground, propping his head with one hand and picking lice off his body with the other.

“Should we show ourselves and ask where Xie An is?” The two communicated through auditory messages, not rashly revealing themselves to inquire with the old beggar.

If the old beggar knew Xie An, the latter would learn of their presence, which would be detrimental to their task of discreetly observing his character.

Lu Yang analyzed, “Let’s wait a bit longer. Look, the bedding is neatly folded; it certainly wasn’t the old beggar who did it, but likely Xie An. This means that even if Xie An has left, he hasn’t gone far.”

Sure enough, when evening fell, a grimy Xie An was supported by a young girl as he entered the temple.

The old beggar gloated. “What, you went to the Primordial Ancient Sword Sect? I told you they wouldn’t want you two.”

Xie An remained silent. The girl supporting him spoke up indignantly on his behalf. “They’re too much! They didn’t even test Xie-gege’s bone foundation and aptitude. They simply saw his ragged clothes and claimed he had no cultivation talent, then threw him out of the sect!”

The girl was dressed in tatters, as if she had just been dug out of a dirt pit. Lu Yang could tell that if she was cleaned and dressed up nicely, she would be a budding beauty.

The old beggar yawned. “Bone Foundation Stones are expensive and have limited uses. It would be strange if they were willing to test your spirit roots for free.”

Xie An frowned but said nothing.

“Alright, enough sulking. Look what I got today.” The old beggar produced three large white mantou steamed buns like a magician.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had been stationed here the whole day and saw that the old beggar hadn’t moved an inch.

“It’s mantou!” The little girl’s eyes shone.

The old man and the two youngsters ate the mantou by the fire, quiet and content.

Halfway through eating, Xie An suddenly said, “Qiao'er-meimei,[1] I’ll try the Daytime Ascension Sect tomorrow.” His gaze was resolute.

“Okay, I’ll go with Xie-gege tomorrow.”

The old beggar sneered, seemingly mocking Xie An’s futile efforts.

After eating the mantou, the old beggar excitedly pulled Xie An to the side and cleared the grass, revealing a weiqi board drawn with stones. The old beggar pulled out a handful of small black and white stones.

“Come come come, Xie boy. Play a couple of rounds with me.”

Xie An agreed. The old and young players battled on the board, while the girl named Qiao’er watched from the side.

All five games ended in a victory for Xie An, and the old beggar was filled with regret.

After the night passed, the old beggar was still asleep. Xie An took Qiao’er to the Daytime Ascension Sect, with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou following secretly.

At the entrance of the Daytime Ascension Sect, Xie An stated his purpose, hoping to have his bone foundation tested. However, the two outer sect disciples on duty scoffed at him.

“Get lost, get lost! Where did this little beggar come from? How could someone like you have a spirit root?”

“Even the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace, whose Nascent Soul old ancestor has disappeared, wouldn’t want you two.”

Once again, Xie An was pushed to the ground. He endured quietly, biting his lips until they bled.

I will repay today’s humiliation a hundredfold!

In the evening, Xie An was helped back by Qiao’er again. The old beggar still wore his gloating expression.

“I told you already, no place would want someone like you.”

It was the same routine—eating mantou and playing weiqi, with the old beggar losing continuously.

Just as he was about to lose the fifth game, the old beggar suddenly asked, “Xie boy, do you really wish to cultivate?”

Xie An nodded vigorously.

“Little girl, what about you? Xie boy saved you from bandits, and you’ve been following him ever since. Do you also want to cultivate?”

“I’ll go wherever Xie-gege goes!”

The old beggar stared into Qiao’er’s eyes and suddenly burst into loud laughter. “Good good good! This old man didn’t misjudge you two! You are naturally gifted seedlings for cultivation!”

The old beggar pulled out a command token like a magician and tossed it to Xie An.

“What is this?” Xie An’s eyes were full of bafflement.

“Take this token to the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace tomorrow. Let’s see who dares not accept you!”

Right afterward, the old beggar’s figure gradually faded.

“Wait, who exactly are you?” Xie An tried to grab the old beggar but only caught a wisp of white smoke.

“After you join the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace, you’ll naturally know who this old man is. Hahahaha.”

The old beggar vanished.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou remained silent.

How was he a beggar? He was clearly the missing Nascent Soul old ancestor from the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace. After encountering Xie An here, he had the intention of taking him as a disciple.

If they didn’t show themselves now, Xie An would become a member of the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace. The Dao-Seeking Sect couldn’t possibly stoop to competing with such a minor sect for a disciple.

Space warped, and the two stepped out. Their bright and colorful clothes were starkly out of place in the dilapidated temple.

“Who are you?!” Xie An watched Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou warily, subtly shielding Qiao’er behind him.

Lu Yang wore a smile. “Don’t panic. We are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect...”

In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remarked, “Hmm? This kid is actually a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in disguise.”

Lu Yang’s smile stiffened.

Immortal Fairy, can you say it earlier next time?

“You even saw him at the sect celebration. If I remember correctly, he’s the Wuji Venerable Lord, the Grand Elder of the Wuji Sect, an S-class sect.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Do you big shots have nothing better to do than impersonate mortals all day?

Upon learning Xie An’s true identity, Lu Yang pieced together the whole story.

Judging by the current situation, if I hadn’t intervened, Xie An would have joined the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace. The disciples there would humiliate him in various ways, perhaps even suspecting he had picked up the token from somewhere. Then, Xie An would train diligently and defeat all the disciples until they conceded, shocking everyone. Afterward, he would progress from being an outer sect disciple to an inner sect disciple.

Due to vested interests, the elders would try to frame Xie An, and the weak sect leader wouldn’t be able to protect him. At that time, the old beggar would make his appearance, accepting Xie An as his disciple in public, shocking everyone.

Next, Xie An would lead the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace to conquer the other two major sects, making it the strongest sect in Jiulong City. He might even find the secret domain hidden outside Jiulong City, acquiring a fortuitous opportunity and a new reason to grow stronger.

From then on, he would soar to great heights.

While Meng Jingzhou was still kindly asking Xie An if he wanted his bone foundation tested, Lu Yang suddenly said, “Are you the Wuji Venerable Lord?”

Meng Jingzhou froze before silently retreating backward. He knew Lu Yang wouldn’t make a mistaken judgment in matters like this.

Xie An’s face turned cold. “As expected of a disciple taught by Yun Zhi. You actually could see through this esteemed one’s true form.”

At the mention of Yun Zhi, Lu Yang suddenly recalled what Gan Tian had said. Some mighty experts who had their Dao heart shattered due to setbacks would recover their Dao heart by starting to act arrogantly and slap faces from the mortal stage.

Is this the case for Wuji Venerable Lord?

That doesn’t seem right; the timeline doesn’t match up.

Lu Yang asked gingerly, “You should have already recovered your Dao heart, right? Why are you starting over again?”

A cruel smile spread across Xie An’s face. “This esteemed one got addicted.”

1. “Meimei” means “little sister.” ☜

Chapter 696: Ice Spirit Root—Peerless Genius!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that Xie An made a lot of sense. It’s indeed easy to get addicted to this kind of thing. She had often done this with Jiang Lianyi and Ao Ling.

Lu Yang thought, I knew it, Xie An, you are suspicious. There are no beggars in Great Xia. The old beggar was in disguise, and so are you, the young beggar, really a beggar?

What kind of character test is this? It’s unclear who is testing whom.

Senior Brother Dai, what kind of lousy name list did you give us? The first person is already abnormal.

“Then we wish you a pleasant cultivation, Venerable Lord. We’ll take our leave first.” Lu Yang signaled to Meng Jingzhou with a glance. His brain had momentarily malfunctioned earlier, causing him to expose Xie An’s identity in front of Qiao’er and potentially ruining Xie An’s chance of being an old cow eating tender grass. Lu Yang felt terribly guilty.

The two backed away, leaving the dilapidated temple.

“Wait.” Xie An looked at Lu Yang with an unfriendly expression. You brat called out my true identity in front of Qiao’er. How am I supposed to interact with her in the future?

After learning that Xie An was a Transcendent Tribulation mighty cultivator, Qiao’er was dazed, clearly shocked by the revelation.

“Senior, what’s the matter?” Lu Yang smiled widely, his demeanor as respectful as it could be.

“Since you call me ‘senior,’ I can’t be stingy. How about this? I’ll suppress my cultivation to the Basic Nascent Soul Stage, and we can have a match. Let me teach you how to fight!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Senior, if you want to hit me, you can just say so; no need to go through such trouble.

“Are you fighting or not?” Xie An clearly possessed the bearing of a senior, not using his cultivation realm to bully others.

Lu Yang sighed. It looks like a flight is unavoidable. “Please grant me your guidance then, Senior.”

The two walked out of the rundown temple. They were outside the city, where pedestrians were rare; otherwise, the temple wouldn’t have fallen into disrepair.

Xie An released part of his suppression, and his cultivation realm rose gradually—Qi Training, Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Basic Nascent Soul! Using his immense power, he imitated his appearance back at the Nascent Soul Stage, even simulating the nascent soul itself. Simulating the Nascent Soul Stage was effortless for him; he had done it the last time he recovered his Dao heart.

“Lu boy, come on!” Xie An adopted a stance and exuded the airs of a senior as he allowed Lu Yang to make the first move.

Lu Yang dared not be careless. He faced the enemy with the Qingfeng Sword, drawing it smoothly like water. The sword’s sharp edge gleamed brightly, and his essence, qi, and mind unified. His ethereal sword intent put all sword cultivators under heaven to shame.

“Great swordsmanship!” Xie An’s eyes lit up. This kid’s Sword Dao ability has improved yet another notch since the battle with the Heavenly Court Creed at the sect celebration.

If I were truly at the Nascent Soul Stage, I would genuinely not have been a match for this kid.

Fortunately, I’m now a Nascent Soul cultivator with the insight of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!

Crack!

The nine-section whip lashed out, its tip striking the air and sending sparks of lightning flying. It used softness to overcome hardness like a jiao-dragon in water, its variations endless and unfathomable. A mere contact of the whip against the Qingfeng Sword deflected the blade’s edge. No matter how powerful the sword strike was, it would be useless if it didn’t land.

Lu Yang flicked his wrist, and the sword transformed into four, making it hard to distinguish which was the real Qingfeng Sword.

Sword light gathered sword qi and descended from the nine heavens, entangling with the jiao-dragon in a fierce and inextricable battle.

Then, both the Three Flavor True Fire and the Golden Bird True Flame shot forth. The temperature soared abruptly, and the air was scorched and distorted.

Xie An spat out purple lightning. The collision of lightning and fire produced a rumble as if the heavens were collapsing and the earth was cracking.

Using Draw Underground Prison, Lu Yang trapped Xie An. The latter laughed heartily, and countless water dragons erupted from beneath his feet, bursting through the prison cage.

Lu Yang used the Water-Splitting Technique to dissolve them, but the water dragons turned to vapor and dissipated into the air before they could even touch him.

He burrowed underground. The Twin Lotus Flower bloomed, giving birth to twins. The two people and two swords simultaneously attacked Xie An.

Xie An’s steps shifted as he weaved between the gaps of the two swords. At the same time, a nascent soul flew out from his brow. It held a nine-section whip and wrestled with the two Lu Yangs.

The two battled with their arsenal of moves, embroiled in a tough battle without a clear winner.

“Good kid, you can actually trade blows with me.” The corners of Xie An’s mouth curled into a cold smile. But do you think this is all I’m capable of?

Today, I’ll let you witness how terrifying a Nascent Soul cultivator with a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s insight can be!

Xie An’s feet performed the Supreme Taiji Steps, using his footwork to outline a great array. Within the array, spirit energy became restless, the earth cracked, and plants grew wildly. This array could control all plants within its range and required extremely high precision in setting up the array. It was an array that a Nascent Soul cultivator could never cast!

The frenzied plants carrying heavy clods of earth and the nascent soul holding the nine-section whip above sealed off all escape routes.

“Break!” With a muffled shout from Lu Yang, the Qingfeng Sword and the Mingyue Sword slashed simultaneously. Wood splintered explosively as the swords cleaved open a gap, but before he could charge out, it was blocked by the madly growing trees.

Lu Yang soared skyward, trying to escape, but Xie An’s nascent soul blocked him from above. There was simply no way out!

He looked enviously at Xie An’s nascent soul fighting with the nine-section whip. Why does my Unbeatable Nascent Soul only know how to hit me... Wait, maybe it can do more than just hit me.

“Senior, apologies for the offense!” Lu Yang activated a cultivation technique, severing the connection with his Unbeatable Nascent Soul and sending it into Xie An’s dantian.

Xie An laughed heartily. “If you have any more tricks, feel free to show me! Let’s see how much of Yun Zhi’s style you have... Holy crap, what is this?!”

Before Xie An finished laughing, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul darted into his dantian and started hitting anything it saw. Despite having lived for several thousand years, he had never seen anyone’s nascent soul fight like this!

Xie An hastily summoned his nascent soul back to engage the Unbeatable Nascent Soul in his dantian. However, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s every move was exquisite and peerless. Every strike hit Xie An’s pain points. Even with his insight from the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he couldn’t cope with such attacks. The pain forced him to the ground, sweat beading on his forehead like soybeans.

Suddenly, boundless power erupted from within Xie An, expelling the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

Lu Yang relinked the connection with his Unbeatable Nascent Soul and smiled. “Senior, this isn’t the combat power of the Nascent Soul Stage.”

Just now, Xie An had subconsciously used a portion of his true power to avoid the vicious beating from the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

“Alright alright, you win. If you’ve got nothing else, quickly get lost!” Xie An waved his hand irritably, admitting his defeat.

Lu Yang cupped his fists and sheathed his sword. He turned and called out, “Old Meng, let’s get ready to leave.”

“Wait a moment. This little lass has exceptionally good bone foundation.” Meng Jingzhou’s tone carried delight.

He was holding a palm-sized Bone Foundation Stone. It was of the highest quality and didn’t require contact; simply placing it near a mortal could detect their bone foundation and aptitude.

Seeing Lu Yang and Xie An locked in an intractable battle, he figured it was a good chance to test Qiao’er’s spirit roots.

He placed the Bone Foundation Stone near Qiao’er. Within the transparent stone, an ice crystal without a trace of impurity appeared.

A Variant Single Spirit Root—Ice Spirit Root!

“This little lass has an Ice Spirit Root!”

“What? There’s such a good thing?” Lu Yang was also overjoyed. This was an unexpected windfall.

“Oh, I forgot to mention earlier. That lass is also a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. You saw her at the sect celebration. She’s the Grand Elder of the Allure Sect,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded.

Lu Yang, “...”

Miss Qiao’er finally snapped out of the shock that her beloved gege was actually the Wuji Venerable Lord. An aura of extreme cold emanated from her, causing one to shudder.

“Wuji, I never imagined it was you!”

I’ve been calling him “Xie-gege” for nearly half a year, planning to secretly provide him with resources and enjoy the thrill of nurturing him before finally revealing my identity so we can marry. I never expected Xie An to be this old scoundrel, Wuji Venerable Lord!

Xie An sensed this familiar power, and he was similarly furious. “Qianjiao, it’s you, old vixen hag!”

I’ve been hoping to cultivate together with Qiao’er, brave numerous dangers, win her heart, be forced to reveal my identity at a critical moment, defeat the enemy, and fly off with her as an inseparable couple. I never expected Qiao’er to be this old vixen hag, Qianjiao Venerable Lord!

Lu Yang thought the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace truly had profound luck. To think they managed to recruit two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators as disciples. Even the Dao-Seeking Sect doesn’t have such an ability.

Chapter 697: Jiulong City’s Secret Domain

Lu Yang felt it wasn’t a bad thing for Xie An and Qiao’er to go to the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace. They would gain two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and the other sects wouldn't be harmed. A win-win solution.

Meng Jingzhou quietly retreated to Lu Yang’s side. Qiao’er, or rather, Qianjiao Venerable Lord, emitted a chilling aura that made even his bone marrow shiver in fear.

“Are Transcendent Tribulation cultivators so common now? We run into two just by going out,” Lu Yang muttered under his breath.

Meng Jingzhou seriously thought about his past outings with Lu Yang. “It seems like we encounter Transcendent Tribulation cultivators every time we go out.”

Lu Yang, “...”

It really does seem to be the case.

“Wuji, you old thing, why are you pretending to be a child?! And make yourself look so young too?!” Qiao’er berated Xie An. Had I known Xie An is Wuji Venerable Lord, why would I have stayed here for nearly half a year?

What a waste of my feelings!

Xie An refused to be outdone and spat in disdain. “You have the nerve to talk about me? Back then, you were chased by bandits, crying and pleading, ‘Gege, please save me! The bandits killed my parents and all the servants!’ You acted so convincingly!”

“Not as convincing as you! You hung around an old beggar all day, played chess with him, and went through so many convoluted steps just to get into a mere Nascent Soul-level sect!”

“You're shameless!”

“You have no sense of shame!”

The two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were locked in a heated altercation, their gazes clashing. The air seemed to solidify, and Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were fearful they would come to blows.

If a fight breaks out, the first to suffer will be the two of us.

When Lu Yang was the acting sect leader of the acting sect leader, he had read intelligence on these two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

Coming from the same generation, the two had known each other since they were young and were childhood sweethearts. There were even rumors that they were betrothed as infants. However, the Wuji Venerable Lord’s family fell into decline, and the Qianjiao Venerable Lord’s family broke off the engagement, which was why the two never married.

Regardless of the rumor’s veracity, after these two joined their respective sects, they competed with each other from the Qi Training Stage all the way to the Transcendent Tribulation, incidentally elevating their sects to S-class sects.

In their era, they were the most dazzling geniuses. Their peers of similar ages felt ashamed when witnessing their talent and couldn’t muster the will to compare with them.

No matter the era, those capable of cultivating to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage were geniuses among geniuses.

After reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the two adopted the demeanor of elders, not acting as rashly as before. Furthermore, as Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, their fights would be cataclysmic, and recovering afterward would be quite troublesome.

Nonetheless, the number of times they competed covertly wasn’t small either—for instance, by grooming disciples and having them fight or impersonating disciples to battle each other.

Realizing the situation, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stealthily prepared to leave, afraid they wouldn’t be able to get away if they lingered any longer.

“Wait a moment, don’t leave yet. There seems to be a secret domain in this temple.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stopped Lu Yang.

“Secret domain? Where?”

“Right in the temple, behind the lotus platform.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed the way to Lu Yang.

Spurred by curiosity, Lu Yang secretly moved to the area behind the lotus platform in the dilapidated temple.

The back of the lotus platform was covered in dust. Lu Yang brushed it away, revealing the secret domain’s entrance—a small indentation.

“Old Meng, come quickly. There’s a secret domain here,” Lu Yang called out to Meng Jingzhou, who was guarding the temple’s entrance.

Meng Jingzhou hurriedly walked over.

Hearing there was a secret domain here, the two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators ceased their hostilities. They were also surprised upon noticing the indentation. Both had been assiduously pretending to be mortals, yet they hadn’t noticed the secret domain entrance was so close.

“Legend says there’s a secret domain outside Jiulong City. This must be it,” Lu Yang reasoned.

“To think there really is a secret domain?” Xie An was astonished. He had even prepared a secret domain in the nearby mountains, waiting for the day he would join the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace, become the Big Senior Brother, and stumble upon the fortuitous opportunity by chance. The opportunity he had arranged was sufficient for him to cultivate until the Fusion Stage.

“Why don’t we try dripping blood?” Meng Jingzhou proposed.

“Alright.” Lu Yang dripped his blood, filling the indentation, but it showed no reaction.

Xie An analyzed carefully, “This probably requires a specific token to fill it. As for what item it is, I don’t know.”

“Why does this indentation look so familiar?” Lu Yang was puzzled. “Oh right, Senior, why don’t you try the command token the old beggar gave you?”

Xie An placed the token shaped like a purple cloud into the indentation. It fit snugly, filling exactly one-third.

“Could this need the command tokens of all three major sects? Do we have to get them from the other two sects?”

“No need for such trouble.” Qiao’er pressed her hand onto the indentation and gently pulled, tearing open a spatial rift. She pointed at the secret domain entrance and said, “We can enter now.”

Lu Yang, “...”

All four were curious about what the secret domain held and jumped directly in.

The secret domain wasn’t large. Its main structure was a luxurious palace hall.

The four walked inside, where a statue was enshrined. The statue appeared to be in disrepair, not having received offerings for years.

As if it had sensed the secret domain being opened and the presence of visitors, the statue shook slightly. A man with a white beard drifted out, regarding the four with a gratified gaze.

“I presume it was the four of you who gathered the three command tokens according to the prophecy and opened the secret domain.

“This is a wisp of divine thought I left behind. I know you have many questions, but don’t rush; listen to me explain slowly.

“I’m not sure if you have heard of my name. I am Zhang Dao, once the strongest in Jiulong City, at the Apex Divine Transfiguration Stage. Even the city lord had to pay his respects as a junior when he saw me.

“Unfortunately, although I lived a carefree life, it ultimately came down to two words: ‘lifespan.’

“The strong do not have limitless lifespans. At that time, I had no hope of reaching the Void Refinement Stage, and my end was near. I had no fear of death, but I had three disciples. They were all outstanding, yet discord grew between them. Each established their own school, founding the three major sects. When I was alive, I could still restrain them. If I died, an internal strife would inevitably occur.

“Hence, before my death, I left a prophecy: ‘Three sects united, three tokens gathered, beneath the Buddha’s gate lies Transcendent Tribulation.’ I left behind a cultivation manual that led to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.
