To obtain this cultivation technique, one must gather three tokens belonging to each of my three disciples.

“The fact that you could gather the three tokens likely means that the three of them have reconciled. This brings me great comfort. Figuring out that the prophecy’s final line pointed here demonstrates your exceptional intelligence and talent.”

The old man opened a small wooden box. Inside was a cultivation manual bound by threads.

“This is a cultivation technique I obtained from the Wuji Sect in my youth. Although it’s incomplete with only the first half, it can ensure you cultivate to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. It was through this manual that I reached the Apex Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“If you wish to obtain the subsequent parts, you must find a way to join the Wuji Sect.”

Xie An looked at the old man and clasped his hands behind his back as he asked coolly, “Do you know who I am?”

“Who are you?”

Xie An altered his appearance; his facial structure and physique reverted to his original form. He stared coldly at the old man.

“I am Xie Jiu. You may also call me the Wuji Venerable Lord.”

The old man was silent for two seconds, then quietly knelt.

“I’m sorry, I shouldn’t have stolen the cultivation manual.”

Chapter 698: The Kind-Hearted Ji Hongwen

If a talented youth joined the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace, with talent, hard work, and fortuitous opportunities, they could cultivate until the Nascent Soul Stage, unify the other two major sects, gather the three command tokens, open the secret domain, receive the ancestral teachings of the founder Zhang Dao, obtain the incomplete Divine Transfiguration cultivation manual from an S-class sect, and smoothly advance to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

With better luck, they could even join an S-class sect, complete the cultivation technique, and rise rapidly to become a Transcendent Tribulation expert.

Of course, the precondition for all this was the existence of a genuine talented youth, not an old monster like the Wuji Venerable Lord impersonating a youth.

Withdrawing his thoughts, Lu Yang silently watched the scene before him.

Zhang Dao knelt on the ground, kowtowing vigorously. “I’m sorry, I shouldn’t have stolen. Venerable Lord, you are magnanimous, please spare me!”

Never in his wildest dreams did Zhang Dao imagine that stealing a single cultivation manual would bring a prominent figure like the Wuji Venerable Lord to his doorstep after such a long time had passed.

Zhang Dao was only a little over a hundred years old. Before he began cultivating, the Wuji Venerable Lord was already a lofty Transcendent Tribulation expert, a peerless mighty figure he could never hope to reach in his lifetime.

Is there something wrong with this manual? Does it hide a secret that can tempt even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?

Zhang Dao couldn’t figure it out.

The Wuji Venerable Lord sighed softly. “Enough, get up. Your original body is already dead. What remains here is merely a wisp of divine thought. What use is punishing a divine thought with hardly any time left?”

“Many thanks, Venerable Lord!” Zhang Dao kowtowed three more times before getting up.

“However, there is one matter that requires your cooperation.”

“As long as it’s the Venerable Lord’s command, I, Zhang Dao, will brave raging fire and boiling water!”

The Wuji Venerable Lord instructed, “I will join the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace tomorrow. Later, I’ll find an opportunity to gather the three tokens and come back to look for you. At that time, pretend you don’t know me and impart that manual to me.”

Zhang Dao’s mind was full of question marks; what the Wuji Venerable Lord said was beyond his comprehension. However, he didn’t dare ask more and could only repeatedly nod his head in agreement.

“Wuji, you still want to continue this charade?” The Qianjiao Venerable Lord teased.

Hearing how the Qianjiao Venerable Lord addressed the Wuji Venerable Lord, Zhang Dao broke out in a cold sweat. Judging by her tone, this young girl is also an incredibly formidable figure.

The Wuji Venerable Lord snorted coldly. “Why not?” Having just been beaten up by Lu Yang’s Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he was struggling to accept this fact and needed to go to the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace to regain some confidence.

The four left the secret domain. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou hastily bade farewell to the two mighty experts and hurried away. Even from a distance, they could still hear the two experts conversing.

“Why are you following me?”

“To see what you old thing are up to at the Cosmos Purple Cloud Palace.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickened their footsteps. The two returned to the stable in the city to find the old horse, who looked at them sideways.

Its cultivation level was the highest in Jiulong City. While others couldn’t sense the commotion outside the city, it perceived everything clearly.

What’s wrong with you two? Weren’t you out recruiting disciples and assessing their character? Why were there auras of two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in the direction you left?

Can you two please consider the cultivation level of me, your guardian?

“Why are you looking at us like that? It was all an accident,” Meng Jingzhou said truthfully and defended themselves upon noticing the old horse’s skeptical gaze.

“Right, I can confirm what Old Meng said.” Lu Yang stepped forward as a witness.

The old horse rolled his eyes. What’s the point of you two testifying for each other?

After boarding the carriage, they swiftly left Jiulong City. Taking out the small booklet, they drew a cross next to “Xie An” on the first page.

“Let me see. The closest from here should be this person called Gu Junye from Lintian[1] City in You Province. According to the report, Junior Brother Wei Nanfei encountered him while he was on an undercover mission as a private school teacher in Lintian City. Junior Brother Wei praised him as someone who is youthful yet steady, is meticulous in thought, acts only after planning, and has excellent academic results.”

Wei Nanfei had entered the Dao-Seeking Sect in the same cohort as Lu Yang. He cultivated the Incinerating Heaven Burning Blood Art. Although his talent couldn’t be compared to Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s, he was still a top-tier genius by outside standards. He had shone brilliantly in the finals, clinching first place in the Advanced Foundation Establishment category.

Lu Yang analyzed, “In other words, this person called Gu Junye doesn’t like talking, enjoys random speculation, and isn’t fond of moving about?”

“You could say that.”

Just as the two were about to continue studying the information on Gu Junye, they felt the carriage shake slightly and come to a stop.

“Old horse, what’s the matter?” Meng Jingzhou leaned out and asked.

The old horse snorted through his nose and gestured for Meng Jingzhou to look upward.

An elegant laugh came from the sky.

“Junior Brother Meng, did Old Dai send you out too?” A young man in Confucian robes descended and greeted them after recognizing the carriage.

“Senior Brother Ji?”

It was none other than Fourth Elder’s eldest disciple, Ji Hongwen, a Basic Fusion cultivator.

Hearing the commotion outside, Lu Yang also peeked his head out.

Ji Hongwen was amused upon noticing Lu Yang. “Old Dai sent both of you out? It seems the sect truly has no one else.”

“Senior Brother Ji, what are you doing here?”

Ji Hongwen waved the booklet in his hand. “Well, Old Dai told me that staying in the mountains all day isn’t beneficial for cultivation, so he sent me out to observe the characters of the people on the name list too.”

“How many have you observed?”

“Just one; I’ve just finished observing one. He’s a good seedling. His father is a mortal, and his mother is a cultivator, but she disappeared when he was young, leaving only half a jade pendant as a clue, while he and his father depended on one another for survival. He claims he wants to work hard in cultivating and become a great cultivator in order to locate his mother through his half jade pendant.

“When he said this, his eyes flickered with an indomitable will. It’s just that his bone foundation is rather average—a Triple Spirit Root—barely meeting the sect’s entry criteria.

“Seeing this kid’s commendable filial piety, I figured I’d help him search for his mother, so I examined this jade pendant carefully. If worn long-term, the half jade pendant can improve one’s bone foundation and constitution. It also hides a cultivation manual inside, which can only be opened after the kid draws qi into his body. From this half of a jade pendant, I concluded the kid’s mother is no ordinary cultivator.

“However, that’s all I could analyze. I still couldn’t find the person. Without any other choice, I went to the Heaven Strategy Sect and asked a friend to use karmic divine abilities to trace the origin and track down the kid’s mother.”

“So you just came back from the Heaven Strategy Sect?” Lu Yang asked.

Ji Hongwen shook his head. “I learned from the Heaven Strategy Sect that the source of the jade pendant’s karma was at the Sea-Listening Sect, a first-class sect in Yu Province, so I went there directly.

“Only after arriving at the Sea-Listening Sect did I discover that the kid’s mother is the Holy Maiden of the sect. She had defied the sect’s wishes and secretly married a mortal. The Sea-Listening Sect was furious and captured her, suppressing her under the sect.”

Realization dawned upon Meng Jingzhou. “Then Senior Brother Ji, you must have decisively taken action, battled the Sea-Listening Sect Leader, and rescued the Holy Maiden, right?”

Ji Hongwen looked at Meng Jingzhou with bafflement. “No? I reported the case to the authorities. The Sea-Listening Sect restricted someone’s personal freedom, constituting the crime of illegal detention. That’s obviously a matter under the jurisdiction of the authorities.”

“Then did the family of three reunite?”

This time, Ji Hongwen nodded. “They reunited.

“After the authorities rescued the Holy Maiden, they arrested a group of members from the Sea-Listening Sect, including the Sect Leader and the Grand Elder. I reckon they’ll be imprisoned for a few hundred years.

“After investigation, it was uncovered that the half jade pendant the kid wore was a supreme treasure of the Sea-Listening Sect, which had been stolen by the Holy Maiden. Since she committed theft, I reckon she’ll also be imprisoned for a few hundred years.

“Why, I just sent that kid to visit her in prison.

“Before leaving, I told him that if he’s interested in cultivation, he can come to the Dao-Seeking Sect to take the entrance exams on the second day of the second month next year. I’m not sure whether he’ll come.”

1. The name “lintian” can be interpreted as “arriving in the sky.” ☜

Chapter 699: Curse

Lu Yang felt that the junior brother he had yet to meet might not necessarily join the Dao-Seeking Sect. Besides, even if he does join, his purpose for cultivating will be questionable.

What if he cultivates diligently to attempt a jailbreak?

Seeing Ji Hongwen immeasurably pleased with his good deed, Lu Yang was embarrassed to voice his thoughts.

When Ji Honggwen ran into their carriage and greeted them, flaunting his good deed to a couple of acquaintances was also one of his motives.

“What about you two? Did you just leave the sect, or have you also finished observing someone?”

Lu Yang wasn’t sure how to explain the earlier events, so he could only steel himself and say, “We’ve finished observing one person. However, he’s already preselected by the Wuji Sect and probably won’t join our sect.

“We also incidentally found a good seedling not on the name list. She has an Ice Spirit Root, but she’s also been preselected by another sect.”

“Which sect?” Ji Hongwen asked.

“The Allure Sect.”

Ji Hongwen felt slightly regretful. “That is really unfortunate then.”

I trust these two junior brothers’ judgment. Anyone they find promising, though I can’t be sure about their character, their cultivation talent is undoubtedly the cream of the crop.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded in unison. Unfortunate indeed.

“Alright then, I’m off to observe the second person. See you back at the sect.” Ji Hongwen waved his hand and soared into the air, headed for his next destination.

“See you, Senior Brother Ji.”

The carriage began moving slowly. The old horse traversed space at incredible speed; only a Fusion expert like Ji Hongwen could notice the carriage’s whereabouts.

~~~

Lintian City in You Province was a rather unremarkable small city. The highest cultivation level within the city was only at the Nascent Soul Stage.

As usual, Meng Jingzhou left the old horse in the stable and took out his meticulously prepared fodder. The old horse ate leisurely, swishing its tail.

Gu Junye attended classes at the White Dew Academy in the city and was easy to find.

“The sages say, 'To study and practice regularly, is that not a form of joy...” The teacher lectured on the platform, swaying his head.

Gu Junye sat in a corner, exuding an aura that kept others at a distance. His smooth, fair complexion revealed sharply defined contours and coldly handsome features. His long eyebrows were like willow leaves, his eyes were somber, and his stature resembled a jade tree. The fitting Confucian robe accentuated his slender build.

Lintian City had a relatively open ethos; even women could receive an education.

Despite Gu Junye’s unapproachable countenance, many young women still secretly cast flirtatious glances his way, ignoring the teacher’s lecture and frequently looking at Gu Junye.

“Young Master Gu is so handsome.”

“It’s a pity Young Master Gu wasn’t born to the legitimate wife. As a concubine-born son, he can’t inherit the Gu Family’s property.”

“Not inheriting is perfect—he can marry into my family.”

“Get real. How many sisters in the city think the same? How could it be your turn?”

“I heard he hides some secrets. Some have seen him talking to himself often.”

The young women whispered among themselves, stealing glances at Gu Junye with their cheeks flushing and hearts racing.

Gu Junye acted as if he didn’t hear their chatter, concentrating on the lecture and taking notes. His handwriting was like his upright posture—neat, tidy, and strict.

After school, a young woman secretly called Gu Junye to a corner behind the academy and boldly confessed her feelings.

“Junye, I like you.”

Gu Junye stared at the woman coldly. Even he himself had lost count of how many people had confessed to him.

The nearer the young woman got to Gu Junye, the more excited she became, and her heart pounded so quickly it nearly leaped out.

“Apologies, I need to study. Also, please don’t call me Junye. Our relationship isn’t that close.”

Gu Junye rejected her mercilessly. I, a Transcendent Tribulation mighty expert, withstood eighty tribulation lightning in the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation, only one step away from ascending to an immortal. Alas, my cultivation wasn’t complete, and I failed to overcome the tribulation, perishing in the immortal tribulation and somehow ending up in this later era.

In this life, I will definitely cultivate anew and become a supreme true immortal!

As a Transcendent Tribulation mighty expert, how can I accept the love and affections of a mere mortal?

The young woman covered her face and fled.

Gu Junye simply found it boring. He returned to the academy, packed his things, and prepared to go home.

Just as he was about to leave, he heard a commotion.

“Mu Yu, you actually pushed Junior Sister Mu Xi on purpose!”

“I...I didn’t.”

“You didn’t? Don’t tell me Junior Sister Mu Xi fell by herself!”

“No, that’s not what I meant.”

“Then what did you mean?! You were the only one behind Junior Sister Muxi just now. If it weren’t you, who else could it be?!”

“Making things hard for Junior Sister Mu Xi all the time isn’t enough for you? This time, you’ve gone so far as to make a move on her!”

“Everyone, please don’t blame my elder sister. I believe she didn’t do it on purpose.”

“Junior Sister Mu Xi, you’re just too kind-hearted. This is why Mu Yu always bullies you.”

“Junior Sister Mu Xi, we’re all here. Don’t be afraid.”

A delicate young woman sat on a chair, her clothes slightly disheveled. She was likely Mu Xi, the one who fell.

Gu Junye knew Mu Xi. She was from the Mu Family, but concubine-born like him. She had a frail appearance that easily evoked a protective instinct from others. The male students in the academy often showed concern for her.

Another young woman, Mu Yu, was anxiously defending herself.

Mu Yu was Mu Xi’s elder sister. Gu Junye had heard that Mu Yu often bullied Mu Xi by leveraging her status as the elder sister.

“Please move aside. You’re blocking the way,” Gu Junye said flatly with a commanding tone, slightly displeased.

Reincarnated alongside him was an immortal-level demon beast sealed within his eyes—the Heaven-Swallowing Beast. If he was in a bad mood, he might lose focus and allow the Heaven-Swallowing Beast to escape and wreak havoc in the mortal world.

Seeing it was Gu Junye, everyone quickly cleared a path for him.

“Junior Sister Mu Xi.” Gu Junye also followed the others in calling her Junior Sister Mu Xi.

“Senior Brother Junye...” Mu Xi met Gu Junye’s gaze, her pretty face slightly blushing.

“You’re also blocking the way.”

“Ah? Oh.” Only then did Mu Xi realize the chair she was sitting on was placed right in the middle of the path. She hurriedly got up and moved it.

Gu Junye nodded in satisfaction and left.

All this time, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had been hiding nearby and observing everything. They inhaled sharply.

Setting aside the matter of Mu Xi deliberately falling and then shifting the blame to Mu Yu...

“Immortal Fairy, this time, tell me clearly first. Is this Gu Junye a reincarnation of a mighty expert, a reforged cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew, or a mighty expert in disguise?” Learning from the lesson last time, Lu Yang first did his due diligence by verifying with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand boredly. “You’re overthinking it. How could there be so many mighty experts? He’s just a mortal.”

“Really?”

“Since when has this immortal ever been mistaken?”

“That’s good then.” Lu Yang still trusted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s discernment.

“However, there is indeed a problem with this kid.”

“What problem?” Lu Yang grew tense.

“He’s been cursed.”

“Cursed?”

“A rather simple little curse. The effect is that any young woman in his surroundings who sees him will develop heart problems.”

Lu Yang nudged Meng Jingzhou, who was grinding his teeth beside him.

“No need to be jealous of this kid. The women around him blush and feel their hearts race because they have heart problems.”

Chapter 700: The Mindset of the Strong

Meng Jingzhou was gnashing his teeth when he heard Lu Yang’s words. He calmed down, straightening his tidy collar.

“Nonsense. Who’s jealous of this kid? I’m just concerned that his excessive romantic peach blossom luck could easily turn into romantic peach blossom tribulation.”

Lu Yang nodded, pretending to believe Meng Jingzhou’s nonsense.

“But you said he’s cursed? What’s going on?”

Meng Jingzhou had once suffered from a curse backlash and traveled far to Wilderness Province to seek a solution. He knew how troublesome it was to deal with curses.

Lu Yang turned and tossed the question to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Immortal Fairy, care to elaborate?”

“It’s a rather simple minor curse. It doesn’t even work on cultivators. It merely causes the young women around him to experience accelerated heartbeats. Over time, this will lead to heart conditions.

“Right now, it’s not a big issue, as it hasn’t reached the stage of causing illness yet. But given time, problems will definitely arise.”

“Can we find out who cast it?”

“Not sure.”

“Is there a way to break the curse?”

“That’s easy. I remember your identity jade tablet contains Xirang Soil, Wood Essence, and Thousand-Illusion Bamboo... As long as these ingredients are refined into a pill according to proper ratios, the curse can be lifted.”

It was unlike the curse backlash Meng Jingzhou encountered last time. That was too high-level and something the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t proficient in, so she could only think of the Play-Dead Technique. It was different this time. This was a beginner-level minor curse. She had encountered it multiple times in the ancient era and could handle it with ease.

“Refining it into a pill... looks like we need to find a pill-concocting master.” Neither Lu Yang nor Meng Jingzhou knew how to concoct pills.

As long as the curse was removed, the caster would notice the anomaly and naturally surface.

The two tailed Gu Junye back home. The Gu Family was a locally renowned Golden Core clan. He was the family head’s second son and had his own independent courtyard.

Returning to his courtyard, he completed the academy’s assigned homework as usual. By then, it was already night.

He stood in the courtyard with his arms spread wide and slowly closed his eyes, bathing in the moonlight.

After a long while, he opened his eyes and looked up at the bright argent moon in the sky. His eyes flickered with reminiscence, as if he was remembering someone from the distant past.

He withdrew his gaze and sighed softly. “To think even the power of moonlight is so sparse now. The day my cultivation is restored seems so far away. I wonder when all my cultivation will recover. Could this be the Age of Declining Dharma,[1] where everything is in decline and headed toward destruction?

“How I miss the days when I roamed freely between heaven and earth. I wonder if the world still remembers the name of this esteemed one—the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. I fear it has been lost to time.

“The ancients are gone; the past cannot be pursued.”

He felt a sharp pain in his right eye and covered it, grimacing. “Fellow Daoist Heaven-Swallowing, I’m afraid you’re the only one in this world who still remembers this esteemed one.”

“Young Master, dinner is ready,” the steward announced respectfully from the door.

Gu Junye ceased his nostalgic thoughts. “To think that this esteemed one can’t even achieve fasting now. If the Xuanyuan[2] Sword Master and the Unbreakable Saint were to learn of this, they would surely laugh until their teeth drop out.”

“There’s your favorite ginseng old duck soup,” the steward added.

“Got it. I’ll go over now.”

~~~

After eating dinner with his family, Gu Junye returned to his room. He took out a brush, ink, paper, and inkstone, then pinched his sleeve and ground the ink, beginning to paint.

He concentrated on the tip of the brush, holding his breath. Two hours later, a painting titled The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord Attains the Dao appeared on the paper. In the blank spaces, he wrote about his previous life’s experiences.

He stepped onto the path of cultivation at sixteen, established his foundation at seventeen, condensed his golden core at eighteen, and formed his nascent soul at nineteen, breaking the record for the fastest cultivation speed and becoming the youngest Nascent Soul cultivator. Countless Nascent Soul old monsters were wary of him and addressed him as a fellow Daoist.

Gu Junye set down the brush and looked at the painting with satisfaction. In his previous lifetime, he had been known as the “Painting Sage.” Although he had lost most of his power and skill, painting something like this was still not difficult for him.

He tidied up the Four Treasures of the Study and went to sleep peacefully.

~~~

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou hid on the roof, awkwardly looking around. They really didn’t want to continue surveilling Gu Junye.

“Old Lu, you stay here and watch this kid. I’m going out for a stroll.”

Lu Yang grabbed Meng Jingzhou, who was about to flee. “Don’t dream of running! Did you forget the oath we swore when we became sworn brothers? We should share blessings and hardship alike, for better or for worse!”

Meng Jingzhou retorted furiously, “Bullshit! When did I ever become your sworn brother?!”

“I think this kid is very suited for cultivation,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared arbitrarily after observing for a long while.

“Why?” Lu Yang was bemused.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others often used to talk like this. They said it was the mindset of the strong and told me to learn it too. Although I didn’t really understand their thinking, I believed there must be some merit to it. Who knows, it might actually aid in cultivation.”

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

In the early morning, Gu Junye washed his face and freshened up before running to the academy.

“The Great Era is approaching. Although I haven’t reached the age for cultivation yet, I can prepare in advance. Running strengthens the body and builds physical fitness.”

Gu Junye assumed a posture, his eyes cold and determined, and quickly ran toward the academy.

He loved running in the early morning best. The streets were sparse with people, and he wouldn’t have to worry about colliding with pedestrians while running.

As he ran around a corner of the street, a figure suddenly dashed out.

It was the pitiful-looking Mu Xi.

It was well-known that Gu Junye had the habit of running to the academy. Mu Xi had been waiting here early to bump into him!

Success!

Mu Xi watched Gu Junye get increasingly closer, unable to stop his footsteps. Delight surged through her heart. She pretended to be frightened and screamed, not knowing where to put her hands. That way, it would be convenient for Gu Junye to catch her with a hug.

Soon, Mu Xi couldn’t laugh anymore. Gu Junye directly sent her flying two meters away. She fell to the ground, utterly disoriented.

“Junior Sister Mu Xi, are you alright?” Gu Junye looked at Mu Xi vigilantly. Through his observation as the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, he discerned that the girl before him seemed to possess a Charming Immortal Physique and would certainly bring calamity upon the nation in the future. I must not have too much contact with her.

“I’m...I’m fine.” Mu Xi felt that when Gu Junye had hit her, it was like being struck by a carriage. Even now, she was still dizzy.

Although she will bring calamity upon the nation in the future, I’m the one who knocked her over after all. Gu Junye kindly helped Mu Xi up.

“Thank you, Senior Brother Junye.”

Gu Junye’s brows were knitted as he corrected her. “Men and women are different and should keep a distance. There is hardly any relationship between us; you cannot address me so intimately.

“Moreover, your academic performance is too poor. My mother taught me since childhood not to associate with those who have poor academic results.”

Mu Xi, “...”

Out of guilt, Gu Junye accompanied Mu Xi to the academy. When the male students at the academy saw Mu Xi’s slightly flushed face, they felt jealous.

The female students felt the same.

However, some students felt they were a perfect match made in heaven.

Mu Xi secretly glanced up to observe Gu Junye’s reaction.

Gu Junye noticed Mu Xi looking at him and frowned inwardly. Could Mu Xi have detected the Heaven-Swallowing Beast sealed within my eyes?

The teacher came onto the platform with a metal ruler and textbooks, beginning the day’s lessons.

The academy advocated not just rigid studying but also physical fitness. After two hours of lecture, the students were made to run laps around the academy.

After the run, Mu Xi’s expression changed.

“Junior Sister Mu Xi, what’s wrong?”

“The jade bracelet my father gave me is missing! I had it tucked in my book while I was running just now, but I can’t find it now!”

“What? What should we do?”

Her classmates became somewhat panicked. Everyone knew Mu Xi had a bracelet that was quite valuable.

“Search! It must be hidden in this room!”

“That’s right, it must be here!”

It was unclear who had proposed it, but other classmates concurred.

Soon, the jade bracelet was found.

“Mu Yu, it was indeed you who stole it!”

1. You could read up more here if you’re interested. ☜

2. Xuanyuan is the name of the Yellow Emperor. ☜

Chapter 701: Very Much In Line With Senior Brother Dai’s Standards

Everyone’s gaze turned toward Mu Yu’s wrist at the same time and spotted a green jade bracelet identical to the one Mu Xi had described.

“Mu Yu, what do you have to say for yourself this time?!”

“No, that’s not it. Back then, our father gave one jade bracelet each to me and my younger sister Mu Xi. This bracelet is mine,” Mu Yu explained frantically.

“Mu Xi’s jade bracelet is missing, and now it’s with you. You say it’s yours, but do you have proof?”

Mu Yu couldn’t defend herself even if she had a hundred mouths. How on earth do I explain this?

“Quickly return the bracelet to Junior Sister Mu Xi!”

“Elder Sister, if you wanted this jade bracelet to make a pair, you could have just told me. Why be like this?”

“I can prove who the jade bracelet belongs to.” Gu Junye suddenly spoke up.

Everyone looked at Gu Junye, not understanding why he was suddenly siding with Mu Yu.

But when did Gu Junye ever care about others’ opinions? In a cool tone, he elaborated, “This morning, I accidentally knocked Junior Sister Mu Xi two meters away. Under those circumstances, her jade bracelet definitely wouldn’t have remained intact.

“Look at the jade bracelet on Mu Yu’s wrist. It doesn’t have a single flaw. Clearly, it hadn’t bumped into something before.”

The classmate who first noticed Mu Yu had the bracelet was displeased. “What if the jade bracelet is of high quality and couldn’t be damaged by the impact?”

Gu Junye replied unhurriedly, “There’s a second method then. Do you know why the authorities often have criminals sign confessions?

“Everyone, look at the inner side of your fingers. Do you see circular patterns? These are called fingerprints. Everyone’s fingerprints are unique. Whenever you touch something with your hands, your fingerprints are naturally left behind.

“However, our naked eyes can’t discern them. I suggest reporting it to the authorities and requesting a cultivator to examine it with their Dharma Eye. We’ll find out the answer then.”

“Fine, let’s report it to the authorities then!”

Soon, the authorities sent a constable with cultivation to inspect Mu Yu’s jade bracelet.

“Strange, why are there no fingerprints on it?” The constable frowned.

Mu Xi laughed inwardly. It’s useless even if you bring a cultivator over.

Someone from her family worked for the authorities. Under their influence, she learned about the existence of fingerprints. Both she and Mu Yu had the habit of bathing every night. Any fingerprints would have been washed off in the warm water long ago. There won’t be a single fingerprint.

“The absence of fingerprints indicates that this is Mu Yu’s bracelet,” Gu Junye said insipidly, looking at both Mu Yu and Mu Xi. “This morning, when I knocked down Junior Sister Mu Xi and helped her up, I touched her jade bracelet. My fingerprints should be on that bracelet.

“Constable big brother, you came at the perfect time. You can scour this room to find out where the jade bracelet actually is.”

“Ah! I found the bracelet,” Mu Xi suddenly exclaimed, offering an apologetic smile to everyone. “It was pressed right at the bottom of my books.”

“Junior Sister Mu Xi, you’re too careless.”

“Exactly, you had us so worried.” Everyone breathed a sigh of relief, signaling to Mu Xi that she shouldn’t take this matter to heart.

“Wait, this matter isn't over yet. You all searched someone arbitrarily and falsely accused Mu Yu just now. You should apologize to her,” Gu Junye said with furrowed brows.

“Gu Junye, I advise you not to go overboard!” the classmate who first noticed Mu Yu’s bracelet rebuked angrily. “There are so many people here. Do you want all of them to apologize to Mu Yu?”

“Not everyone. Him, her, her, her...” Gu Junye pointed out several individuals. “These people didn’t speak earlier; they don’t need to apologize.”

“You!”

Gu Junye continued, “And Junior Sister Mu Xi, although you didn’t falsely accuse Mu Yu, your carelessness caused constable big brother to make a trip here for nothing and wasted everyone’s time. You need to apologize to constable big brother and everyone.”

“Junye is right,” the teacher said. He tapped the metal ruler rhythmically against his palm, producing an intimidating sound.

Left with no choice, everyone succumbed to the pressure and apologized one by one.

After the matter concluded, Mu Xi privately approached Gu Junye and whispered, “Junye, actually, things don’t have to be so strained between us.”

Gu Junye didn’t respond. I have already stated that our relationship isn’t this close. Who is Junye? In any case, it’s not me.

“Junye, my father thinks we’re very well-suited. He intends to propose a marriage to your family and finalize our engagement tonight.”

Only then did Gu Junye react, looking up at Mu Xi.

As the reincarnation of an almighty Transcendent Tribulation expert, how can I lose my primordial yang here? How will I cultivate in the future?

He remained silent, continuing to read his book with his head lowered, as if indifferent to this matter.

Seeing this, Mu Xi stood for a moment longer before leaving.

In truth, she had privately told her father that she wanted to marry Gu Junye. It doesn’t matter that he doesn’t have feelings for me now. Once the engagement is set, which provides a reason for us to interact, he will gradually come to like me.

After school, just as Mu Xi had said, the Mu Family arrived at the Gu residence with betrothal gifts to propose marriage.

Family Head Gu, also Gu Junye’s father, had already discussed and agreed to the marriage during the day. Now, it was merely a formality.

Both the Gu and Mu families were Golden Core ancestral clans. Be it family background or appearance, Gu Junye and Mu Xi were a perfect match.

“No, I do not agree to this marriage,” Gu Junye announced publicly in front of everyone, openly opposing the decision of both families.

“Impudence! You have no right to speak here?!” His father flew into a rage, feeling his pride hurt. He had never paid much attention to this second son of his.

“This engagement involves me, so why wouldn’t I have the right to speak?” Gu Junye ignored his father’s ire. As the almighty Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s reincarnation, I didn’t even bow to the Ninety-Nine Immortal Ascension Tribulation. Who have I ever feared?

“Marriage is decided by the parents’ orders and the matchmaker’s words. There’s no place for you to act willfully and make a scene!

“You knocked into Mu Xi this morning! Men and women must maintain proper boundaries. How will Mu Xi be able to marry in the future if you act this way?!”

Gu Junye countered, “We’re both ancestral cultivation clans. Once we embark on the path of cultivation, some physical contact between men and women is normal. Don’t tell me we still need to distinguish between men and women during future battles?”

I have no idea how many female diabolic cultivators I’d slain in my previous life. Does that mean I have to marry all of them?

“Sophistry!” Gu Junye’s father couldn’t win the argument and could only accuse him of sophistry.

Mu Xi also looked at Gu Junye, her eyes glistening with tears. “Junye, do you hate me so much?”

With so many people present, Family Head Gu found it hard to save face. Mu Xi’s father stepped in to smooth things over. “It’s fine, it’s fine. It’s just a child throwing a tantrum. Once they enter the nuptial chamber, everything will be alright.”

“I will not enter any nuptial chamber.”

“It’s not up to you! I’ll drag you to the nuptial chamber if I have to!”

Hearing this, Gu Junye said nothing, simply nodding. He walked to the door and invited several constables who had been waiting outside for some time to enter.

“Constable big brothers, see what I was saying? This is a case of violent interference with another’s freedom of marriage. They intend to forcibly send me into the nuptial chamber.”

After learning about the engagement, he had gone to report the case after school before returning home.

~~~

Observing from the shadows, Meng Jingzhou turned to Lu Yang and gave Gu Junye a high appraisal. “Abides by the law, honest in conduct, sticks to his duties, steady and diligent in cultivation—very much in line with Senior Brother Dai’s standards. This must be someone Senior Brother Dai is looking for.”

Lu Yang also nodded. “He’s a good seedling for joining our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Chapter 702: Deity Temple

Under the pressure from the constables, the two family heads were forced to annul the marriage engagement they had just set.

Gu Junye did not choose to escalate the matter. The offense of violent interference with another’s freedom of marriage would not be prosecuted unless a complaint was filed; with the involved party withdrawing the accusation, the matter was dropped.

After the constables left, Gu Junye’s brows were tightly furrowed as he pondered a question.

If my father gets imprisoned for violent interference with another’s freedom of marriage, will it affect my chances at the imperial examinations?

“It seems my grasp of the law is still not proficient enough.” Gu Junye reflected on himself. He decided to forgo absorbing moonlight power tonight in favor of continuing his legal studies.

Although he was the reincarnation of an ancient mighty expert, that was extremely long ago. The current environment differed from that of ancient times; the only proper path was to adapt in advance.

This was why he paid close attention in class and studied diligently afterward, resulting in his academic results far surpassing his peers. The teacher even praised him as a potential bangyan who would score the second highest in the imperial examinations.

“Why don’t you go find a pill-concocter who can concoct a pill to lift the curse?” Lu Yang suggested to Meng Jingzhou.

Through their observation, they concluded that Gu Junye was precisely the person Dai Bufan was looking for, so there was no need to continue assessing his character.

Of course, the main reason was that observing this kid felt too awkward; even Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s thick skins couldn’t withstand it.

“Alright.” Meng Jingzhou took the pill formula that Lu Yang had written down based on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s dictation.

Finding a pill-concocter was easy; the Luodi Merchant Guild offered pill-concocting services. Even if the merchant guild’s pill-concocter wasn’t the best in the city, they were still among the top five and more than capable to refine this kind of beginner-level pill.

“Xi’er, let’s go,” Mu Xi’s father said.

Mu Xi never imagined Gu Junye could be so heartless. To think that he had called the constables just to avoid marrying me!

“Junye, you will regret this! Your fate profile is flawed, and only I can mend it! Apart from me, anyone else you like will be harmed because of you!”

Gu Junye remained unmoved. He did not believe in the concept of fate profile. If I had believed in fate and predestination, I wouldn’t have defied the heavens and attained the Dao to become an immortal in my previous life.

Cultivation is about defying the heavens!

“My fate is mine to command, not Heaven’s.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy instructed Lu Yang, “You mustn’t think like that. The Heaven Mandate Immortal is particularly fierce when striking down people like that.”

Lu Yang nodded repeatedly. The Heaven Mandate Immortal claimed to be born in accordance with the mandate of Heaven. If you suddenly declare “my fate is mine to command, not Heaven’s,’ isn’t that directly opposing him?

Even if one has such thoughts, they shouldn’t voice them aloud.

~~~

After Meng Jingzhou revealed his identity at the Luodi Merchant Guild, the person in charge promptly attended to Eldest Young Master Meng personally with utmost cordiality. Upon hearing that Eldest Young Master Meng needed a pill refined, he immediately summoned the merchant guild’s top pill-concocting master.

Logically, any pill-concocting apprentice with ten years of experience could refine the pill Meng Jingzhou needed, but that wouldn’t display the importance they placed on Meng Jingzhou.

Even without his status as the Meng Family’s eldest young master, being a Nascent Soul disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect alone would warrant the same treatment. This was someone equivalent to a Divine Transfiguration cultivator, while the strongest in the city was only at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“By the way, the pill needs to be soluble in water, colorless, and odorless,” Meng Jingzhou reminded. He planned to administer the pill to Gu Junye secretly.

“Uh, Young Master Meng, a friendly reminder: poisoning is a crime.” The merchant guild manager was unaware of the pill’s effect and kindly reminded Meng Jingzhou.

Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened. “I know.”

Soon, a gray pill was presented on a tray.

Meng Jingzhou was slightly disappointed. If someone from the Pill Cauldron Peak had refined it, it should have had at least one pill mark.

But I can’t be too picky. Where am I supposed to find a senior brother from the Pill Cauldron Peak? It’s fine as long as this can lift the curse.

Meng Jingzhou accepted the pill and went to the Gu residence to reconvene with Lu Yang.

~~~

“How’s the observation going?”

“My shoes are almost worn out from me picking at them.”

Meng Jingzhou took out the pill. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy glanced at it and confirmed it was the type of pill she described. Only then did Meng Jingzhou feel reassured enough to dissolve the pill in the old duck soup for the Gu Family’s dinner.

Gu Junye finished the old duck soup and wiped his mouth, but showed no abnormalities.

“No reaction?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “What reaction were you hoping for? Although the curse is placed on him, the curse’s effect is on those around him. After the curse is removed, this kid will naturally not feel anything.”

“Come on, let’s go check the Mu residence,” Lu Yang called out to Meng Jingzhou. Mu Xi’s reaction after the annulment of the engagement had been very abnormal.

The two made their way to the Mu residence under the cover of darkness and spied on Mu Xi’s boudoir.

In the boudoir, Mu Xi gritted her teeth as she clutched a red paper doll. Its back was written with Gu Junye’s birth bazi information.[1]

“Gu Junye, you will regret this!”

The red paper doll was a treasure she had obtained from the Deity Temple outside the city. It could cause anyone who stayed near Gu Junye for a long time to develop heart problems.

This way, Gu Junye will have no choice but to marry me!

Suddenly, the paper doll spontaneously combusted and burned her fingers, causing her to shriek in pain.

Not only did her hand hurt, but her heart also ached terribly!

“Ah!

“Why did the paper doll burn?”

To maintain the paper doll’s potency, she had to drip a drop of blood onto it daily, gradually dyeing the white paper doll red.

This was actually a method for refining a life-bound magical treasure. Now that her life-bound magical treasure was destroyed, she suffered a backlash, and the heart pain was one of the symptoms.

“To the Deity temple!”

Instantly sensing something was wrong, she fled to the Deity Temple outside the city in a panic.

“Follow her!” Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message to Meng Jingzhou.

They had been in Lintian City for less than two days and hadn’t heard of any Deity Temple. No one knew when the temple was built; it had appeared overnight. Its location was hidden, and hardly anyone knew of it.

Mu Xi had learned of it by chance from a classmate, who said praying at the Deity Temple before exams could lead to good results.

~~~

The Deity Temple had no incense acolyte and received no incense offerings. It housed only a clay statue of an old man with a benign face. The interior was neat and clean, as if the place was protected by some deity.

“Deity, my paper doll burned!”

A voice reverberated within the temple. “Someone has broken the curse. You suffered from the backlash.

“And the one who broke it has already secretly followed you here.”

Lu Yang was startled. We’ve been discovered!

The other party’s cultivation is higher than mine and Old Meng’s!

An overwhelmingly powerful force surged toward Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Lu Yang hastily drew his Qingfeng Sword to block it, while Meng Jingzhou roared, bulging his muscles to withstand the blow with his body.

The disparity in cultivation realm was too vast. The two were directly swept out of the temple and slammed into a tree outside!

The colossal clay statue seemed to have come alive. Opening its eyes, it stepped down from the altar and leaned on the temple’s doorframe with one hand before bending and walking out of the temple.

The three-meter-tall clay statue stared at the two coldly.

“Immortal Fairy, what is this?”

“This is a method using faith and worship. His true body can no longer be used for some unknown reason, leaving only his soul. To obtain a physical body, he built this temple here, granting followers’ wishes to gain their faith!”

“This is a method from the Great Qian era,” Lu Yang said through clenched teeth. If the Great Yu Dynasty’s characteristic was the “Imperial Preceptor system,” then the Great Qian Dynasty’s characteristic was “Deity Dao” and “faith.”

“What about his cultivation realm?”

“Fusion Stage.”

The clay statue looked at the two icily, a human-like sneer curling its lips.

“Two reckless juniors who don’t know their place. Judging by your appearance, you must be prodigies from some major sect. I originally had no intention to bring about slaughter, but you just had to discover my existence. In that case, I cannot let you live!”

The oppressive aura of the Fusion Stage enveloped them, rendering them immobile.

Suddenly, a neighing sound came from the sky, resembling the legendary roar of a dragon.

A pure white horse without a single stray hair arrived, treading on the air. It kicked the clay statue over with one hoof, its eyes arrogant and domineering!

A few dragon scales on the white horse’s forehead emitted a faint glow in the darkness.

After the clay statue was sent tumbling, it stared fixedly at the white horse.

“Great Demon King!”

Why would a Great Demon King of the Dragon-Horse Tribe appear here?

1. The birth bazi, or just bazi, are eight characters that are often used for fortune-telling. The “ba” means eight, and “zi” means character/word. It states information such as the year, month, day, hour, heavenly stem, and earthly branch. There are 10 heavenly stems and 12 earthly branches. ☜
